Here ïs tha femlie line o Jesus Christ, tha sinn o Davit an o Abraham: Abraham wus tha faither o Isaac, Isaac tha faither o Jacob, Jacob tha faither o Judah an hïs brithers.  An Judah wus tha faither o Perez an Zerah, an thair mither wus Tamar. Perez wus tha faither o Hezron, Hezron tha faither o Ram.  Ram wus tha faither o Amminadab, Amminadab tha faither o Nahshon, an Nahshon tha faither o Salmon.  Salmon wus tha faither o Boaz, an tha mither o Boaz wus Rahab. Boaz wus tha faither o Obed, an tha mither o Obed wus Ruth. Obed wus tha faither o Jesse,  an Jesse tha faither o Kïng Davit. Davit wus tha faither o Solomon, bi hir that wus yinst tha wife o Uriah.  Solomon wus tha faither o Rehoboam, Rehoboam tha faither o Abijah, Abijah tha faither o Asa,  Asa tha faither o Jehoshaphat, Jehoshaphat tha faither o Jehoram, Jehoram tha faither o Uzziah.  Uzziah wus tha faither o Jotham, Jotham tha faither o Ahaz, Ahaz tha faither o Hezekiah.  Hezekiah wus tha faither o Manasseh, Manasseh tha faither o Amon, an Amon tha faither o Josiah.  Josiah wus tha faither o Jeconiah an hïs brithers. That wus roon aboot tha time the' wur cairriet aff tae Babylon. An eftèr the' wur cairriet awa tae Babylon, Jeconiah becum tha faither o Shealtiel, an Shealtiel tha faither o Zerubbabel.  Zerubbabel wus tha faither o Abiud, Abiud tha faither o Eliakim, an Eliakim tha faither o Azor.  Azor wus tha faither o Zadok, Zadok tha faither o Akim, an Akim tha faither o Eliud.  Eliud wus tha faither o Eleazar, Eleazar tha faither o Matthan, an Matthan tha faither o Jacob.  An Jacob wus tha faither o Joseph, an Joseph wus merriet tae Mary. An Mary wus tha mither o Jesus, tha Yin caad Christ. That made fowerteen genèrations ïn aa frae Abraham tae Davit, fowerteen frae Davit til the' wur cairriet awa tae Babylon, an anither fowerteen frae that tae tha cumin o Christ. An thïs ïs hoo tha birth o Jesus Christ cum aboot: hïs mither Mary wus promist tae Joseph, but afore the' cum thegither, she fun oot she wus wi a wean. An ït wus bi tha Halie Spïrit.  Noo Joseph hir husban wus a dacent man an he dïdnae want hir tae be affrontit, sae he thocht tae senn hir awa on tha quait.  He wus thïnkin aboot aa thïs, whan lo an behoul, an angel o tha Loard appeart tae hïm ïn a draim an saed, “Joseph, sinn o Davit, dïnnae be feart tae tak Mary fer yer wife, fer tha wean she's cairryin ïs o tha Halie Spïrit.  She wull hae a sinn, an ye ir tae gie hïm tha name Jesus, fer he wull save hïs ain fowk  frae thair wrangdaeins.”  Noo aa thïs wus daen tae brïng aboot whut tha Loard haed saed throu tha proaphit: “A virgin wull cairrie a wean, a sinn, an whan he's boarn, he'll be caad Immanuel” - mainin “God ïs wi iz.” Whaniver Joseph waakent up, he daen whut tha angel o tha Loard haed toul hïm tae dae, an he tuk Mary hame fer tae be hïs wife.  But he dïdnae sleep wi hir til eftèr tha wean wus boarn. An he caad hïm bi tha name Jesus. Eftèr Jesus wus boarn ïn Bethlehem ïn Judea, durin tha time that Herod wus Kïng, spaemen frae tha East cum tae Jerusalem  an the' axt, “Whar ïs tha yin that haes bin boarn Kïng o tha Jews? Fer we hae saen hïs starn ïn tha East an hae cum fer tae woarship hïm.”  Whaniver Kïng Herod heerd thïs, he wus baadlie püt aboot, an aa Jerusalem wi hïm.  Sae he brocht thegither aa tha Jewish fowk's heid preeshts an maistèrs o tha Laa, an he axt thaim whar tha Christ wus tae be boarn.  “In Bethlehem o Judea,” the' saed, “fer thïs ïs whut tha proaphit writ:  ‘But you, Bethlehem, ïn tha lan o Judah, ye ir bi nae mains tha laist amang tha rulers o Judah; fer oot o you wull cum a ruler that wull herd ma fowk Israel.’ ” Then Herod caad tha wise men thegither on tha quait, an he fun oot frae thaim whan ït wus that tha starn haed cum ïntae sicht.  He sent thaim tae Bethlehem an he toul thaim, “Luk ïn iverie airt fer tha wean. As shuin as yis fin hïm, wud ye brïng me wurd, sae as A can gae an woarship hïm as weel!”  Eftèr the' haed heerd whut tha kïng haed tae say, the' set aff on thair wye, an lo an behoul, tha starn the' haed saen ïn tha East went aheid o thaim, til ït stapt richt ower tha place whar tha wean wus.  Whaniver the' saa tha starn, the' wur hairt gled.  The' cum ïntae tha hoose, the' saen tha wee wean wi hïs mither Mary, an the' bood doon an wurshipt hïm. Then the' apent thair kïsts an the' set afore hïm thair gifts o gowld an frankincense an myrrh.  An bein warnt ïn a draim no tae gae bak tae Herod, the' tuk anither róad bak hame. An eftèr the' went awa, an angel o tha Loard appeart tae Joseph ïn a draim. “Git up,” he toul hïm, “tak aff tae Egypt wi tha wean an hïs mither. Bide thair til A gie ye tha wurd, fer Herod ïs aboot tae hunt oot tha wean fer tae dae awa wi hïm.”  Sae up Joseph got, he tuk tha wean an hïs mither wi hïm ïn tha mïddle o tha nicht, an he set aff fer Egypt.  He stapt thair til Herod deed. An aa thïs brocht aboot whut tha Loard haed saed throu tha proaphit: “Oot o Egypt A hae caad ma sinn.” Whaniver Herod fun oot he'd bin haad, he wus rïppin, an he gien oardèrs fer tae kïll aa tha weechils ïn Bethlehem an roon aboot, thaim at wus twa yeir oul an unnèr, takkin ïntae accoont tha time he haed bin telt bi tha spaemen.  Then whut tha proaphit Jeremiah saed aforehan wud happen cum aboot:  “A voice wus heerd ïn Ramah, greetin an lamentin. It wus Rachel greetin fer hir weans; an she niver devalved, acause hir weans wus nae lang'r wi hir.” But whaniver Herod deed, lo an behoul, an angel o tha Loard appeart ïn a draim tae Joseph ïn Egypt  an he saed, “Git up, tak tha wean an hïs mither awa tae tha lan o Israel, fer tha yins that wus gaun tae kïll tha wean ïs deid.”  Sae Joseph upt an tuk tha wean an hïs mither an he went ïntae tha lan o Israel.  But whan he heerd that Archelaus wus tha Kïng o Judea ïn tha ruim o hïs faither Herod, he wus feart tae gae thair. Bein warnt ïn a draim, he pued bak tae tha dïstrict o Galilee,  an he went an settelt doon ïn a toon caad Nazareth. An sae ït cum tae pass whut wus saed bi tha proaphits: “He wull be caad a Nazarene.” In thaim days Jhone tha Baptiser cum praichin ïn tha wiles o Judea  an sayin, “Turn awa frae yer sïns, fer tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs nearhan.”  Jhone ïs tha yin tha proaphit Isaiah spauk aboot, tellin: “Thair's a voice cryin oot ïn tha wiles, ‘Mak tha wye readie fer tha Loard, mak hïs pads strecht fer hïm!’ ”  Jhone's claes wus made o kemel's hair, an he haed a leather belt roon hïs mïddle. An he leeved bi aitin gresshoppers an wile honey.  Croods gaed oot tae hïm frae Jerusalem alang wi aa tha fowk frae Judea an tha hale dïstrict o tha rïver Joardan.  An thaim at confesst thair sïns wur baptised bi hïm ïn tha Joardan rïver. But whan he saa a wheen o Pharisees an Sadducees cumin tae whar he wus baptisin, he saed tae thaim, “Ye sleekit shooer o vipers! Wha telt ye tae rin frae tha wrath o God that's cumin?  Ye maun show bi tha wye ye leeve that ye hae turnt awa frae yer sïns.  An dïnnae be thïnkin tae yersels, ‘We hae Abraham fer oor faither’ an hae daen wi that. A tell ye that oot o thon stanes God can mak weans fer Abraham.  God's hatchit ïs noo at tha ruit o tha trees, an thaim that dïnnae gie guid fruit wull be fellt, an pïtcht ïntae tha fire. A'm baptisin yis wi wattèr fer tae show yis hae repentit. But thair's yin cumin eftèr me that ïs michtier ner me. A'm no fït tae cairrie hïs buits. He wull baptise ye wi tha Halie Spïrit an wi fire.  Hïs winnowin fork ïs ïn hïs han, an he wull redd up hïs thrashin-flure, getherin hïs wheat ïntae hïs barn an burnin tha caff wi a fire ye cannae pit oot.” Then Jesus cum frae Galilee tae tha Joardan fer tae be baptised bi Jhone.  But Jhone tried tae pit hïm aff, sayin, “It's me that needs tae be baptised bi you, an you ir cumin tae me?”  Jesus saed, “Jist dae thïs fer noo; fer thïs ïs tha richt thïng fer iz tae dae, tae cairrie oot tha wull o God.” Sae Jhone gien ïn.  Tha mïnit Jesus wus baptised, he ris up oot o tha wattèr, an jist wi that tha heivens apent, an he saa tha Spïrit o God cumin doon laik a doo an lichtin on hïm.  An a voice cum frae heiven sayin, “Thïs ïs ma Sinn, ma hairt's delicht; A'm weel plaised wi hïm.” Then Jesus wus taen bi tha Spïrit ïntae tha wuldèrness fer tae be tempit bi tha Deil.  Eftèr gaun wioot mait fer fowertie days an fowertie nichts, he wus gye hung'rie.  Tha tempter cum tae hïm an saed, “If ye ir tha Sinn o God, tell thaim thair stanes tae turn ïntae breid.”  Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “It ïs writ: ‘Man cannae leeve bi breid alane, but bi iverie wurd at cums frae tha mooth o God.’ ”  Then tha Deil tuk hïm tae tha halie cïtie an stud hïm up on tha verie tap o tha Hoose o God.  “If ye ir tha Sinn o God,” saed he, “throw yersel doon! Fer tha Guid Buik says: ‘He wull tell hïs angels tae luk eftèr ye, an wi thair hans the' wull haud ye up, fer fear ye dunt yer fit agin a stane.’ ”  Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “It's ïn tha Buik forbye: ‘Ye ir no tae temp tha Loard yer God.’ ”  An nixt thïng, tha Deil tuk hïm tae a bïg heich muntin an lut hïm see aa tha kïngdoms o tha warl ïn aa thair glorie.  “A wull gie ye aa thïs,” he saed, “ïf ye'll jist boo doon an woarship me.”  Jesus saed tae hïm, “Awa or that, Satan! Fer ït ïs writ doon: ‘Ye ir tae woarship tha Loard yer God an tae sarve naebodie but hïm.’ ”  Then tha Deil lut hïm be, an angels cum an lukt eftèr hïm. Noo whan Jesus heerd tha wittins that Jhone haed bin püt ïn jail, he went bak ïntae Galilee.  An eftèr leain Nazareth, he gaed tae Capernaum an he stapt thair. Capernaum wus bi tha Loch ïn tha dïstrict o Zebulun an Naphtali --  tae brïng aboot whut wus foretoul bi tha proaphit Isaiah: “In tha lan o Zebulun an tha lan o Naphtali, on tha wye tae tha Loch, on tha ither side o tha Joardan, ïn Galilee whar tha Gentiles leeve - tha fowk that sut ïn tha dairk hae saa a bricht licht; an on tha yins leevin ïn tha lan o tha shedda o deith, tha licht haes cum ïn.” Frae then on Jesus begun tae praich, “Turn awa frae yer sïns, fer tha Kïngdom o Heiven haes cum nearhan ye.” Yin day, whan Jesus wus waakin alang tha loch shore o Galilee, he saa twa brithers, Simon caad Petèr an hïs brither Andra. The' wur castin a neyt ïntae tha wattèr, fer the' wrocht at tha fïshin.  “Cum an follae me,” Jesus saed, “an A wull mak ye fïshers o men.”  An richt awa the' layed doon thair neyts an the' follaed eftèr hïm.  He gan on frae thair, an saen twa ither brithers, Jeames tha sinn o Zebedee an hïs brither Jhone. The' wur ïn a bóat wi thair faither Zebedee, mennin thair neyts. Jesus caad thaim,  an richt awa the' left tha bóat an thair faither, an the' follaed hïm. Jesus trevelt aa roon Galilee, taichin ïn thair Meetin Hooses, an praichin tha Guid Wittins o tha Kïngdom, an curin iverie disaise an ailment amang tha fowk.  Wurd aboot hïm spreed aa ower Syria, an the' brocht tae hïm aa tha seeck fowk wi aa kines o disaises: thaim that wus tormentit, or bothert wi ïll spïrits, or tuk fïts, or fowk that wus paralysed, an he made thaim bettèr.  Bïg croods follaed hïm frae Galilee, an tha Ten Toons, an Jerusalem, an Judea an tha dïstrict on tha ither side o tha rïver Joardan. Noo whaniver he saa tha croods, he gaed up tha muntin an sut doon. Hïs follaers gethert roon hïm,  an he stairtit tae taich thaim, sayin, “Blisst ir tha puir ïn spïrit, fer thairs ïs tha Kïngdom o Heiven. Blisst ir tha yins that greet, fer the' wull be comfortit. Blisst ir tha yins that ir gentle, fer the' wull inherit tha irth. Blisst ir tha yins that hae a hung'r an a druith fer whut's richt, fer the' wull get thair fïll. Blisst ir tha yins that ir merciefu, fer the' wull be showed mercie. Blisst ir tha pure ïn hairt, fer the' wull see God. Blisst ir tha yins that warks fer peace, fer the' wull be caad sinns o God. Blisst ir tha yins that's traitit ïll fer daein whut's richt, fer thairs ïs tha Kïngdom o Heiven. Blisst ir you whan fowks baadmooth ye, an trait ye ïll, an miscaa ye on accoont o me.  Be joyfu an gled, acause yis hae a pooerfu reward waitin fer ye ïn heiven, fer the' ïll-traitit tha proaphits that wus thair afore ye ïn jist tha same wye. Yous ir tha saut o tha irth. But ïf tha saut loasses ïts taste, hoo can ït git bak ïts tang? It ïs nae lang'r onie use, but fer tae be throwed oot an thrampt unnèr fit. Yous ir tha licht o tha warl. A toon bigged on a hïll cannae be hïd.  Ye dïnnae licht a lamp an pit ït unnèr a boul. Na, ye pit ït on a stan, whar ït gies licht tae tha hale hoose.  In tha same wye, let yer licht shine afore iveriebodie, sae as the' wull see yer guid warks an gie glorie tae yer Faither ïn heiven. Dïnnae be thïnkin that A hae cum fer tae dae awa wi tha Laa or tha Proaphits; A hinnae cum fer tae dae awa wi thaim, but fer tae fülfill thaim.  A tell ye tha truith, afore heiven an irth passes awa, no tha weeest lettèr, ner even tha weeest stroke o a pen, wull pass awa frae tha Laa afore iveriethin God wants fer ït ïs brocht aboot.  Oniebodie that breks yin o these commauns, even tha laist o thaim, an lairns ithers tae dae tha same, wull be laist thocht o ïn tha Kïngdom o Heiven, but whaiver keeps these commauns an lairns ithers tae dae thaim, wull be gye weel thocht o ïn tha Kïngdom o Heiven.  Fer A'm tellin yis thïs: less yer guidness gaes beyont that o tha Pharisees an tha maistèrs o tha Laa, yis'll no git ïntae tha Kïngdom o Heiven, that's fer shair! Yis hae heerd that ït wus saed tae fowk lang syne, ‘Dïnnae commït murdèr, an oniebodie that murdèrs wull be judged fer ït.’  But A'm tellin ye, oniebodie that's even ang'rie wi hïs brither [wioot onie caas] ïs gaun tae be judged fer ït. Agane, oniebodie that says tae hïs brither, ‘Ye eejit ye!’ - that bodie wull hae tha Heich Cooncil tae answer tae. An oniebodie that says, ‘Ye oul fool!’ wull be rinnin tha risk o hell fire.  Sae, ïf ye ir brïngin yer offerin tae tha althar, an ye mine that yer brither haes ocht agin ye,  jist lea ït doon fornent tha althar. Awa an mak ït up wi yer brither furst; then cum bak an gie yer offerin ïn.  Soart thïngs oot quïck wi yer enemie that ïs takkin ye tae coort. Dae ït while ye ir still wi hïm on tha wye thair, or he'll mebbe han ye ower tae tha judge, an tha judge cud han ye ower tae tha offysher, an ye cud be cloddit ïntae jail.  A tell ye tha truith, ye'll no git oot o thair afore yer last pennie's pyed! Yis hae heerd that ït wus saed, ‘Dïnnae commït adultèrie.’  But A'm tellin yis that oniebodie that even luks at a wumman wi lust haes aareadie commïtit adultèrie wi hir ïn hïs hairt.  If yer richt ee maks ye dae wrang, hoke ït oot an clod ït awa. It's faur bettèr fer ye tae loass tha yin pairt o yer bodie ner fer yer hale bodie tae be throwed ïntae hell.  An ïf yer richt han maks ye dae wrang, cut ït aff an clod ït awa. It's faur bettèr fer ye tae loass tha yin pairt o yer bodie ner fer yer hale bodie tae gang ïntae hell. It's bin saed ïn tha Scrïptures as weel: ‘Oniebodie that divorces hïs guidwife maun gie hir a notysh o divorce.’  But A'm tellin ye that oniebodie that pits awa hïs wife - fer ocht ither ner rinnin aff wi anither man - he maks hir an adultèress; an oniebodie that merries a divorced wumman commïts adultèrie as weel. Forbye, ye ken that ït wus saed tae tha fowk lang syne, ‘Dïnnae brek yer oath, but keep tha oaths ye hae made tae tha Loard.’  A'm tellin ye but, dïnnae sweer ava: ether bi heiven, fer ït ïs God's throne;  or bi tha irth, fer ït ïs hïs fit-creepie; or bi Jerusalem, fer ït ïs tha cïtie o tha michtie Kïng.  An dïnnae sweer bi yer heid, fer ye cannae mak even yin o yer hairs white or blek.  Jist let yer ‘Ay’ be ‘Ay’, an yer ‘Na’, ‘Na’; oniethin mair ner thïs cums frae tha wïckit yin. Yis hae heerd that ït wus saed, ‘An ee fer an ee, an a tuith fer a tuith.’  But A tell ye, Dïnnae fecht agin a wïckit bodie! If summodie hïts ye on tha richt cheek, turn tha ither side til hïm forbye.  An ïf summodie wants tae sue ye an tak tha shirt aff yer bak, let hïm hae yer tap-cóat as weel.  If summodie gars ye tae gang yin mile, gang twa mile wi hïm.  Gie tae tha yin that axes ye fer ocht, an dïnnae turn yer bak on a bodie that's lukkin tha lenn o sumthin. Yis hae heerd that ït wus saed, ‘Love yer nighber an hait yer enemie.’  But A tell ye: Love yer enemies an pray fer thaim that traits ye ïll,  that ye micht be childèr o yer Faither ïn heiven. He maks hïs sin tae rise on tha wïckit as weel as on tha guid, an he senns rain on thaim that daes whut's richt, as weel as on tha yins that daesnae.  If ye jist love thaim at loves you, whut reward wull ye get? Shair even tha tex men daes that!  An ïf ye onlie pass tha time o day wi yer ain yins, whut ir ye daein mair ner ithers? Even pagans daes tha same, dae the' no?  But you maun be perfait, jist as yer heivenlie Faither ïs perfait.” “Dïnnae mak a show afore fowk o onie guid yis dae, fer yer Faither ïn heiven wull gie yis nae reward fer that. Sae, whan ye gie ocht tae tha needie, dïnnae soon tha trumpet, tha wye tha hippycrates daes ïn tha Meetin Hooses an on tha streets, fer tae be weel thocht o. A tell ye tha truith, the' hae got aa tha reward the'ir gaun tae get.  But whan ye gie ocht tae tha needie, dïnnae let yer left han ken whut yer richt han ïs daein,  sae that yer giein micht be on tha quait. Then yer Faither, that sees whut ïs daen on tha quait, wull reward ye. An whan yis pray, dïnnae be laik tha hippycrates, fer the' love tae stan an pray ïn tha Meetin Hooses an on tha street coarners fer aa tae see. A tell ye tha truith, the' hae got aa the'ir gaun tae get.  But whan you pray, gang awa ïntae a ruim alane, shut tha dure an pray tae yer Faither ïn saicret. Then yer Faither at sees whut ïs daen ïn saicret, wull reward ye. An whan ye pray, dïnnae keep rhymin on an on laik pagans, fer they thïnk tha mair the' taak, tha bettèr the' wull be heerd.  Dïnnae be laik thaim, fer yer Faither kens whut ye hae need o afore ye ax hïm.  Sae thïs ïs hoo ye shud pray: ‘Oor Faither that bides Abain, Halie be yer name. Micht yer Kïngdom cum shuin, An yer wull be daen on irth Jist tha wye ït ïs Abain. Gie iz theday eneuch breid tae dae iz. An forgie iz oor debts, jist as we hae forgien tha yins that's ïn debt tae us. An dïnnae róad iz ïntae temptation, but save iz frae tha wïckit yin, [fer yours ïs tha Kïngdom, tha pooer an tha glorie, fer iver an iver, Amen.]’ Fer ïf you forgie fowk whan the' dae wrang agin ye, then yer heivenlie Faither wull forgie you as weel.  But ïf ye dïnnae forgie fowk thair wrangdaeins, yer Faither wull no forgie you tha wrangs yous hae daen. Whan ye fast, dïnnae luk doon In tha mooth as tha hippycrates dae, fer the' mak thair faces luk mïserable jist tae let fowk see the'r fastin. A tell ye tha truith, thïs ïs aa tha reward the'r gaun tae get.  But whan ye fast, pit oiyle on yer heid an waash yer face,  sae fowk wull no notysh that ye ir fastin; yer Faither but, wha ye cannae see, wull notysh; an tha Yin that sees whut ïs daen ïn hidlins, he wull gie ye yer reward. Dïnnae hoord up fer yersels treysures on irth, whar moths an roost desthroy, an whar thiefs brek ïn an steal.  But hoord up fer yersels treysures ïn heiven, whar nether moth ner roost can desthroy, ner thiefs brek ïn an steal.  Fer whut ye thïnk tha maist o, wull aye be ïn yer hairt. Yer ee ïs tha lamp o tha bodie. If yer ee ïs guid, yer hale bodie ïs fu o licht.  But ïf yer ee ïs baad, yer hale bodie ïs fu o dairkness. If then tha licht wi'ïn ye ïs dairkness, ït maun be pïtch blek! Naebodie can sarve twa maistèrs, fer ether he'll hait tha yin an love tha ither, or he'll stïck bye tha yin an thïnk naethin o tha ither. Ye cannae sarve baith God an Gowld. Sae A'm tellin ye, tak nae thocht fer yer life, whut ye'll ait or whut ye'll drïnk; ner yit aboot yer bodie, whut claes ye'll pit on ye. Is life no mair impoartin ner mait, an tha bodie mair impoartin ner claes?  Luk at tha burds o tha air; the' dïnnae sow ner reap ner hoord awa ïn barns, an yit yer heivenlie Faither feeds thaim. Ir yous no warth faur mair ner thaim?  Ye cannae add a sing'l oor tae yer life bi worryin aboot ït.  An why dae ye worrie aboot tha claes ye pit on ye? Luk hoo tha lïlies o tha fiel growe. They nether wark ner spïn!  Yit A'll tell ye thïs, e'en Solomon cudnae match thaim, wi aa hïs fancie claes!  An ïf that ïs tha wye God pits claes on tha gress o tha fiel, that's here theday an throwed ïntae tha fire themorra, dae you dooters no unnèrstan that he'll luk eftèr you anaa?  Sae dïnnae fash yersels bi sayin, ‘Whut wull we ait?’ or ‘Whut wull we drïnk?’ or ‘Whut wull we pit on iz?’  Fer thaim at daesnae know God rin eftèr aa these thïngs, but yer heivenlie Faither kens aa ye hae need o.  Seek oot hïs Kïngdom an hïs righteousness furst o aa, an aa these ither thïngs wull tak care o thairsels. Sae dïnnae fash yersels aboot themorra, fer themorra wull luk eftèr ïtsel. Iverie day haes eneuch bother o ïts ain.” “Dïnnae judge ithers, sae as ye'll no be judged yersels.  Fer ïn tha same wye yis judge ithers, yis'll be judged that wye yersels; an tha misure yis gie wull be tha misure yis get.  An why dae ye see tha skelf ïn yer brither's ee, but ye dïnnae see tha plenk ïn yer ain ee?  Hoo can ye say tae yer brither, ‘Let me tak tha skelf oot o yer ee,’ whan luk, aa tha time thair ïs a plenk ïn yer ain ee?  Ye oul hippycrate ye, pu tha plenk oot o yer ain ee furst, an then ye'll be able tae see proper, tae tak tha skelf oot o yer brither's ee! Dïnnae gie whut's halie tae tha doags; an dïnnae scattèr yer pearls afore pïgs. If ye dae, the' may thramp thaim unnèr thair feet, an then turn an teer ye tae bïts. Keep on axin, an ït wull be gien tae ye, keep on lukkin an ye'll fin whut ye'r eftèr, keep on rappin an tha dure wull be apent tae ye.  Fer iveriebodie that axes wull get; hïm that keeps on lukkin wull fin whut he's eftèr; an tae hïm that keeps on rappin, tha dure wull be apent.  Whutch faither amang ye, ïf hïs sinn axes hïm fer breid, wull gie hïm a stane?  Or ïf he axes hïm fer a fïsh, wull he gie hïm a snake?  An sae ïf sïnfu fowk laik yersels know hoo tae gie guid thïngs tae yer weans, hoo much mair wull yer Faither ïn heiven gie guid thïngs tae thaim that axes hïm! Sae ïn iveriethin, dae tae ithers whut yis wud want thaim tae dae tae yersels, fer thïs ïs whut tha Laa an tha Proaphits ïs aa aboot. Gae ïn bi tha nerra gate. Fer wide ïs tha gate an braid ïs tha róad that leads tae destruction, an monies a yin gaes that wye.  But nerra ïs tha gate an reuch tha rodden that leads tae life, an thair's no monie that fins ït. Watch oot fer fauss proaphits. The' cum tae ye lukkin laik hairmless sheep, but on tha inside the'r naethin but a paak o wolfs.  Ye'll ken thaim bi thair fruit, ay, bi whut the' dae. Daes fowk gether grapes frae a thoarn büsh, or fïgs frae thrïstles? Na.  In tha same wye iverie guid tree gies guid fruit, but a baad tree gies ye baad fruit.  A guid tree cannae gie baad fruit, an a baad tree cannae gie ye guid fruit.  Iverie tree that daesnae gie guid fruit ïs cut doon an throwed ïntae tha fire.  It's laik that wi tha fauss proaphits tae. Ye'll ken thaim bi whut the' dae. It's no iverie yin that says tae me, ‘Loard, Loard,’ that'll git ïntae tha Kïngdom o Heiven, but ït's onlie hïm that daes tha wull o ma Faither wha ïs ïn heiven.  Monies a yin'll say tae me on tha Day o Reckonin, ‘Loard, Loard, dïd we no proaphesy ïn yer name, an ïn yer name dïd we no drive oot ïll spïrits an dae a hale lock o mïracles?’  Then A wull tell thaim strecht, ‘A niver knowed ye. Awa frae me, ye wrangdaers!’ Sae iverie yin that hears these wurds o mine an heeds thaim ïs laik a wise man that bigged hïs hoose on a roak.  Tha rain cum doon, tha wattèr ris, an tha wuns got up an hut agin tha hoose; yit ït dïdnae faa, acause ït wus bigged on tha roak.  But iverie yin that hears these wurds o mine an daesnae heed thaim ïs laik a gormless man that bigged hïs hoose on san.  Tha rain cum doon, tha wattèr ris, an tha wuns blattèrt an bate agin thon hoose o hïs. Tha hoose faad doon, an whut a cresh thair wus!”  Whan Jesus haed daen sayin these thïngs, tha croods wur aa thunnèrstruck wi hïs taichin,  fer he taicht thaim laik a bodie wi thortie, an no laik thair maistèrs o tha Laa. Whaniver Jesus cum doon frae tha braeside, bïg croods follaed hïm.  An here cum up thïs man wi leprosie, an he got doon on hïs knees afore hïm an saed, “Loard, ïf ye hae a mine tae, ye can mak me clain.”  An Jesus püt hïs han oot an toucht tha man. “A'm wullin,” he saed. “Be clain!” An richt awa he wus cured o hïs leprosie.  Then Jesus saed tae hïm, “Luk here, mine ye dïnnae tell oniebodie. But gang awa an show yersel tae tha preesht. Gie an offerin fer yer cleansin as Moses toul iz ïn tha Laa, fer a wutness tae yin an aa that ye'r weel agane!” Whan Jesus wus gaun ïntae Capernaum, a centurion cum tae hïm, plaidin wi hïm,  an sayin, “Loard, ma sarvin man ïs lyin on hïs bed at hame. He's no weel, an cannae move ava. He's sufferin sumthin tarrible!”  Jesus saed tae hïm, “Weel, A'm cumin tae mak hïm bettèr.”  Tha centurion saed, “Loard, tha laiks o me's no fït tae hae ye cum unnèr ma ruif. But jist say tha wurd, an ma sarvin man wull be bettèr agane.  Fer A ken hoo tae tak oardèrs, an A hae sodgers unnèr me as weel. A tell yin tae gang an he gangs, an anither yin tae cum, an he cums. A tell ma sarvin man tae dae thïs or that, an he daes ït!”  Whan Jesus heerd thïs, he wus stoondit an saed tae thaim that follaed hïm, “A tell ye tha truith, A niver fun oniebodie wi sitch faith ïn aa Israel!  A say tae ye that monie fowk wull cum frae tha East an tha Wast, an the' wull tak thair place roon tha boord wi Abraham, Isaac an Jacob ïn tha Kïngdom o Heiven.  But monie o tha yins tha Kïngdom wus got readie fer, the' wull be cast oot ïntae tha dairk, whar thair wull be greetin an scringein o teeth.”  Then Jesus saed tae tha centurion, “Gae! It wull be daen fer ye tha wye ye believed ït wud.” An hïs sarvint got bettèr agane that verie mïnit. Noo whaniver Jesus cum ïntae Petèr's hoose, he saen Petèr's mither-ïn-laa lyin ïn bed wi a faivir.  He toucht hir han an tha faivir left hir, an she got up an stairtit tae sarve an luk eftèr hïm.  An that evenin, the' brocht tae hïm a hale lock o fowk that wur bothert wi ïll spïrits, an he driv oot tha spïrits wi a wurd an cured aa that wus seeck.  Thïs wus fer tae brïng aboot whut wus spauk throu tha proaphit Isaiah: “He tuk oor ailments on hissel, an he cairriet oor disaises.” Noo whan Jesus saa tha thrang gethert roon hïm, he toul hïs follaers tae gang ower tae tha ither side o tha loch.  Then thair wus thïs maistèr o tha Laa cum up an saed, “Maistèr, A wull follae ye nae mettèr whar ye'r gaun!”  An Jesus saed tae hïm, “Foxes hae holes an burds hae nests, but tha Sinn o Man haes naewhar he can caa hame.”  Anither o hïs follaers saed tae hïm, “Loard, let me gang an burie ma faither furst.”  But Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “Follae me, an let tha deid burie thair ain deid.” Then he got ïntae tha bóat, hïs follaers got ïn eftèr hïm, an awa the' went.  Wi'oot onie warnin, a wile stoarm cum up on tha loch, an tha waves waasht ower tha bóat. But Jesus slep throu ït.  Hïs follaers cum an waakent hïm, sayin, “Loard, save iz, or we'll aa be droont!”  “Hoo cum yis ir sae feart?” saed he. “Hae yis nae faith ava?” Then he stud up an chackt tha wun an tha waves, an ït wus aa peace an quaitness.  Tha men wur dumfoonèrt an axt, “Whut kine o a man ïs thïs? Tha verie wun an tha waves daes hïs bïddin!” An whan he got tae tha ither side o tha loch, tae tha lan whar tha Gadarenes leeved, thair wus these twa men cum oot frae tha graveyaird fer tae meet hïm. The' wur bothert wi ïll spïrits, an that reuch, naebodie cud get bye thaim.  “Whut ïs ït ye ir eftèr wi us, Sinn o God?” the' guldèrt. “Hae ye cum here tae torment iz afore tha day o Reckonin?”  A bït awa frae thaim, a bïg herd o pïgs wus hokin fer food.  An tha ïll spïrits plaidit wi Jesus, “Gin ye ir gaun tae drive iz oot, jist senn iz ïntae tha herd o pïgs thonner.”  He saed tae thaim, “Awa wi ye!” Sae the' cum oot o tha men, an gaed ïntae tha pïgs, an aa tha herd tuk aff doon tha hïll, heid furst ïntae tha loch, an tha hale lock o thaim deed ïn tha wattèr.  Tha yins lukkin eftèr tha pïgs run aff; the' gaed ïntae tha toon an toul iveriebodie aa that haed tuk place, an whut haed happent tae tha men bothert wi ïll spïrits.  Then tha hale toon gaed oot tae meet Jesus. An whan the' saen hïm, the' plaidit wi hïm tae lea thair pairt o tha kintrie. Jesus climmed ïntae a bóat, sailed ower tha ither side an cum tae hïs ain toon.  The' brocht a paralysed man tae hïm, lyin on a bed. An whaniver Jesus saa tha faith the' haed, he saed tae tha paralysed man, “Tak hairt, sinn; yer sïns ïs aa forgien.”  At thïs, some o tha maistèrs o tha Laa saed amang thairsels, “That's naethin but blesphemie!”  Knowin whut the' wur thïnkin, Jesus saed, “Hoo cum yis hae sitch wïckit thochts ïn yer hairt?  Is ït aisier tae say, ‘Yer sïns ïs forgien ye,’ or tae say, ‘Get up an waak’?  But jist sae as ye'll ken tha Sinn o Man haes tha pooer tae forgie sïns here on irth...” - he then saed tae tha paralysed man - “Up ye get, lïft yer bed an gae hame.”  An tha man stud up, sae he dïd, an he went awa hame.  Whan tha thrang saen thïs, the' wur fïllt wi wunnèrment; an the' gien glorie tae God fer giein sitchana thortie tae a man. Whan Jesus wus trevelin on frae thair, he saa a tex man bi tha name o Mattha sïttin ïn hïs hut. “Follae me,” he toul hïm, an Mattha ris up an follaed hïm. A while latèr, whan Jesus wus at a dennèr at Mattha's hoose, thair wus a hale lock o tex men an ither fowk o ïll repute aitin alang wi hïm an hïs follaers.  Whaniver tha Pharisees saen thïs, the' axt hïs follaers, “Whut's yer maistèr daein aitin wi thaim tex men an sïnners?”  On hearin thïs, Jesus saed, “It ïs no thaim that's weel needs a doctèr, but thaim that's seeck.  But awa an lairn tha mainin o thïs Scrïpture: ‘It's mercie A'm eftèr, A'm no eftèr secryfice.’ Fer A hinnae cum fer tae caa tha guid fowk [tae repent], A hae cum fer tae caa sïnners.” An ït wus then that Jhone's follaers cum up an axt hïm, “Hoo ïs ït that tha Pharisees an us ir aye fastin, but your follaers dïnnae fast?”  Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “Dae ye thïnk tha waddin guests wud murn while tha bridegruim ïs still wi thaim? Thair'll cum a day but, whaniver tha bridegruim wull be tuk awa frae thaim; an ït's then the'll be fastin.  Naebodie patches thair oul duds wi a bït o new claith, fer tha patch'll pu awa an mak ït waur.  Nether wud the' poor new wine ïntae oul wineskïns. Fer ïf the' dae, tha skïns wull brust, tha wine wull rin oot an tha wineskïns wull be ruint. Na, the' poor new wine ïntae new wineskïns, an tha baith o thaim wull keep.” Noo whaniver he wus sayin thïs, a heidyin o tha Meetin Hoose cum an got doon on hïs knees afore hïm an saed, “Ma wee dochtèr haes deed jist thair noo. But cum an pit yer han on hir, an she'll cum bak tae life.”  An Jesus got up an gaed wi hïm, as weel as hïs follaers.  An lo an behoul, thair wus thïs wumman that wus bothert wi bleedin fer twal yeir. She cum up behin hïm an toucht tha enn o hïs cloke.  Fer saed she til hirsel, “If A can jist touch hïs cloke, A wull be made weel agane.”  Jesus turnt roon an saen hir. “Tak hairt, dochtèr dear,” he saed, “Yer faith haes made ye weel.” An tha wumman wus hailt that verie mïnit.  Noo whan Jesus cum tae tha hame o tha heidyin o tha Meetin Hoose, he saa tha funèral flutèrs an aa tha hale thrang foofin an greetin, an he saed,  “Awa er that! Tha wee lass ïs no deid, she's jist sleepin.” But the' begun tae lach at hïm.  Eftèr tha crood wus püt oot tha dure, Jesus gaed ïn an tuk tha wee lass bi tha han, an she ris tae hir feet.  An thïs wus aa tha taak o that hale kintrieside. As Jesus gaed on frae thair, twa blin men follaed hïm, caain oot, “Sinn o Davit, tak peetie on iz!”  Whaniver he went ïntae hïs hoose, tha blin men cum ïn tae, an he axt thaim, “Dae yis believe A hae tha pooer fer tae dae whut ye'r wantin?” “Ay, Loard,” the' saed, “we dae.”  Then he toucht thair een an saed, “It'll be daen tae ye, accoardin tae yer faith.”  An thair sicht cum bak, an the' cud see! Jesus gien thaim a guid warnin an saed, “Luk here, dïnnae you be tellin oniebodie aboot thïs.”  But nae shuiner wur the' oot, than the' stairtit tae spreed tha news aboot hïm aa roon tha hale kintrie. An eftèr the' left, a man that wus bothert wi ïll spïrits an cudnae spake wus brocht tae Jesus.  An Jesus driv oot tha ïll spïrit, sae tha man that wus dum cud noo spake. Tha crood o fowk wus dumfoonèrt an saed, “We niver saen tha laiks o thïs ïn Israel afore!”  But tha Pharisees saed, “It's tha Deil, tha heidyin o tha ïll spïrits that gies hïm tha pooer tae cast oot ïll spïrits!” An Jesus trevelt throu aa tha toons an vïllages, taichin ïn thair Meetin Hooses, praichin tha Guid News o tha Kïngdom, an hailin iverie kine o disaise an ailment.  Whaniver he saen tha croods, hïs hairt went oot tae thaim, acause the' wur aa laik sheep wi nae shepherd: troublet, on thair lane, wi nae róad tae turn.  Then he saed tae hïs follaers, “Thair's a gran hairst waitin, but thair's no monie warkers tae gether ït ïn.  Sae keep on axin tha Loard o tha hairst tae senn oot mair warkers ïntae hïs hairvest fiel.” He caad hïs twal follaers thegither an he gien thaim tha pooer tae drive oot ïll spïrits an tae cure aa kines o disaises an ailments.  Tha names o tha twal possels wus: furst, Simon (caad Petèr) an hïs brither Andra; then Jeames tha sinn o Zebedee, an hïs brither Jhone;  Phïlip an Bartholomew; Tammas an Mattha tha tex man; Jeames tha sinn o Alphaeus, an Thaddaeus;  Simon tha Zealot an Judas Iscariot, tha yin that bethrayed Jesus. An Jesus sent oot tha twal o thaim an gien thaim thair oardèrs: “Dïnnae be gaun amang tha Gentiles or ïntae onie toon o tha Samaritans.  But rether gae tae tha loast sheep o Israel.  An as ye ir gaun alang, praich thïs: ‘Tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs nearhan.’  Heal seeck fowk, rise tha deid, cleanse thaim wi leprosie, drive oot ïll spïrits. Ye hae freelie received, sae ye maun gie freelie.  Dïnnae tak alang onie gowld or siller, ner e'en a copper ïn yer girthpooch;  tak nae baag fer tha róad, ner spare claes, ner shune ner a stav; fer tha warker ïs warth hïs keep.  Whutiver toon or vïllage ye gae ïntae, luk fer some warthie dacent bodie thair an stap ower at hïs hoose til ye tak yer lave o tha place.  As ye gae ïntae thïs hame or that, bïd thaim tha time o day.  If tha hame ïs warthie, let yer blissin be on ït; ïf ït ïsnae warthie, let yer blissin cum bak tae ye.  If the' dïnnae mak yis walcum or gie yis a hearin, dicht tha stour aff yer feet whan ye lea that hame or toon.  A tell ye tha truith, tha fowk o Sodom an Gomorrah wull be bettèr aff on tha Day o Reckonin ner that toon. A'm sennin yis oot laik sheep amang wolfs. Sae be as cannie as sarpents an as hairmless as doos.  Be on yer gaird agin men; the'll han yis ower tae tha cooncils an gie yis a guid whuppin ïn thair Meetin Hooses.  On accoont o me, ye'll be brocht afore guviners an kïngs as wutnesses tae thaim an tae tha Gentiles.  But whaniver yis ir lïftit an brocht tae thrial, dïnnae be ower enxious aboot whut tae say or hoo tae say ït. Ye'll be gien tha richt wurds at tha richt time.  Fer ït'll no be you that's spakin, but tha Spïrit o yer Faither spakin throu ye.  Brithers wull han ower thair brithers tae be kïllt, an faithers thair weans; an weans wull rise up agin thair faithers an mithers an hae thaim püt tae deith as weel.  Ye'll be haitit bi yin an aa on accoont o me, but he that tholes tae tha enn wull be saved.  Whan yis ir persecutit ïn yin place, fly tae anither. A tell ye tha truith, ye'll no hae feenished gaun throu aa tha toons o Israel afore tha Sinn o Man cums bak! A follaer ïs no abain hïs taicher, ner a sarvint abain hïs maistèr.  Whut mair can tha follaer ax than tae be laik hïs taicher, or tha sarvint tae be laik hïs maistèr? Gin the' hae caad tha heid o tha hoose Beelzebul , weel, whut wull the' no caa aa tha yins o hïs hoosehold! Sae dïnnae be afeart o thaim. Thair's naethin covert ower that'll no cum tae licht, ner hïd that'll no be kent.  Whut A tell ye ïn tha dairk, spake oot ïn tha braid daylicht; whut's whuspert ïn yer ear, blare ït oot frae tha ruiftaps.  Dïnnae be feart o thaim that kïll tha bodie but cannae kïll tha sowl. Rether, be afeart o tha Yin that can desthroy baith bodie an sowl ïn hell.  Ir twa wee sparras no soul fer a pennie? Yit no yin o thaim wull faa tae tha grun wioot yer Faither knowin ït.  Fer tha verie hairs o yer heid ir aa coontit.  Sae dïnnae be feart; yis ir warth mair ner a hale wheen o sparras.  Whaiver's no feart tae own me afore men, A wull own hïm tae afore ma Faither ïn heiven.  But whaiver disowns me afore men, A wull disown hïm afore ma Faither ïn heiven. Dïnnae be thïnkin A hae cum tae brïng peace tae tha irth. Na, A dïdnae cum tae brïng peace, but a sword.  Fer A hae cum tae turn a man agin hïs faither, a dochtèr agin hir mither, a dochtèr-ïn-laa agin hir mither-ïn-laa;  ït'll be tha yins leevin wi a man that wull be agin hïm.  Oniebodie that loves hïs faither or hïs mither mair ner me ïs no warthie o me; nether ïs tha yin that loves hïs sinn or hïs dochtèr mair ner me warthie o me.  An oniebodie that daesnae tak up hïs cross an follae me ïs no warthie o me.  Whaiver fins hïs life wull loass ït, an whaiver loasses hïs life on accoont o me wull fin ït. Hïm that walcums you walcums me, an hïm that walcums me walcums tha Yin that sent me.  Oniebodie that maks a proaphit walcum on accoont o hïs bein a proaphit wull be gien a proaphit's reward, an oniebodie that maks a guid man walcum on accoont o bein a guid man wull git a guid man's reward.  An ïf oniebodie gies even a bicker o coul wattèr tae yin o these weans acause he ïs ma follaer - A tell ye, he wull no be wantin fer a reward, that's fer shair!” Eftèr Jesus haed daen giein oardèrs tae hïs twal follaers, he gaed on frae thair tae taich an praich ïn tha toons roon aboot. Noo Jhone wus ïn jail, an whaniver he heerd whut Christ wus daein, he sent [twa o] hïs follaers  an the' axt hïm, “Ir you tha Yin that wus supposed tae cum , or shud we be lukkin oot fer some ither bodie?”  Jesus toul thaim, “Gae bak an gie Jhone an accoont o whut ye hear an see.  Blin fowk can see noo, lameters can waak, fowk wi leprosie ir made weel. Deef fowk can hear. Tha deid leeve agane. An tha Guid News ïs praicht tae tha puir.  An blisst ïs tha yin that daesnae misdoot me .” As Jhone's follaers wur leain, Jesus stairtit tae taak tae tha croods aboot hïm: “Whut dïd yis gang oot ïntae tha wuldèrness fer tae see? Wus ït tae see tha rushes sweein ïn tha wun?  If no, whut dïd ye thïnk ye wud see oot thair? A man aa rigged oot ïn fancie claes? Na, tha yins ïn fancie claes, ït's ïn kïngs' palaces ye wull fin them.  Sae whut dïd yis gae oot fer tae see? Wus ït a proaphit? Ay, A tell ye, an faur mair ner a proaphit.  Thïs ïs tha yin tha Scrïptures taak aboot whan the' say: ‘Lïsten, A wull senn oot ma messenger aheid o ye; he wull mak readie tha wye afore ye.’ A tell ye tha truith: amangst thaim boarn o a wumman, naebodie haes iver leeved that's mair impoartin ner Jhone tha Baptiser; yit tha yin that ïs laist ïn tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs a bettèr man ner hïm.  Frae tha time Jhone tha Baptiser stairtit tae praich up til noo, fowk ir tryin tae püsh thair wye ïntae tha Kïngdom o Heiven, an violent men ir takkin houl o ït.  Fer up tae Jhone's time, aa tha proaphits an tha Laa foretoul whut wus tae happen.  An ïf ye ir wullin tae believe whut A say, Jhone ïs tha Elijah that wus tae cum.  Let hïm that haes ears ïn hïs heid tak tent! Whut can A say aboot tha fowk noo-a-days? The' ir laik weans sïttin doon at tha mairket an caain oot tae tha ithers, ‘We played tha whustle fer ye, an ye wudnae daunce; we sung a dirge tae ye, an ye wudnae greet.’ Fer Jhone wusnae ïntae aitin ner drïnkin whan he cum, an the' say, ‘Thair's a baad spïrit ïn hïm.’  Yit tha Sinn o Man cum aitin an drïnkin, an the' say, ‘Wud ye luk at hïm, he's a glutton, an he's tarrible fand o tha drïnk sae he ïs - tha freen o tex men an wrangdaers!’ But daein whut's richt proves tha wusdom o God's wyes.” Then Jesus stairtit tae tak tae task tha cïties whar he haed daen tha maist o hïs mïracles, acause the' dïdnae repent.  “Sorra tae Chorazim, an sorra tae Bethsaida, fer ïf tha fowk o Tyre an Sidon haed saen tha warkin o God's pooer as yous hae saen ït, the' wud hae repentit lang syne ïn seckclaith an eshes.  But A'm tellin ye, tha fowk o Tyre an Sidon wull be bettèr aff on tha Day o Reckonin than yous wull.  An Capernaum, you micht thïnk ye'r weel on yer wye tae heiven. Na, but A'm tellin ye, ye'll be brocht doon tae hell! Fer ïf tha mïracles that wus daen ïn you haed bin daen ïn Sodom, ït wud be thair tae thïs day.  But A tell ye that Sodom wull be bettèr aff on tha day o Reckonin ner you.” At that time Jesus saed, “Faither, Loard o heiven an irth, A praise ye that ye hae kep these thïngs frae clivir an warlie-wise fowk, an made thaim clear eneuch fer weans tae unnèrstan.  Ay, Faither, ït haes plaised ye tae dae ït thïs wye. Ma Faither haes gien aa thïngs ower tae me, an naebodie unnèrstans tha Sinn apairt frae tha Faither, an naebodie unnèrstans tha Faither apairt frae tha Sinn, an whaiver tha Sinn wants tae reveal hïm tae.  Cum tae me, aa you that's wearie an burdent, an A wull gie ye rest.  Tak ma yauk upon ye an lairn frae me, fer A'm gentle an hummle ïn hairt, an yis'll fin rest fer yer sowls.  Fer ma yauk ïs aisie, an ma burden ïs licht.” At that time Jesus gaed throu tha coarnfiels on tha Sabbath day. Hïs follaers wur hung'rie got, an the' begun tae pluck tha heids aff tha coarn an the' et thaim.  Whaniver tha Pharisees saen thïs, the' saed tae hïm, “Luk! Yer follaers ir daein whut's agin tha Laa on tha Sabbath day!”  He saed bak tae thaim, “Hae ye no read whut Davit daen whaniver hïm an hïs freens wus hung'rie?  He gaed ïntae tha Hoose o God, an hïm an hïs freens et tha halie showbreid. An thair wus naebodie barrin tha preeshts allooed tae dae thïs.  Or hae ye no read ïn tha Laa that tha preeshts ïn tha Hoose o God ir allooed tae wark on tha Sabbath Day, an yit the'ir no hel tae accoont fer brekkin tha Laa?  A tell ye, we'r taakin aboot sumthin mair impoartin ner tha Hoose o God here.  Tha Scrïpture says: ‘It's mercie A'm eftèr, A'm no eftèr secryfice’, an ïf ye haed unnèrstud tha mainin o these wurds, ye wudnae hae saed that ma follaers wus sïnners whan the' ir no!  Fer tha Sinn o Man ïs Loard o tha Sabbath anaa.” Jesus gaed on frae that place, an he gaed ïntae thair Meetin Hoose.  An thair wus a man thair an hïs richt han wus wuthert. Lukkin tae hae sumthin agin Jesus, tha Pharisees axt hïm, “Ir ye allooed tae hail on tha Sabbath day?”  Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “If onie o yis haes a sheep an ït faas ïntae a sheuch on tha Sabbath, wud ye no tak houl o ït an pu ït oot?  Is a man no warth faur mair ner a sheep? Ay, sae ït's aa richt tae dae guid on tha Sabbath day!”  Wi that, he saed tae tha man, “Streetch oot yer han.” Sae he streetcht ït oot an ït wus aa hailt, an jist as guid as tha ither yin.  But tha Pharisees gaed oot an the' collogued thegither hoo the' cud dae awa wi Jesus. Jesus, knowin thïs, left that place. An a wile thrang o fowk follaed hïm, an he made aa thair seeck fowk bettèr,  an he gien thaim a warnin no tae tell oniebodie wha he wus.  Thïs wus tae fülfill whut wus spauk aboot hïm throu tha proaphit Isaiah: “Here ïs ma sarvint, ma Han-waaled Yin; he's tha yin A love, he's tha yin A'm weel plaised wi; A'll pit ma Spïrit on hïm, an he'll tell oot justice tae tha nations. He'll no cum argyin or cryin oot; nether wull he rise hïs voice ïn tha raas. A bent reed he'll no brek aff, an he'll no snuff oot a smoldèrin wïck, til he leads justice on tae vïctrie. In hïs name tha nations wull pit thair trust.” Then the' brocht hïm a man bothert wi ïll spïrits. He wus blin an dum, an Jesus made hïm bettèr, sae he cud baith taak an see.  Aa tha fowk wur thunnèrstruck an the' saed, “Cud thïs be tha Sinn o Davit?”  But whaniver tha Pharisees heerd thïs, the' saed, “It ïs onlie bi Beelzebul, tha heidyin o tha ïll spïrits, that thïs fella casts oot ïll spïrits.”  Knowin thair thochts Jesus saed tae thaim, “Iverie kïngdom divïd agin ïtsel wull gae tae reck an ruin, an iverie cïtie or hoose divïd agin ïtsel wull no stan.  An ïf Satan casts oot Satan, he ïs divïd agin hissel, an hoo then cud hïs kïngdom stan?  An ïf A cast oot ïll spïrits bi tha pooer o Beelzebul, bi whut pooer then daes yer ain fowk cast thaim oot? Sae let thaim be tha yins tae judge ye fer whut ye hae saed.  But ïf A cast oot ïll spïrits bi tha Spïrit o God, ït proves that tha Kïngdom o God ïs here amang ye.  Or agane, hoo can oniebodie git ïntae a strang man's hoose an cairrie aff hïs belangins, less he furst tyes up tha strang man? Eftèr that, he can plunner awa!  Hïm that ïs no for me ïs agin me, an hïm that ïsnae giein me a han tae gether ïn, he micht as weel be scattèrin.  An sae A tell ye, men wull be forgien iverie sïn an blesphemie, but tha blesphemie agin tha Spïrit wull no be forgien.  Oniebodie that spakes a wurd agin tha Sinn o Man wull be forgien, but oniebodie that spakes agin tha Halie Spïrit wull no be forgien, nether ïn thïs age ner ïn tha age tae cum. Ye can tell a tree bi its fruit. Gin tha tree's guid, ïts fruit wull be guid; gin ït's baad ïts fruit wull be baad.  Ye sleekit shooer o vipers, hoo can ye say ocht that's guid whan ye'r wïckit yersels? Fer whut's ïn yer hairt wull cum oot o yer mooth.  A guid man brïngs guid thïngs oot o tha guidness stored ïn hïs hairt; a wïckit man brïngs wïckit thïngs oot o hïs store o wïckitness.  But A tell ye, on tha Day o Reckonin men wull hae tae mak answer fer iverie careless wurd the' hae spauk.  Fer bi yer wurds ye'll be judged no guiltie, an bi yer wurds ye'll be condemned.” Then some o tha Pharisees an maistèrs o tha Laa saed tae hïm, “Maistèr, we want a mïraclis sign frae ye!”  He saed bak tae thaim, “It's onlie a wïckit an adultèrous genèration wud luk fer a mïraclis sign! But thair'll be nane gien apairt frae tha sign o tha proaphit Jonah.  Fer jist as Jonah wus thrie days an thrie nichts ïn tha belly o a bïg fïsh, ïn tha same wye tha Sinn o Man wull be thrie days an thrie nichts ïn tha hairt o tha irth.  Tha men o Nineveh wull stan up at tha Day o Reckonin wi thïs genèration an the'll condemn ït; fer they repentit whaniver Jonah praicht tae thaim, an yit tha yin that's here noo ïs mair ner onie Jonah.  Tha Queen o tha Sooth wull stan up wi thïs genèration tae be judged as weel on that Day, an she wull condemn ït; fer she cum frae tha enns o tha irth fer tae lïsten tae Solomon's wusdom, an noo yin abain Solomon ïs here, an yis ir no lïstenin! Whan an ïll spïrit cums oot o a man, ït raiks throu tha desert lukkin fer rest. But ït fins nane.  Then ït says, ‘A'll jist gae bak tae whar A wus leevin afore.’ Whaniver ït gaes bak, ït fins tha hoose empie, swep clain an aa redd up.  Then ït gangs an taks wi ït seiven ither spïrits mair wïckit ner ïtsel, an the' aa gae ïn an the' settle thair. An that man enns up faur waur ner he wus afore. That's tha wye ït'll be wi thïs wïckit genèration.” While Jesus wus still taakin tae tha thrang, hïs mither an hïs brithers stud ootbye, lukkin tae spake tae hïm.  Summodie toul hïm, “Yer mither an yer brithers ir waitin ootbye, lukkin tae spake tae ye.”  But Jesus cum bak wi thïs, “Wha ïs ma mither, an wha ir ma brithers?”  Pointin tae hïs follaers, he saed, “Luk, thair's ma mither an ma brithers!  Fer thaim at daes tha wull o ma Faither ïn heiven ïs ma brither an ma sïstèr an ma mither!” That verie day Jesus gaed oot o tha hoose an sut doon bi tha loch shore.  Sitch a thrang o fowk gethert roon hïm that he got ïntae a bóat an sut ïn ït, while aa tha fowk stud bye on tha shore.  An he toul thaim a hale wheen o thïngs bi parables, laik thïs yin: “Thair wus thïs fairmer gaed oot tae saa seed.  An as he wus scattèrin ït, some drapt doon alang tha pad, an tha burds flew doon an peckt thaim up.  Thair wus some seed faad doon on roakie grun, whar thair wusnae much clye. It sprung up quïck, becas tha clye wus shalla,  but as shune as it brairdit an tha sin ris, tha plants wus scorcht, an the' wuthert awa acause the' haed nae ruits.  Ither seed faad doon amang thoarns an breers, that sprung up, tuk ower an chokt ït.  Yit ither seed faad on guid grun, whar ït brocht a hairst o a hunnèr, sïxtie or thurtie times whut wus sowed.  Let hïm that haes ears ïn hïs heid tak tent!” Hïs follaers cum tae hïm an axt, “Fer why dae ye spake tae tha fowk ïn parables?”  He saed, “Tae you God haes gien an unnèrstannin o tha saicrets o tha Kïngdom o Heiven, but no tae thaim.  Fer hïm that haes plentie wull be gien mair, an he wull hae mair ner eneuch. An hïm that haes lïttle, even whut he haes wull be tuk awa frae hïm.  Thïs ïs tha raison A spake tae thaim ïn parables: ‘Tha mair the' luk, the' dïnnae see; tha mair the' hear, the' dïnnae lïsten or unnèrstan.  Isaiah's proaphesie cums aboot ïn thaim whaniver he says: “You wull aye be hearin but niver unnèrstannin; ye'll aye be seein but niver takkin ït ïn. Fer tha hairt o these fowk haes becum haird; the' can harlie hear wi thair ears, an the' hae shut thair een. Itherwise the' cud see wi thair een, the' cud hear wi thair ears, the' cud unnèrstan wi thair hairts, an the' wud turn tae me, tae hail thaim.”’ But your een ïs blisst acause they can see, an your ears tae, acause they can hear.  Fer A tell ye tha truith, thair's monies a proaphit an monies a guid man wud hae gien oniethin fer tae see whut yous see but the' dïdnae see ït; an tae hear whut yous hear but the' dïdnae hear ït. Lïsten then tae whut tha parable o tha sower mains:  Whan oniebodie hears tha message aboot tha Kïngdom an daesnae unnèrstan ït, alang cums tha Wïckit Yin an snaps awa whut wus sowed ïn hïs hairt. Thïs ïs whut tha seed sowed nixt tha pad stans fer.  An then tha seed that faad on roakie grun stans fer tha bodie that hears tha message, an taks ït ïn richt awa wi a gled hairt.  But seein as he haes nae ruits, ït onlie houls wi hïm fer a wee while. Whan haird times an trouble cums acause o God's wurd, he jist gies up thair an then.  Then tha seed that faad doon amang tha thoarns, that's laik a bodie that hears tha message, but wi hïm chasin eftèr money, an tha bothers o thïs warl, tha message gets chokt an ït aa cums tae naethin.  But tha seed that faad doon on guid grun ïs laik tha bodie that taks tha wurd tae hairt an unnèrstans ït, brïngin ïn a yiel o thurtie, sïxtie or a hunnèr times mair ner wus sowed.” Jesus toul thaim anither parable: “Tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs laik a man that sowed guid seed ïn hïs fiel.  But whaniver aa tha fowk wus sleepin, hïs enemie cum an sowed geel amang tha wheat, an then he tuk aff.  Noo as shune as tha wheat brairdit an tha ears appeart, tha weeds cum up as weel.  An tha fairmer's sarvin men cum up tae hïm. ‘Maistèr,’ the' saed, ‘dïd ye no sow guid seed ïn yer fiel? Whar then dïd tha weeds cum frae?’  ‘An enemie haes daen thïs,’ he saed. Tha sarvints axt hïm, ‘Dae ye want iz tae gae oot an pu thaim up?’  ‘Na,’ he saed bak tae thaim, ‘becas whaniver ye'r pu'in oot tha weeds, ye'll mebbe ruit up tha wheat alang wi thaim.  Let thaim baith growe thegither tae tha hairvest. An then A'll tell tha reapers: Gether up tha weeds furst an tye thaim up ïn bunnels fer burnin; then awa an gether up tha wheat an brïng ït ïntae ma barn.’ ” Jesus toul thaim yit anither parable: “Tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs laik a wee mustèrt seed, that a man tuk an sowed ïn hïs fiel.  Tha mair ït stairts aff as a gye wee seed, yit whan ït growes, ït becums a bïg büsh an then a tree, sae as tha wee burds cum an tuk shiltèr ïn ïts brenches.” An here's anither yin he toul thaim: “Tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs laik yeast that a wumman tuk fer tae mak breid. She warkt that wee bït ïntae a bïg boul o flure, tae tha hale lock o ït ris.” Jesus spauk ïn parables whan he toul tha croods aa these thïngs; he dïdnae say ocht tae thaim wi'oot uisin a parable.  Thïs wus tae brïng aboot whut tha proaphit saed wud happen: “A wull taak tae ye ïn parables, A wull tell ye thïngs hïd since tha warl begun.” Then he left tha crood o fowk an went ïntae tha hoose. Hïs follaers cum tae hïm an saed, “Wud ye tell iz whut that parable o tha weeds ïn tha fiel mains?”  He answert, “Tha yin that sowed tha guid seed ïs tha Sinn o Man.  Tha fiel ïs tha warl, an tha guid seed stans fer tha sinns o tha Kïngdom. Tha weeds stans fer tha childèr o tha wïckit yin,  an tha enemie that sows thaim ïs tha Deil. Tha hairvest ïs tha enn o tha warl, an tha reapers ir tha angels.  Jist tha wye tha weeds ir pu'ed up an brunt ïn tha fire, that's tha wye ït'll be at tha enn o tha warl.  Tha Sinn o Man wull senn oot hïs angels, an the'll ruit oot o hïs Kïngdom iveriethin that brïngs aboot sïn an aa thaim that daes wrang.  An tha angels wull flïng thaim ïntae tha fierie furnace, whar thair wull be sair greetin an scringein o teeth.  Then tha yins that's daen richt wull shine brichtlie laik tha sin ïn thair Faither's Kïngdom. Let hïm that haes ears ïn hïs heid tak tent! Tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs laik treysure hïd ïn a fiel. Thair wus thïs man fun ït, an he went an hïd ït agane; an he wus that plaised aboot ït, he went an soul aa he haed an he bocht tha fiel. An agane, tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs laik a dailer on tha luk-oot fer fancie pearls.  Whaniver he fun yin that wus warth a hale lock, awa he went an soul iveriethin he haed, an he bocht ït. Or agane, tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs laik a neyt that the' lut doon ïntae tha loch, an ït catched aa kines o fïsh.  Whaniver ït wus fu, tha fïshermen haaled ït ashore. Then the' sut doon an the' waaled throu ït. The' püt tha guid fïsh ïntae creels, but the' throwed tha baad yins awa.  That's hoo ït'll be at tha enn o tha warl. Tha angels'll cum an soart oot tha wïckit fowk frae tha guid,  an the'll cast thaim ïntae tha fierie furnace, whar thair'll be greetin an scringein o teeth.” “Hae ye unnèrstud aa these thïngs?” Jesus axt hïs follaers. “Ay, we hae,” the' saed.  He saed tae thaim, “Weel then, iverie maistèr o tha Laa that haes bin schuiled ïn tha thïngs o tha Kïngdom o Heiven, ïs laik tha guidman o tha hoose that brïngs oot o hïs storeruim treysures baith oul an new.” An whan Jesus wus daen tellin these parables, he gaed on frae thair,  an bak tae hïs hametoon. An whaniver he stairtit taichin tha fowk thair ïn tha Meetin Hoose, the' wur aa dumfoonèrt. “Whar dïd thïs man get hïs wusdom an mïraclis pooers frae?” the' axt.  “Is thïs no jist tha cairpentèr's sinn? Hïs mither's caad Mary, ïsn't she? An ir hïs brithers no Jeames, Joseph, Simon an Judas?  Shair hïs sïstèrs ir aa here wi iz! Sae whar dïd thïs bodie get aa thïs frae?”  An the' tuk umrage at hïm. But Jesus saed tae thaim, “A proaphit's niver weel thocht o ïn hïs hametoon, or ïn hïs ain hoose.”  An he dïdnae dae monie mïracles thair acause o thair want o faith. At that time Herod tha Tetrarch heerd whut the' wur sayin aboot Jesus,  an he saed tae hïs sarvin men, “Thïs ïs Jhone tha Baptiser; he haes ris frae tha deid! That's tha raison he haes these mïraclis pooers.”  Noo afore thïs, Herod haed tuk houl o Jhone, an he haed hïm tyed up an püt awa ïn jail acause o Herodias, hïs brither Phïlip's wife,  fer Jhone wus aye tellin hïm, “Tha Laa daesnae alloo ye tae hae hir!”  Herod wud hae kïllt Jhone, but he wus afeart o tha crood turnin on hïm, acause the' lukt on Jhone as a proaphit. But at Herod's birthday pairtie, tha dochtèr o Herodias daunced afore thaim an plaised Herod that much, that he swore he'd gie hir whutiver she axt fer.  Tha wee lass saed - ït wus hir mither püt hir up tae ït - “Jist gie me tha heid o Jhone tha Baptiser on a plattèr!”  Tha kïng wus wile annoyt aboot thïs, but acause o whut he'd swore an tha yins wi hïm roon tha table, he oardèrt thaim tae gie hir whut she haed axt fer.  Sae he got thaim tae tak tha heid aff Jhone ïn tha jail.  The' brocht ït bak on a plattèr an the' gien ït tae tha wee lass, an she cairriet ït tae hir mither.  Jhone's follaers cum an tuk hïs bodie awa an buriet ït. Then the' went an toul Jesus whut haed happent. Whaniver Jesus heerd thïs, he went awa ïn a bóat bi hïs lane tae a quait place. But whan tha croods got tae know aboot ït, the' follaed hïm on fit frae tha toons.  An whan Jesus cum tae lan, he fun a quare thrang o fowk fornent hïm, an hïs hairt went oot tae thaim an he cured thair seeck fowk.  Then as evenin wus draain ïn, hïs follaers cum tae hïm an saed, “Thïs ïs a richt oot o tha wye place, an ït's gettin late. Senn tha croods awa, sae the' can gang tae tha clachans an buy thairsels a bite tae ait.”  Jesus saed, “The' dïnnae need tae gae awa. Yous gie thaim sumthin tae ait.”  “We hae naethin here but five bannocks an twa fïsh,” the' reponed.  “Weel, brïng thaim here tae me,” he saed.  He oardèrt tha fowk tae sït doon on tha gress. An takkin tha five bannocks an tha twa fïsh an lukkin up tae heiven, he blisst ït an brauk tha bannocks. Then he gien thaim tae hïs follaers, an tha follaers gien thaim tae tha fowk.  The' aa et thair fïll, an hïs follaers gethert up twal creels fu o aa tha wee bïts that wus left ower.  Tha nummer o thaim that et wus aboot five thoosan men, niver mine weemen an weans. Richt awa, Jesus made tha follaers get ïntae tha bóat an gae on aheid o hïm tae tha ither side, while he toul tha thrang tae gae hame.  Eftèr he haed sent thaim awa, he went up tha muntin bi hissel fer tae pray. At dailygan, he wus thair on hïs lane. Bi noo tha bóat wus aareadie miles awa frae tha lan; ït wus takkin a hemmerin frae tha waves, an tha wun wus agin ït.  Cum tha fowerth watch o tha nicht  Jesus gaed oot tae thaim, waakin on tha wattèr.  Whaniver hïs follaers saen hïm waakin on tha wattèr, the' wur hairt-scarred, an trimmlin wi fear the' caad oot, “It's a wraith!”  But strecht awa Jesus spauk oot an saed tae thaim, “Tak hairt! It's masel. Dïnnae be feart!” “Loard, ïf ït's you,” Petèr saed, “bïd me cum tae ye on tha wattèr.”  “Cum on then,” saed Jesus. Sae Petèr got doon oot o tha bóat, he waakt on tha wattèr, an he went nixt Jesus.  But whaniver he saen hoo strang tha wun wus, he wus afeart an he stairtit tae sink. “Loard, save me!” he caad oot.  At yinst Jesus raxt oot hïs han an grïpt hïm. “Hae ye nae faith ava?” he saed. “Why dïd ye doot me?”  An whaniver the' climmed bak ïntae tha bóat, tha wun deed doon.  Then thaim that wur ïn tha bóat wurshipt hïm, sayin, “You are tha Sinn o God, an that's tha truith o ït!” Whan the' gaed bak ower tha loch agane, the' landit at Gennesaret.  An whaniver tha men o that place reconised Jesus, the' sent wurd roon tha hale kintrieside. An the' brocht aa thair seeck fowk tae hïm,  an plaidit wi hïm tae let thaim jist touch tha hem o hïs robe. An iveriebodie that toucht ït wus makkit weel agane. Then some Pharisees an maistèrs o tha Laa cum tae Jesus frae Jerusalem an the' axt hïm,  “Fer why dae yer follaers lea aside tha oul wyes o oor eldèrs? The' dïnnae even waash thair hans afore the' ait!”  Jesus cum bak wi thïs, “An fer why dae you lea aside tha laas o God fer tha sake o yer ain tradeetions?  Fer God gart ye thïs: ‘Honour yer faither an yer mither’, an: ‘Oniebodie that miscaas thair faither or mither maun be püt tae deith.’  But yous say that ït's aa richt fer a bodie tae tell hïs faither or mither, ‘Whutiver halp ye wud hae got frae me A hae vood tae gie tae God’;  an ye say he ïsnae obliged tae honour hïs parents wi ït. Bi thïs, ye mak a nonsense o tha wurd o God fer tha sake o yer tradeetion.  Ye hippycrates! Isaiah got ït richt whan he proaphesied thïs aboot ye: ‘Thïs nation honours me wi thair mooth,’ says God, ‘but thair hairt ïs faur awa frae me. Thair woarship's nae use ava; thair taichins ir naethin but man-made rules an regulations.’ ” Jesus caad tha thrang tae hïm an saed, “Lïsten tae me an unnèrstan whut A'm sayin.  Whut gaes ïntae a man's mooth daesnae sullie hïm, but whut cums oot o hïs mooth, ït's that sullies hïm.”  Then hïs follaers cum tae hïm an axt, “Dae ye ken that tha Pharisees wur gye ïll plaised whaniver the' heerd thïs?”  He saed, “Iverie plant ma heivenlie Faither haesnae plantit wull be pu'ed up bi tha ruits.  Lea thaim alane! The' ir naethin but blin guides. If a blin man taks anither blin man bi tha airm, tha baith o thaim wull faa ïntae tha sheuch.”  Petèr saed tae Jesus, “Tell iz whut that ither parable wus aboot.”  “Ir yous slow on tha uptake tae?” Jesus axt thaim.  “Dae yis no see that whutiver gaes ïntae yer mooth gaes ïntae yer belly an then passes on oot doon tha drain?  But tha thïngs that cum oot o tha mooth cum frae tha hairt, an that's whut sullies a bodie.  Fer oot o tha hairt cums wïckit thochts: murdèr an adultèrie, lustin an thievin, blesphemin an slandèrin fowk.  These thïngs ïs whut sullies a bodie; but aitin wioot tha rïtual waashin o hans daesnae sullie hïm.” Then Jesus upt an left that place, an he went awa tae tha dïstrict roon Tyre an Sidon.  An thïs Canaanite wumman frae thaim pairts cum tae hïm, cryin oot, “Loard, Sinn o Davit, hae peetie on me! Ma dochtèr ïs sufferin sumthin tarrible wi an ïll spïrit.”  Jesus niver saed a wurd. Sae hïs follaers cum tae hïm an plaidit wi hïm, “Senn hir awa, fer she's follaein iz an she'll no stap hir yellin oot.”  He saed bak, “A wus onlie sent tae tha loast sheep o tha Hoose o Israel.”  Tha wumman cum an got doon on hir knees afore hïm an she saed. “Loard, halp me!”  “It ïsnae richt,” saed he, “tae tak tha weans' breid an clod ït tae tha wee dugs.”  “Ay, Loard, that's richt” she saed, “but still wi aa, e'en tha wee dugs gits aitin tha crumbs that faa frae thair maistèrs' boord!”  Then Jesus saed bak tae hir, “Wumman, sitch an a faith ye hae! Ye'll get whut ye axt fer.” An hir dochtèr got bettèr that verie oor. Jesus quït thaim pairts an cum tae tha loch shore o Galilee. Then he gaed up tha side o tha muntin an sut doon.  An a wile thrang o fowk cum tae hïm, brïngin tha lameters, tha crippelt, blin fowk an dum fowk, an a hale lock o ithers, an the' leed thaim doon at hïs feet; an he made thaim weel agane.  Tha fowk wur stoondit whaniver the' wutnesst tha dum spakin, tha crippelt makkit weel, lameters waakin an tha blin bein able tae see. An the' gien glorie tae tha God o Israel. Jesus caad hïs follaers tae hïm an saed, “Ma hairt gaes oot tae these fowk; the' hae bin here wi me thïs thrie days an the' hae naethin lef tae ait. A dïnnae want tae senn thaim awa hame, or the'll drap wi hung'r alang tha róad.”  Hïs follaers saed bak tae hïm, “Whar cud we get eneuch breid oot here ïn tha wiles, tae feed sitch a crood o fowk?”  “Hoo monie loafs dae yis hae?” Jesus axt. “Seiven,” the' saed, “an a wheen o wee fïsh.”  He bïd tha crood o fowk sït thairsels doon on tha grun.  Then he tuk tha seiven loafs an tha fïsh, an whaniver he haed gien thenks, he brauk thaim ïntae bïts an gien thaim tae hïs follaers. Then they gien thaim tae tha crood.  The' aa et thair fïll. An eftèr that, tha follaers gethert up seiven creels fu o tha leains.  Tha nummer o men that et that day wus fower thoosan, niver mine weemen an weans.  Then Jesus sent tha thrang awa, an he got ïntae a bóat an gaed ower tae tha kintrie roon aboot Magadan. Yin day, tha Pharisees an Sadducees cum tae Jesus an tried tae ketch hïm oot bi axin hïm tae show thaim a sign frae heiven.  He saed, “At dailygan, ye say, ‘Tha weather's gaun tae be guid, fer tha sky ïs rid.’  An ïn tha moarnin, ye say, ‘It'll be wundie theday, fer tha sky ïs rid an threatinin.’ Sae yis can tell tha weather bi tha luk o tha sky, but yis cannae wark oot tha signs o tha times!  A wïckit an adultèrous genèration luks fer a mïraclis sign, but nane wull be gien ït apairt frae tha sign o Jonah.” Jesus then left thaim an gaed awa. An whaniver the' crosst tae tha ither side o tha loch, hïs follaers dïdnae mine tae tak breid wi thaim.  “Luk oot,” Jesus saed tae thaim. “Be on yer gaird agin tha yeast o tha Pharisees an tha Sadducees.”  The' taakt aboot thïs amang thairsels an saed, “It's becas we dïdnae brïng onie breid wi iz.”  Jesus kent whut the' wur on aboot, sae he saed tae thaim, “Fer why ir ye taakin amang yersels aboot haein nae breid? Hae yis nae faith ava?  Dae yis still no unnèrstan? Dae yis no mine tha five loafs A gien til tha five thoosan, an aa tha baskets o leains yis gethert up eftèr?  Or tha seiven loafs A gie til tha fower thoosan, an hoo monie creels yis gethert up anaa?  Hoo ïs ït yis dïnnae unnèrstan that A wus no taakin tae ye aboot breid? A'm tellin ye, jist be on yer gaird agin tha yeast o tha Pharisees an Sadducees.”  An then the' unnèrstud that he wus no tellin thaim tae gaird agin tha yeast uised ïn breid, but agin tha taichin o tha Pharisees an Sadducees. Whaniver Jesus cum tae tha dïstrict o Caesarea Phïlippi, he axt hïs follaers, “Wha dae fowk say tha Sinn o Man ïs?”  The' saed, “A wheen say Jhone tha Baptiser; some wud say Elijah; an still ithers, Jeremiah or yin o tha proaphits.”  “But whut aboot yersels?” he axt. “Wha dae you say that A am?”  Simon Petèr saed bak, “You ir tha Christ, tha Sinn o tha leevin God.”  Jesus saed, “Blisst ir ye, Simon sinn o Jonah, fer thïs wus no revealt tae ye bi onie human bein, but bi ma Faither ïn heiven.  A tell ye, frae noo on you ir Petèr , an on thïs roak A wull big ma kirk, an aa tha pooers o hell wull no owercum ït.  A wull gie ye tha keys o tha Kïngdom o Heiven; an whutiver ye bine on irth wull be bun ïn heiven, an whutiver ye lowse on irth wull be lowsed ïn heiven.”  Then he bïd hïs follaers no tae tell oniebodie that he wus tha Christ. Frae that time on Jesus stairtit tae mak ït clear tae hïs follaers that he maun gae tae Jerusalem, an he maun suffer monies a thïng at tha hans o tha eldèrs, tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa. He toul thaim that he maun be püt tae deith an be ris up tae life on tha thurd day.  Petèr tuk hïm tae tha yin side an begun tae scoul hïm. “Niver, Loard!” he saed. “Thïs wull niver happen tae you!”  Jesus turnt an saed tae Petèr, “Git ahint me, Satan! Ye ir a thrip-stane tae me; fer ye gie nae thocht tae tha thïngs o God. Yer heid's fu o tha thïngs o men!” Then Jesus saed tae hïs follaers, “If oniebodie wants tae follae eftèr me, he maun ferget aboot hissel aathegither, tak up hïs cross an stïck clase tae me.  Fer whaiver wants tae save hïs life wull loass ït, but hïm that loasses hïs life on ma accoont wull fin ït.  Whut guid wull ït be fer a bodie ïf he gets tha hale warl, an yit loasses hïs ain sowl? Shair thair's naethin a man cud gie tae get bak hïs ain sowl, ïs thair?  Fer tha Sinn o Man ïs gaun tae cum wi hïs angels ïn hïs Faither's glorie, an then he'll reward iverie sing'l bodie accoardin tae whut the' hae daen.  A tell ye tha truith, thair's yins stannin here, an ït's fer sartin the'll no dee, afore the' see tha Sinn o Man cumin ïn hïs Kïngdom.” Eftèr sïx days Jesus tuk wi hïm Petèr, Jeames an Jhone tha brither o Jeames, an brocht thaim up ïntae a heich muntin bi thairsels.  Thair tha hale luk o hïm wus changed afore thair verie een. Hïs face shone laik tha sin, an hïs claes turnt white as tha licht.  An jist then thair appeart afore thaim Moses an Elijah, an the' wur taakin wi Jesus.  Petèr saed tae Jesus, “Loard, A'm gled we ir here tae see thïs. If ye laik, A wull pit up thrie shiltèrs, yin fer you, yin fer Moses an yin fer Elijah.”  An he wus still taakin, whaniver a bricht clood cum roon thaim, an a voice frae tha clood saed, “Thïs ïs ma Sinn that A love; wi hïm A'm weel plaised. Lïsten tae hïm!”  Whaniver tha follaers heerd thïs, the' faad doon wi thair faces tae tha grun, hairt-scarred.  But Jesus cum an püt hïs han on thaim. “Git up,” he saed. “Dïnnae be feart.”  Whaniver the' lukt up, thair wus naebodie thair but Jesus. An as the' wur cumin doon tha muntin, Jesus warnt thaim, “Dïnnae tell oniebodie whut yis hae saen, til tha Sinn o Man haes bin ris frae tha deid!”  Tha follaers axt hïm, “Sae hoo cum tha maistèrs o tha Laa tell iveriebodie that Elijah haes tae cum furst, afore tha Messiah?”  Jesus saed, “Deed ay, Elijah ïs tae cum furst tae get aa readie fer tha Messiah.  But A'm tellin ye, Elijah haes cum aareadie, an the' dïdnae ken wha he wus, but the' daen tae hïm aa the' wantit. In tha same wye tha Sinn o Man ïs gaun tae suffer at thair hans.”  Then hïs follaers unnèrstud ït wus Jhone tha Baptiser he wus taakin tae thaim aboot. Noo whaniver the' cum bak doon tha muntin tae tha crood o fowk, a man cum up tae Jesus an got doon on hïs knees afore hïm.  “Loard, hae mercie on ma sinn,” he saed, “fer he taks fïts an ïs sufferin wile baad. Monies a time he wud faa ïntae tha fire or ïntae tha wattèr.  A brocht hïm tae yer follaers, but the' cud dae naethin fer hïm.”  “You fowk ir faithless an aisie led,” Jesus saed. “Hoo lang wull A be wi ye afore yis believe? Hoo lang dae A hae tae pit up wi ye? Brïng tha wee lad here tae me.”  Jesus gien tha ïll spïrit a richt barjin, an ït cum oot o tha boy, an he wus bettèr agane frae that verie mïnit.  Then tha follaers cum tae Jesus whaniver he wus on hïs ain, an axt, “Fer why cud we no cast oot tha ïll spïrit?”  He saed, “Acause yer faith ïs sae waik. A tell ye tha truith, ïf yis hae faith as smaa as a mustèrt seed even, yis'll say tae thïs muntin, ‘Shïft frae here tae thair,’ an ït'll shïft! Naethin wull be impoassible fer ye.”  [But ye can onlie git rïd o thïs kine o ïll spïrit bi prayer an fastin.] Whaniver the' cum thegither agane ïn Galilee, he saed tae thaim, “Tha Sinn o Man ïs gaun tae be hannit ower tae men that'll kïll hïm, but on tha thurd day he'll rise frae tha deid.” An wi that, sorra fïllt tha hairts o hïs follaers. Eftèr Jesus an hïs follaers cum tae Capernaum, tha collectors o tha tex fer tha Hoose o God cum up tae Petèr an axt, “Daes your taicher no pye tha Temple tex?”  “He daes shairlie,” he saed. Noo whaniver Petèr cum ïntae tha hoose, Jesus wus tha furst tae spake oot. “Whut dae ye thïnk, Simon?” he axt hïm. “Wha dae tha kïngs o tha irth collect thair dues an texes frae - frae thair ain fowk or frae ithers?”  “Frae ithers,” Petèr saed bak. An Jesus saed til hïm, “Then thair ain yins dïnnae hae tae pye, dae the?  Weel, we dïnnae want tae gie onie offence, sae gae ye doon tae tha loch an cast oot yer line. Tak tha furst fïsh ye ketch; apen ïts mooth an ye'll fin a coin. Tak that an gie ït tae thaim, an ït'll pye tha tex fer tha baith o iz!” Roon aboot that time tha follaers cum tae Jesus an axt, “Wha ïs tha maist thocht o ïn tha Kïngdom o Heiven?”  He caad a wean til hïm an stud hïm amang thaim.  An he saed, “A tell ye tha truith, ïf ye dïnnae change yer hale wye o gaun an becum laik wee childèr, ye'll niver git ïntae tha Kïngdom o Heiven.  Sae, whaiver maks lïttle o thairsels an becums laik thïs wean ïs tha maist impoartin ïn tha Kïngdom o Heiven. An whaiver walcums yin o these weans ïn ma name walcums me.  But ïf oniebodie leads asthray yin o these weans that believes ïn me, ït wud be faur bettèr fer hïm tae hae a mïllstane hung roon hïs neck an tae be droont ïn tha depths o tha sea! Dear halp tha warl fer tempin fowk tae dae wrang! Thair'll aye be thïngs that maks fowk dae wrang, but dear halp tha bodie that daes tha tempin!  If yer han or yer fit maks ye tae dae wrang, cut ït aff an cast ït awa. It ïs faur bettèr fer ye tae gae tae heiven wantin a han or a fit, ner tae hae twa hans or twa feet an be throwed ïntae tha iverlastin fire.  An ïf yer ee maks ye dae wrang, pu ït oot an cast ït awa. It ïs faur bettèr fer ye tae gae tae heiven wantin an ee, ner tae hae twa een an be throwed ïntae tha fire o hell. Tak tent that ye dïnnae luk doon on yin o these weans. Fer A tell ye that tha angels that luk eftèr thaim ir alang wi ma Faither ïn heiven, an the'ir readie onie mïnit tae spake up fer thaim. [Tha Sinn o Man haes cum tae save thaim that's loast.]  Whut dae ye thïnk? If a man haes a hunnèr sheep, an yin o thaim wannèrs, wull he no lea tha ninetie-nine on tha hïlls an gae tae luk fer tha yin that wannèrt aff?  An ïf he fins ït, A tell ye tha truith, he ïs mair gled aboot that yin sheep ner aboot tha ninetie-nine that dïdnae wannèr aff!  In tha same wye ma Faither ïn heiven ïsnae wullin that onie o these weans shud be loast. If yer brither daes ye wrang, gae an show hïm hïs sïn, jist atween tha twa o ye. If he lïstens tae ye, ye hae wun yer brither ower.  But ïf he'll no lïsten, tak yin or twa ithers alang, sae that - as tha Scrïpture says - ‘twarthie wutnesses wull testify tae tha truith o iverie wurd spauk.’  An ïf he wull no lïsten tae thaim, tell ït tae tha kirk; an ïf he wull no lïsten tae tha kirk ether, dail wi hïm tha wye ye wud dae wi a tex man, or tha haithen.  A tell ye tha truith, whutiver ye bine on irth wull be bun ïn heiven, an whutiver ye lowse on irth wull be lowsed ïn heiven.  Agane, A tell ye that ïf twa o ye here on irth agree aboot oniethin ye ax fer, ït'll be daen fer ye bi ma Faither ïn heiven.  Fer whar twa or thrie cum thegither ïn ma name, A'm thair amang thaim.” Then Petèr cum tae Jesus an axt, “Loard, hoo monie times am A tae forgie ma brither whan he daes wrang agin me? Up tae seiven times?”  Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “A tell ye, no seiven times, but mair laik seiventie times seiven  Sae ye see, tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs laik a kïng that wantit hïs sarvints tae settle thair accoonts wi hïm.  An as he stairtit tae dae thïs, a man that owed hïm a foartune  wus brocht tae hïm.  An becas he wusnae able tae pye, tha maistèr oardèrt that baith hïm an tha wife an tha weans, an aa that he haed shud be soul tae pye bak tha debt.  Tha sarvint faad doon on hïs knees afore hïm. ‘Gie me time,’ he plaidit, ‘an A wull pye bak iveriethin.’  Tha sarvint's maistèr tuk peetie on hïm, wiped oot hïs debt an lut hïm gang free.  But whaniver that sarvint gaed oot, he cum on yin o hïs fella sarvints that owed hïm twarthie thoosan pun . He tuk houl o hïm bi tha throat an saed, ‘You pye me bak whut ye owe me!’  Hïs fella sarvint faad doon on hïs knees an begged hïm, ‘Gie me time, an A wull pye ye bak.’  But he wudnae hear o ït. Insteed, he gan aff an haed tha man throwed ïntae jail til he cud pye up.  Whaniver tha ither sarvints saen whut wus gaun on, the' wur wile annoyt, an the' went an toul thair maistèr iveriethin that happent.  Then tha maistèr caad tha sarvint ïn. ‘You wïckit sarvint,’ he saed, ‘A wiped oot that debt o yers acause ye begged me tae.  Shud ye no hae tuk peetie on yer fella sarvint tha same wye A tuk peetie on you?’  Hïs maistèr wus that ang'rie got, he turnt hïm ower tae tha jailers tae be tortured til he pyed bak aa he owed.  Thïs ïs hoo ma heivenlie Faither wull dail wi iverie last yin o ye, ïf ye dïnnae forgie yer brither frae yer hairt.” Whaniver Jesus wus daen sayin these thïngs, he left Galilee. He gaed ïntae Judea an crosst ower tha rïver Joardan.  Bïg croods follaed hïm, an he hailt tha seeck amang thaim. Some Pharisees cum up tae hïm, an tae pit hïm tae tha test the' axt hïm, “Is a man allooed tae pit awa hïs wife fer onie an iverie raison?”  “Hae ye no read,” Jesus answert, “that richt frae tha stairt tha Creator ‘made men an he made weemen,’  an that he saed, ‘Fer thïs raison a man wull lea hïs faither an hïs mither an be joint tae hïs wife, an tha twa wull becum as yin’?  An noo the' ir nae mair twa seprit fowk, but the' ir yin. Sae whut God haes püt thegither, let nae man püll sinnerie.”  “Whut fer then,” the' axt hïm, “whut fer dïd Moses say that a man cud gie hïs wife a notysh o divorce an pit hir awa?”  Jesus saed, “Moses allooed ye tae divorce yer wifes acause yer hairts wus haird. But thïs wusnae tha wye o ït frae tha stairt.  A tell ye that oniebodie that pits awa hïs wife, fer ocht ither ner rinnin aff wi anither man, an then merries anither wumman - that man commïts adultèrie.” Hïs follaers saed tae hïm, “If that's tha wye o ït wi a man that haes a wife, shair ït wud be faur bettèr no tae merrie ava!”  Jesus saed, “It's no iveriebodie can hannle that, jist thaim that's halpt bi God.  Fer some ir eunuchs acause the' wur boarn that wye; ithers wur made that wye bi men; an ithers haes gien up tha chaunce o merriage acause o tha Kïngdom o Heiven. Tha yin that can hannle thïs shud accept ït.” Some weans wur brocht tae Jesus fer hïm tae pit hïs hans on thaim an pray fer thaim. Hïs follaers scoult tha yins that brocht thaim,  but Jesus saed, “Alloo tha weans cum tae me, an dïnnae houl thaim bak, fer tha Kïngdom o Heiven belangs tae tha laiks o thaim.”  An eftèr he püt hïs hans on tha weans tae bliss thaim, he gaed on frae thair. Noo, alang cum thïs man tae Jesus an axt hïm, “Maistèr, whut guid thïng maun A dae tae hae iverlastin life?”  “Whut dae ye main bi ‘guid’?” Jesus saed. “Thair ïs Yin alane that ïs guid. If ït's iverlastin life ye'r wantin, dae whut tha commauns bïds ye!”  “Whutch yins?” tha man axt. Jesus saed, “ ‘Dïnnae murdèr’. ‘Dïnnae commït adultèrie’. ‘Dïnnae tak whut's no yer ain’. ‘Dïnnae tell lees aboot ither fowk’.  ‘Gie respeck tae yer faither an yer mither’, an ‘Ye maun love yer nighber jist as much as yersel’.”  “A hae kep aa these,” tha young man saed. “Whut else dae A hae tae dae?”  Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “If ye hae a mine tae be perfait, awa an sell aa ye hae got, an gie ït awa tae tha puir, an ye'll hae walth ïn heiven. Then cum bak, an follae me.”  Whaniver tha young man heerd thïs, he wus doon ïn tha mooth an went awa, fer he wus quare an weel-aff. Then Jesus saed tae hïs follaers, “A tell ye tha truith, ït ïs haird fer a bodie that's weel-aff tae git ïntae tha Kïngdom o Heiven.  Ay, A'm tellin ye, ït wud be aisier fer a kemel tae gae throu tha ee o a needle ner fer a monied man tae git ïntae tha Kïngdom o God.”  Whaniver tha follaers heerd thïs, the' wur stoondit an axt, “Wha ïn aa tha warl can be saved then?”  Jesus lukt strecht at thaim an saed, “Wi man thïs ïs no poassible, but wi God aa thïngs ir poassible.”  Wi that, Petèr saed bak tae hïm, “Luk, we hae gien up iveriethin tae follae ye! Whut then wull thair be ïn ït fer us?”  Jesus saed tae thaim, “A tell ye tha truith, whaniver tha new warl cums aboot, an tha Sinn o Man sïts on hïs throne o glorie, yous that hae follaed me wull sït doon on twal thrones as weel, judgin tha twal clans o Israel.  An iverie yin that haes gien up hooses, or brithers, or sïstèrs, or faither, or mither, or [wife, or] childèr, or fairm o lan on accoont o me wull git bak a hunnèr times as much; an he wull inherit iverlastin life.  But monies a bodie that's foremaist noo wull be last then, an monie that's last noo wull be foremaist then.” “Fer tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs laik a fairmer that gan oot at tha scraich o day tae hire men tae wark ïn hïs vineyaird.  He saed he wud pye thaim a siller coin  fer tha day an he sent thaim oot ïntae hïs vineyaird.  Aboot nine ïn tha moarnin, he gan oot an saen ithers stannin ïn tha mairket place wi naethin tae dae.  He toul thaim, ‘Gae an wark ïn ma vineyaird as weel, an A'll pye ye a fair wage.’  Sae awa the' went. Tha fairmer gan oot an he daen tha same thïng aboot nuin, an then agane at thrie.  Roon aboot five ïn tha eftèrnuin he gaed oot an fun still ithers stannin roon ïn tha mairket place. He axt thaim, ‘Why hae ye bin hangin aboot here aa day lang daein naethin?’  ‘Acause naebodie haes tuk iz on,’ the' saed. He saed tae thaim, ‘Gae awa noo an wark ïn ma vineyaird as weel.’  Cum dailygan, tha fairmer saed tae hïs lansteward, ‘Caa tha warkers an pye thaim thair wages, stairtin wi tha last yins A tuk on an gaun bak tae tha furst.’  Tha warkers that wus hired roon five ïn tha eftèrnuin they cum, an iverie yin o thaim wus gien a siller coin apiece.  Sae whan tha yins cum that wus hired furst, the' wur lukkin tae git mair. But iverie last yin o thaim wus onlie gien a siller coin tha same as tha ithers.
