Whaniver the' got ït, the' stairtit tae grummle agin tha fairmer.  ‘Thaim men that wus hired last warkt onlie tha yin oor,’ the' saed, ‘an ye hae traitit thaim tha same as us that haes daen tha maist o tha wark an tholed tha hait o tha day.’  But he saed bak tae yin o thaim, ‘Freen, A'm bein fair eneuch tae ye. Dïd ye no say ye wud wark fer yin siller coin?  Tak whut's yours an aff ye gang. Fer A want tae gie tha man that wus hired last tha same as A gien you.  Dae A no hae tha richt tae dae whut A laik wi ma ain siller? Or dae ye begrudge me bein guid tae tha ithers?’  Sae tha last wull be foremaist,” saed Jesus, “an tha foremaist wull be last. [Monie fowk ïs caad, but few sing'lt oot.]” Noo as Jesus wus on tha róad up tae Jerusalem, he tuk tha twal follaers aside, an he saed tae thaim,  “Lïsten here, we'r fer Jerusalem, an tha Sinn o Man wull be bethrayed tae tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa. The' wull condemn hïm tae deith,  an the'll turn hïm ower tae tha Gentiles fer tae be mockt an whuppt an hung up on a cross. But on tha thurd day he'll rise tae life agane!” Then tha mither o Zebedee's sinns cum tae Jesus, an hir twa sinns alang wi hir. Faain doon afore hïm, she axt a favour o hïm.  “Whut ïs ït ye want?” he axt. She saed, “Wud ye see tae ït that yin o these twa sinns o mine wull sït at yer richt han, an tha tither at yer left han, ïn yer Kïngdom?”  “Ye dïnnae ken whut ye'r axin,” Jesus saed tae thaim. “Can you drïnk tha cup o sufferin that A'm gaun tae drïnk, [or can ye be baptised wi tha baptisin that A am tae be baptised wi]?” “Ay, that we can,” the' saed.  Jesus toul thaim, “Yis'll shairlie drïnk frae ma cup o sufferin, but tae sït at ma richt or ma left han side ïsnae fer me tae say. Ma Faither haes made thaim places readie fer tha yins he's sing'lt oot.”  Whan tha ither ten follaers heerd aboot thïs, the' wur wile ang'rie wi tha twa brithers.  But Jesus caad thaim thegither an saed, “Ye ken that thaim that rule ower tha Gentiles laird ït ower thair ain fowk, an thair heidyins aye lets thaim know wha's tha boss.  Wi you ït's no tae be laik that. Na, whaiver wants tae be impoartin amang ye maun be yer sarvint,  an whaiver wants tae be foremaist amang ye maun be yer slave;  jist tha wye tha Sinn o Man dïdnae cum tae be tendit tae, but fer tae sarve ithers, an tae gie up hïs life as a ransom fer monie fowk.” As Jesus an hïs follaers wur leain Jericho, a bïg crood o fowk follaed hïm.  An lo an behoul, sïttin on tha bunker o tha róad, thair wus these twa men that wur blin. An whaniver the' heerd Jesus wus passin bye, the' cryed oot, “Loard, Sinn o Davit, tak peetie on iz!”  Tha thrang chackt thaim an toul thaim tae be quait, but the' guldèrt aa tha mair, sayin, “Loard, Sinn o Davit, tak peetie on iz!”  Whaniver he heerd thaim, Jesus stapt. Then he caad tae thaim, “Whut dae yis want me tae dae fer ye?”  “Loard,” the' saed, “we want oor sicht bak.”  Hïs hairt went oot tae thaim an he püt hïs hans on thair een. An at yinst the' got thair sicht bak, an the' follaed eftèr Jesus. Whaniver the' wur nearhan Jerusalem an the' cum tae Bethphage on tha Moont o Olives, Jesus sent oot twa follaers,  an he saed tae thaim, “Gae tae tha clachan fornent ye, an at yinst ye'll fin a cuddie tethèrt thair, wi hir cowlt alangside o hir. Lowse tha raip, an brïng thaim tae me.  If oniebodie says ocht tae ye, tell hïm ‘tha Loard haes need o thaim’, an he'll senn thaim richt awa.”  Thïs cum aboot fer tae fülfill whut wus spauk throu tha proaphit: “Say tae tha dochtèr o Zion, ‘Luk see, yer kïng ïs on hïs wye tae ye, gentle an ridin on a cuddie, on a cowlt, tha foal o a cuddie.’ ” Tha follaers gan awa an daen as the' wur bïd.  The' brocht tha cuddie an tha cowlt, an the' püt thair claes on thaim fer Jesus tae sït on.  An thair wus a hale thrang o fowk gethert, tha maist o thaim spreedin thair claes on tha róad, while ithers sneddit brenches aff tha trees, an the' strewed thaim on tha pad fer hïm tae ride ower.  Tha croods that gan aheid o hïm an thaim that follaed behin cryed oot, “Hosanna tae tha Sinn o Davit!” “Blisst be tha Yin that cums ïn tha name o tha Loard!” “Hosanna ïn tha heichest heiven!”  Whaniver Jesus went ïntae Jerusalem, tha hale cïtie wus ïn a stïr an the' axt, “Wha wud thïs man be?”  An tha croods saed bak tae thaim, “Thïs ïs Jesus, tha proaphit frae Nazareth ïn Galilee.” Jesus went ïntae tha Hoose o God an driv oot aa tha dailers that wus buyin an sellin ïn tha coortyaird. He coupt tha tables o tha siller changers an whammelt tha saits o thaim that wus sellin doos.  “It ïs writ doon,” he saed tae thaim, “that ‘ma hoose wull be caad a hoose o prayer’, but yous ir turnin ït ïntae a den o robbers!” Tha blin an tha lameters cum tae hïm thair ïn tha Hoose o God, an he made thaim bettèr.  But whaniver tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa saen tha wunnèrfu thïngs he daen, an heerd tha verie weans creein oot ïn tha Temple gruns, “Hosanna tae tha Sinn o Davit!” - weel, the' got wile ang'rie.  “Dae ye hear whut these weans ir sayin?” the' axt Jesus. “Ay,” he reponed, “hae yis niver read whut tha Scrïptures say, ‘Frae oot o tha mooth o childèr an weans ye hae brocht wurds o praise’?”  An Jesus left thaim an he gaed awa oot o tha cïtie tae Bethanie, whar he stapt fer tha nicht. At tha scraich o day, as he wus on hïs wye bak tae tha cïtie, he wus hung'rie.  An seein a fïg tree bi tha róad, he gaed up tae ït but fun naethin on ït apairt frae leafs. Then he saed tae ït, “May ye niver bair fruit agane!” An at yinst tha tree wuthert up.  An whaniver hïs follaers saen thïs, the' wur dumfoonèrt. “Hoo dïd tha fïg tree weezen up an dee sae quïck?” the' axt.  Jesus saed, “A tell ye tha truith, ïf ye hae faith an ye dïnnae doot, no alane can ye dae whut wus daen tae thon fïg tree, but ye cud even say tae thïs muntin, ‘Be shïftit frae whar ye ir, an cast yersel ïntae tha sea!’ an ït'll be daen.  If ye believe, God wull gie ye whut ye ax fer ïn prayer.” Jesus went bak ïntae tha Temple gruns, an while he wus taichin, tha heid preeshts an tha Jewish eldèrs cum up tae hïm. “Bi whut thortie ir ye daein these thïngs?” the' axt. “An wha gien ye tha thortie?”  Jesus saed, “A want tae ax ye yin question. If ye gie me an answer, then A'll tell ye bi whut thortie A dae these thïngs.  Jhone's baptisin - whar dïd ït cum frae? Wus ït frae heiven, or wus ït jist a notion o man?” The' stairtit tae taak aboot ït amang thairsels an the' saed, “If we say, ‘Frae heiven,’ he'll ax iz, ‘Sae hoo cum yis dïdnae believe hïm?’  But ïf we say, ‘Frae men,’ then we hae tha fowk tae reckon wi, fer the' aa houl that Jhone wus a proaphit.”  Sae the' saed bak tae Jesus, “We cannae tell.” An Jesus saed, “Then A'll no be tellin yis ether bi whut thortie A dae these thïngs!” “Whut dae ye thïnk aboot thïs? Thair wus a man that haed twa sinns. He gaed tae tha furst yin an saed, ‘Sinn, aff ye gang an wark theday ïn tha vineyaird.’  ‘A wull not,’ he saed, but latèr on he renaiged, an he dïd go.  Then tha faither gaed tae tha ither sinn an he saed tha same tae hïm. An he saed bak, ‘A wull, sïr,’ but he niver went.  Noo whutch yin o tha twa daen whut hïs faither wantit?” “Tha furst yin,” the' saed. Jesus reponed, “A tell ye tha truith, tex men an weemen wi a baad name aboot tha toon wull get ïntae tha Kïngdom o God aheid o ye.  Fer Jhone cum fer tae show ye tha wye o righteousness, an ye dïdnae believe hïm, but tha tex men an tha weemen wi a baad name, they dïd. An even eftèr ye saa thïs, ye dïdnae repent an believe hïm. Lïsten tae anither parable. Thair wus thïs lanlaird that plantit a vineyaird. He fenced ït aa roon, he dug a winepress ïn ït an bigged a luk-oot tooer. Then he set tha vineyaird tae a wheen o tenant-fairmers tae rin, an gan awa on a thrip tae anither kintrie.  An whaniver ït wus hairvest time, he sent hïs sarvints tae tha fairmers fer tae collect tha fruit.  Tha fairmers tuk houl o hïs sarvints; the' bate yin o thaim, the' püt anither tae deith, an the' staned a thurd.  Then he sent ither sarvints tae thaim, mair ner he sent tha furst time, an tha fairmers traitit thaim aa tha same wye.  Last o aa, he sent hïs ain sinn tae thaim. ‘He's ma ain sinn, shairlie the'll hae regaird fer hïm!’ he saed.  But whaniver tha tenant-fairmers saa tha sinn, the' saed tae yin anither, ‘Thïs ïs tha boy wull tak ower whan hïs da dees. Cum on noo, an we'll dae hïm ïn, an whutiver hïs da wus fer leain hïm wull cum tae us!’  Sae the' tuk houl o hïm an throwed hïm oot o tha vineyaird an püt hïm tae deith.” “Weel noo,” saed Jesus, “whaniver tha laird o tha vineyaird cums, whut wull he dae tae thaim fairmers?” “He wull brïng thaim wïckit fairmers tae a tarrible enn,” the' answert, “an he'll set tha vineyaird tae ithers, that wull gie hïm hïs share o tha crap at hairvest time.” Jesus axt thaim, “Hae yis niver read ïn tha Scrïptures: ‘Tha verie stane tha masons turnt doon ïs noo tha coarner stane. Tha Loard hissel haes wrocht thïs, An a wunnèrfu sicht ït ïs!’ Sae A tell ye that tha Kïngdom o God wull be tuk awa frae ye an be gien tae a nation that wull produce tha fruit ït shud.  [Hïm that faas ower thïs stane wull be smesht tae bïts, an whaiver ït faas on wull be grun tae poodèr.]” Whan tha heid preeshts an tha Pharisees heerd Jesus' parables, the' knowed richtlie he wus gettin at thaim.  The' lukt fer a wye tae hae hïm arrestit, but the' wur feart o tha thrang, acause tha fowk tuk hïm fer a proaphit. Jesus spauk tae thaim agane ïn parables, sayin,  “Tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïs laik a kïng that got a waddin pairtie readie fer hïs sinn.  He sent hïs sarvints tae tha yins that wus axt tae tha pairtie tae tell thaim tae cum - but the' wudnae cum.  Wi that he sent some mair sarvints. ‘Tell thaim that haes bin axt,’ he saed, ‘that tha spreed's aa readie. Ma oxen an ma best fattened kwye haes bin kïllt, an iveriethin ïs readie. The'ir tae cum on aheid tae tha waddin!’  But agane the' pyed nae heed an the' gan aff - tha yin tae hïs fairm, an tha ither tae hïs bïzness.  An thair wus ithers tuk houl o hïs sarvints, traitit thaim wile baad an püt thaim tae deith.  Tha kïng wus ragein. He sent oot hïs sodgers fer tae desthroy thaim murdèrers an he brunt thair cïtie doon.  Then he saed tae hïs sarvints, ‘Tha waddin pairtie ïs readie, but tha yins A axt dïdnae desarve tae cum.  Gang tae tha cross-róads an ax oniebodie ye fin tae cum tae tha waddin!’  Sae tha sarvints gan oot ïntae tha raas an the' gethert aa tha fowk the' cud fin, baith saint an sïnner, til tha waddin haal wus fu o guests. But whaniver tha kïng cum ïn tae see tha guests, he saa a bodie thair that haednae waddin claes on hïm.  ‘Freen,’ he axt, ‘hoo dïd ye git ïn here wi'oot claes fït fer a waddin?’ Tha man haed naethin tae say.  Then tha kïng toul hïs sarvints, ‘Bine hïm han an fit, an clod hïm oot ïntae tha dairk, whar thair wull be greetin an scringein o teeth.’  Fer a hale lock o fowk ïs axt, but thair's no monie pïckt oot.” Then tha Pharisees gaed oot an collogued thegither as tae hoo the' cud ketch Jesus oot ïn sumthin he wud say.  An sae the' sent thair ain follaers tae hïm alang wi some men o Herod's pairtie. “Maistèr,” the' saed, “we ken ye spake tha truith, an that ye taich fowk tha wye o God accoardin tae tha truith, wioot onie thocht o whut ither fowk thïnks o ye. Ye dïnnae mak o yin mair ner tha ither.  Sae tell iz, whut's yer thïnkin? Is ït richt tae pye texes tae Caesar or no?”  But Jesus kent thair wïckit mines, an he saed, “Ye hippycrates, fer why ir ye tryin tae ketch me oot?  Show me tha coin ye pye tha tex wi.” The' brocht hïm a denarius ,  an he axt thaim, “Whase name an laikness ïs on ït?”  “It's Caesar's,” the' saed. Then he saed tae thaim, “Sae gie Caesar whut belangs tae Caesar, an gie God whut belangs tae God.”  Whaniver the' heerd thïs, the' wur dumfoonèrt. Sae the' left hïm an gan awa. That same day tha Sadducees, that say thair ïsnae onie risin frae tha deid, the' cum an pit a question tae Jesus.  “Maistèr,” the' saed, “Moses toul iz that ïf a man dees wi'oot leain onie weans, hïs brither maun merrie tha weeda an hae childèr fer hïm.  Noo supposin thair wus seiven brithers amang iz. Tha oulest gets merriet an he dees, an seein thair wur nae weans, hïs wife wus left tae hïs brither.  Tha same thïng happent tae tha saicont brither an tha thurd, richt on doon tae tha seiventh.  An bye an bye, tha wumman she deed as weel.  Noo then, at tha risin frae tha deid, whase guidwife wull she be o tha seiven, seein she wus merriet tae thaim aa?” Jesus answert, “Ye ir no richt ava, fer ye dïnnae ken tha Scrïptures an ye dïnnae ken tha pooer o God!  At tha risin frae tha deid, thair wull be nae mair merryin; fer whaniver the' dee, fowk wull be laik tha angels [o God] ïn heiven.  But consarnin tha risin frae tha deid, dae yis no mine readin whut God saed tae ye:  ‘A be tha God o Abraham, tha God o Isaac, an tha God o Jacob’? He's no tha God o tha deid; he's tha God o tha leevin.”  Whaniver tha croods heerd thïs, the' wur stoondit at hïs taichin. Hearin that Jesus haed left tha Sadducees wi naethin tae say, tha Pharisees got thegither.  An yin o thaim, a thortie on tha Laa, tried tae ketch hïm oot wi thïs question:  “Maistèr, whut's tha maist impoartin commaun ïn tha Laa?”  Jesus saed, “ ‘Ye maun love tha Loard yer God wi aa yer hairt an wi aa yer sowl an wi aa yer mine.’  Thïs ïs tha furst an tha maist impoartin commaun.  An tha saicont yin ïs laik ït: ‘Ye maun love yer nighber jist as much as yersel.’  Tha hale o tha Laa an tha Proaphits hing on these twa commauns.” Noo whaniver tha Pharisees wus gethert roon hïm thair, Jesus axt thaim,  “Whut dae ye thïnk aboot tha Messiah ? Whase sinn ïs he?” “Tha sinn o Davit,” the' answert.  He saed tae thaim, “Then hoo ïs ït that Davit, spakin bi tha Spïrit, caas hïm ‘Loard’? Fer he says, ‘Tha Loard saed tae ma Loard: Sït doon at ma richt han, tae A pit yer enemies unnèr yer feet.’ Sae ïf Davit caas tha Messiah ‘ma Loard’, hoo can he be hïs sinn as weel?”  An naebodie haed a wurd tae say bak tae hïm, an frae that day on naebodie wud dar ax hïm onie mair questions. Then Jesus saed tae tha croods an tae hïs follaers,  “Tha maistèrs o tha Laa an tha Pharisees sïts ïn Moses' sait.  Sae ye maun obey thaim an dae iveriethin the' tell ye. But dïnnae dae tha same as thaim, fer the' dïnnae prectis whut the' praich.  The' tye up heavie burdens ower-wechtie tae cairt, an the' pit thaim on fowks' shoodèrs, but they thairsels ir no wullin tae lïft a fïng'r tae halp thaim.  Iveriethin the' dae ïs daen fer men tae see: the' mak thair phylacteries  extrae wide an tha taussels on thair clokes extrae lang;  the' love tae be at tha tap table at faists, an tae hae tha best saits ïn tha Meetin Hooses;  the' laik men tae touch thair keps tae thaim ïn tha mairket places, an tae caa thaim ‘Rabbi’. But yous ir tae let naebodie caa you ‘Rabbi,’ fer yis hae onlie tha yin Maistèr an yis ir aa brithers.  An dïnnae caa oniebodie on irth ‘Faither,’ fer yis hae onlie tha yin Faither, an he ïs ïn heiven.  Nether let oniebodie caa ye ‘Leader’, fer yis hae onlie tha yin Leader, an that's Christ.  Tha maist impoartin amang ye maun be yer sarvint.  Fer whaiver sets hissel up wull be brocht doon a peg, an whaiver hummles hissel wull be hel ïn heich regaird. Wae faa ye, maistèrs o tha Laa an Pharisees, ye hippycrates! Fer ye shut tha dure o tha Kïngdom o Heiven ïn fowks' faces. You yersels dïnnae enter, an yis'll no alloo thaim tae enter that's tryin tae git ïn!  [Wae faa ye, maistèrs o tha Laa an Pharisees, ye hippycrates! Fer ye swallae up weedas' hooses an ye mak lang prayers fer a show; sae yis'll be condemned aa tha mair.]  Wae faa ye, maistèrs o tha Laa an Pharisees, ye hippycrates! Fer ye trevel ower lan an sea tae git a sing'l convert, an whaniver he cums roon tae yer wye o thïnkin, ye mak hïm twice as much a sinn o hell as yis ir yersels. Wae faa ye, blin guides! Ye say, ‘If oniebodie sweers bi tha Hoose o God, ït mains naethin; but ïf oniebodie sweers bi tha gowld o tha Hoose o God, he'll be hel tae hïs oath.’  Ye blin coofs ye! Whut's mair impoartin: tha gowld, or tha Hoose o God that maks tha gowld halie?  Ye say as weel, ‘If oniebodie sweers bi tha althar, ït mains naethin; but ïf oniebodie sweers bi tha gift on ït, he ïs bun bi hïs oath.’  Ye blin men! Whut's mair impoartin: tha gift, or tha althar that maks tha gift halie?  Sae, tha yin that sweers bi tha althar sweers bi ït, ay, an bi iveriethin on ït as weel.  An hïm that sweers bi tha Hoose o God sweers bi ït, an bi tha Yin that leeves ïn ït.  An tha yin that sweers bi heiven sweers bi God's throne, an bi tha Yin that sïts on tha throne. Wae faa ye, maistèrs o tha Laa an Pharisees, ye hippycrates! Ye gie a tenth o yer gairden spices - yer mint, dill an cummin. But yis hae neglectit tha mair impoartin mettèrs o tha Laa - justice, mercie an faith. Gie yer tenth, but dïnnae ferget tae be fair an kine tae ithers, as weel.  Ye blin guides! Ye strain oot a mïdge, but ye swallae a kemel. Wae faa ye, maistèrs o tha Laa an Pharisees, ye hippycrates! Ye waash tha ootside o tha bickers an tha plates, but tha inside o thaim's fu o whut ye got bi yer plunnerin an greed.  Blin Pharisee! Furst clain tha inside o tha bicker [an tha plate], an then tha ootside wull be clain as weel. Wae faa ye, maistèrs o tha Laa an Pharisees, ye hippycrates! Ye ir laik white-waashed graves, that luk quare an nice on tha ootside but on tha inside the'r fu o deid men's banes an iveriethin that's no clain.  In tha same wye, on tha ootside fowk wud thïnk ye wur guid leevin, but on tha inside ye'r fu o hypocrisie an wïckitness. Wae faa ye, maistèrs o tha Laa an Pharisees, ye hippycrates! Fer yis big tombs fer tha proaphits an fancie monuments fer guid men o lang syne.  An ye say, ‘If we haed hae leeved ïn tha days o oor forefaithers, we wudnae hae bin pairtie tae sheddin tha bluid o tha proaphits.’  In sayin that, ye'r wutnesses agin yersels. Ye'r bred frae thaim that murdèred tha proaphits, sae ye ir.  Gang aheid, feenish aff whut yer forefaithers begun!  Ye snakes! Ye shooer o vipers! Hoo wull ye escape bein condemned tae hell?  Sae A'm gaun tae senn ye proaphits, an wise men, an taichers. Some o thaim ye'll kïll an hing on a cross; ithers ye'll whup ïn yer Meetin Hooses an ye'll hunt thaim frae toon tae toon.  Acause o thïs, on your heids wull faa tha bluid o aa tha upricht fowk that haes iver bin spïllt on tha irth, frae tha kïllin o that guid man Abel tae tha kïllin o Zechariah sinn o Barachiah - hïm that ye murdèred ïn tha Hoose o God atween tha Halie o Halies an tha althar.  A tell ye tha truith, tha judgemen fer aa thïs wull faa doon on thïs verie genèration. O Jerusalem, Jerusalem, you that kïll tha proaphits an stane thaim that's sent tae ye, monies tha time A wantit tae gether yer weans thegither, laik a hen gethers hir lachter o wee burds unnèr hir wïngs, but yis wudnae let me!  Luk, yer Hoose haes bin forsook, an noo ït's empie.  Fer A tell ye thïs, ye'll no see me agane til ye say, ‘Blisst ïs tha Yin that cums ïn tha name o tha Loard!’ ” As Jesus wus waakin awa frae tha Temple gruns, hïs follaers cum up an saed tae hïm, “Wud ye jist luk at thaim biggins!”  “Dae ye see aa these thïngs?” he axt thaim. “A'm tellin ye, no yin stane here wull be left abain tha ither; the'll aa be tummelt doon!” An latèr on, as Jesus wus sïttin on tha Moont o Olives, tha follaers cum tae hïm on hïs lane. “Tell iz,” the' saed, “whan wull aa thïs cum aboot, an whut wull be tha sign o yer cumin, an o tha enn o tha age?”  Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “Tak heed an dïnnae let oniebodie lead yis aglee.  Fer monies a yin wull cum ïn ma name, sayin, ‘A be tha Christ’, an the'll lead monie fowk aglee.  Ye wull hear tell o wars an o taak aboot wars, but dïnnae be püt aboot. Fer sitch thïngs maun happen, but tha enn ïs no near jist yit.  Nations wull mak war on ither nations, an kïngdoms wull rise up agin ither kïngdoms. Thair wull be dirths, [plagues] an irthquakes ïn monie pairts.  Aa thïs ïs onlie tha stairt o tha bairin pains cumin on. Then ye'll be hannit ower tae be persecutit an püt tae deith, an ye'll be haitit bi aa nations jist fer bein ma follaers.  At that time a hale lock o fowk wull turn awa frae tha faith, an the'll bethray an hait yin anither.  A hale lock o fauss proaphits wull rise up an lead monies a yin asthray;  an acause wïckitness wull be on tha up, tha love o maist fowk wull growe coul,  but tha yin that tholes tae tha enn wull be saved.  An tha Guid News o tha Kïngdom wull be praicht ïn tha hale warl as a wutness tae aa tha nations, an then tha enn wull cum. Sae whaniver ye see ‘tha abomination o desolation’ stannin ïn tha halie place - tha abomination tha proaphit Daniel spauk aboot,” (Reader, ye'll unnèrstan ma mainin here) “then thaim at's ïn Judea maun tak tae tha hïlls.  Naebodie that's on hïs ruiftap  shud gae doon tae tak oniethin oot o tha hoose.  An naebodie that's awa oot ïn hïs fiel shud be gaun bak fer hïs cóat.  In thaim days ït'll be tarrible fer weemen that's expectin, an fer mithers wi weans at tha breesht!  Pray tae God that ye dïnnae hae tae flee ïn tha wuntèr or on tha Sabbath.  Fer then thair'll be sitch despert sufferin - faur waur ner thair iver wus frae tha stairt o tha warl til noo - an tha laik o thïs'll niver be saen agane.  If thaim days wurnae shoartent, thair wud be naebodie left; but fer tha sake o tha chosen yins, thaim days wull be shoartent.  At that time ïf oniebodie says tae ye, ‘Luk, here ïs tha Messiah!’ or, ‘Thair he ïs!’ dïnnae tak onie heed.  Fer fauss messiahs an fauss proaphits wull rise up an dae michtie signs an wunnèrs; an fowk wull be tuk ïn bi thaim, ay, an ïf the'r able, the' wull fool even tha chosen yins as weel.  Luk, A hae toul ye aforehan, sae as ye'll know.  Sae then ïf oniebodie tells ye, ‘Thair he ïs, oot ïn tha wuldèrness,’ dïnnae gae oot; or, ‘He's hidin here ïn tha hoose,’ dïnnae believe ït.  Fer jist as tha lichtnin fleshes ower tha lïft, frae tha East tae tha Wast, that's whut tha cumin o tha Sinn o Man wull be laik.  Whariver ye see a crood o vultèrs, ye know thair's a deid bodie thair. Al at yinst eftèr tha sufferin o thaim days, ‘tha sin wull be dairkint, tha muin wull no gie onie licht; tha starns wull faa frae tha heivens, an tha pooers o tha lïft wull be dinnelt.’ An then, tha sign o tha Sinn o Man wull appear ïn tha heivens abain, an aa tha nations o tha irth wull murn. The'll see tha Sinn o Man cumin on tha cloods o heiven, wi pooer an muckle glorie.  He'll senn hïs angels oot wi a lood caa o tha trumpet, an the'll gether hïs chosen yins frae tha fower wuns, frae tha yin enn o heiven tae tha tither. Noo, lairn thïs lesson frae tha fïg tree. As shuin as ïts brenches stairts tae bud, an ïts leafs cum oot, ye ken tha simmer ïs no faur aff.  In tha same wye, whaniver ye see aa these thïngs, ye'll ken tha time ïs nearhan, ay, richt at tha verie dure.  A tell ye tha truith, thair's fowks leevin noo that'll no dee, afore aa these thïngs haes cum aboot!  Heiven an irth wull pass awa, but ma wurds wull niver pass awa. Hooaniver, naebodie knows tha day an tha oor o aa thïs, no even tha angels ïn heiven, ner tha Sinn; tha Faither alane kens ït.  Whaniver tha Sinn o Man cums bak, ït'll be jist laik ït wus ïn Noah's day.  Fer ïn tha days afore tha Flood, fowk wus aitin an drïnkin an gettin merriet, richt up tae tha verie day Noah went ïntae tha airk;  an the' kent naethin aboot whut wud happen, til tha Flood cum an tuk thaim al awa. An that's whut ït'll be laik, whaniver tha Sinn o Man cums bak.  Twa men wull be at wark ïn tha fiel; yin wull be tuk an tha ither left behin.  Twa weemen wull be grindin mail; yin wull be tuk an tha ither left behin.  Sae yous keep watchin tae, fer yis dïnnae ken whut day yer Loard's cumin.  Ye can be shair o thïs: ïf ye haed a hoose, an ye knowed whut oor o tha nicht a thief wus cumin, ye'd be watchin fer hïm, wud ye no? An ye wudnae alloo yer hoose tae be brauk ïntae.  Sae yous maun be readie tae, fer ye dïnnae ken tha oor tha Sinn o Man wull cum. Wha ïs a sarvint ye'd caa faithfu an wise? Is ït no tha yin that tha maistèr haes püt ïn chairge o tha ither sarvints ïn hïs hoose, tae gie thaim thair fair share o mait at tha richt time?  Whaniver hïs maistèr cums bak, onie sarvint ectin laik thïs wull be a happie man.  A tell ye tha truith, he'll pit that sarvint ïn chairge o iveriethin he haes.  But jist say that sarvint ïs wïckit an says tae hissel, ‘He's a lang time o cumin, tha maistèr,’  an he stairts tae bate up hïs fella sarvints an tae ait an collogue wi thaim that's fand o tha drïnk;  Weel, tha maistèr o that sarvint wull cum bak on a day an oor whan tha sarvint ïsnae lukkin oot fer hïm.  An tha maistèr wull dae awa wi hïm an pit hïm alang wi tha hippycrates ; ye can be shair that whar they wull be, thair'll be greetin an scringein o teeth!” “Then tha Kïngdom o Heiven wull be laik ten lasses that tuk thair lamps an gaed oot fer tae meet tha bridegruim.  Five o thaim wus wutless, an five o thaim wus wise.  Tha yins wi nae wut tuk thair lamps but dïdnae tak eneuch oiyle alang wi thaim.  Tha wise yins but, they tuk jars o oiyle alang wi thair lamps.  Tha bridegruim wus a lang time cumin, an the' aa becum that sleepie the' drapt aff.  At mïdnicht tha cry rung oot: ‘Here's tha bridegruim! Cum on oot an meet hïm!’  Then aa tha lasses waakent up an the' trïmmed thair lamps.  Tha yins wi nae wut saed tae tha wise yins, ‘Oor lamps ïs gaun oot! Gie iz a drap o yer oiyle.’  ‘Na,’ the' answert, ‘fer mebbe thair'll no be eneuch fer iz aa. Awa tae thaim that sells tha oiyle an buy some fer yersels!’  But while the' wur on thair wye fer tae buy tha oiyle, here dïdnae tha bridegruim turn up! Tha lasses that haed made readie gaed wi hïm ïntae tha waddin pairtie. An tha dure wus shut.  Eftèr a while tha ither lasses cum bak. ‘Sïr! Sïr!’ the' saed. ‘Wull ye no apen tha dure tae iz?’  But he answert, ‘A tell ye tha truith, A know naethin aboot ye!’ ”  An Jesus warnt thaim, “Ye'r tae watch oot, al o yis, fer ye dïnnae ken tha day or tha oor A'll be bak.” “Agane, tha Kïngdom o Heiven wull be laik a man gaun aff on hïs trevels, wha caad hïs sarvints thegither an pit thaim ïn chairge o aa he haed.  Tae tha yin he gien five baags  o siller, tae anither twa baags, an tae anither jist tha yin baag, accoardin tae whut he knowed the' cud dae wi ït. Then aff he went on hïs thrip.  Strecht awa, tha sarvint that got tha five baags begun tae püt hïs siller tae wark, an he got bak five mair.  An tha yin wi tha twa baags got twa mair bak as weel.  But hïm that haed bin gien jist tha yin baag, he gaed aff, dïgged a hole ïn tha grun an hïd hïs maistèr's siller. Noo eftèr a lang time tha maistèr o thaim sarvints cum bak an axt thaim tae gie an accoont o whut the'd daen wi hïs siller.  Tha man that haed bin gien tha five baags cum forrit, an brocht wi hïm tha ither five. ‘Maistèr,’ he saed, ‘ye hannit ower five baags tae me. Luk, A hae got five mair fer ye.’  Hïs maistèr saed, ‘Ye hae daen weel, ye guid an faithfu sarvint! Ye hae showed A can trust ye wi wee thïngs, sae A'll pit ye ïn chairge o a hale lock mair. Cum alang wi me, an share yer maistèr's happiness!’  Tha man wi tha twa baags o siller cum forrit as weel an he saed, ‘Maistèr, ye hannit ower twa baags tae me. Luk see, A hae got twa mair fer ye.’  Hïs maistèr saed, ‘Ye hae daen weel, ye guid an faithfu sarvint! Ye hae showed A can trust ye wi wee thïngs, sae A'll pit ye ïn chairge o a hale lock mair. Cum alang wi me, an share yer maistèr's happiness!’  Then alang cum tha man that wus gien tha yin baag o siller. ‘Maistèr,’ he saed, ‘A kent ye wur a haird man; ye hairvest whar ye hinnae plantit an ye gether whar ye hinnae sowed.  Sae A wus feart an gaed oot an hïd yer siller ïn tha grun. Luk, here's whut belangs tae ye.’  Hïs maistèr saed, ‘Ye uisless guid-fer-naethin! Sae ye thocht, dïd ye, that A hairvest whar A hinnae plantit an A gether whar A hinnae sowed?  Weel then, ye shud hae püt ma siller ïn tha bank, sae A wud hae got ït bak wi ïntrèst whaniver A cum bak!  Tak tha baag awa frae hïm,’ he oardèrt, ‘an gie ït tae tha yin that haes tha ten.  Fer iverie yin that haes wull be gien mair, an he'll hae mair ner eneuch. An whaiver haes lïttle or naethin, even tha wee bït he haes wull be taen awa frae hïm!  Noo, jist cast that guid fer naethin sarvint oot ïntae tha dairk, whar thair wull be greetin an scringein o teeth.’ ” An Jesus went on tae say thïs, “Whaniver tha Sinn o Man cums ïn hïs glorie, an aa tha angels alang wi hïm, he'll sït on hïs throne ïn heivenlie glorie.  Afore hïm aa tha nations wull be gethert thegither, an he'll set apairt tha fowk yin frae tha ither, jist laik a shepherd sets apairt tha sheep frae tha gaits.  He wull pit tha sheep on hïs richt han an tha gaits on hïs left.  Then tha Kïng wull say tae tha yins on hïs richt han, ‘Cum, yous that ir blisst bi ma Faither; tak houl o yer inheritance, tha Kïngdom makkit readie fer ye frae tha time tha warl begun.  Fer A wus hung'rie an ye fed me; A haed a druith on me, an ye gien me sumthin tae drïnk; A wus an ootsider an ye tuk me ïn;  A haednae a dud o claes tae ma bak, an ye gien me some; A wus seeck an ye lukt eftèr me; A wus ïn jail an ye cum an vïsitit me.’  Then tha righteous fowk wull say bak tae hïm, ‘Loard, whan wus ït we saa ye hung'rie an gien ye mait, or wi a druith on ye, an gien ye a drïnk?  Whan wus ït we saa ye an ootsider an tuk ye ïn, or wioot a dud an we gien ye some claes?  Whan dïd we see ye seeck or ïn jail, an went an vïsitit ye?’  Tha Kïng wull answer, ‘A tell ye tha truith, whutiver ye daen fer yin o tha laist impoartin o these brithers o mine, ye daen ït fer me.’  An then he'll say tae tha yins on hïs left han, ‘Awa wi ye, yous that ir curst, awa ïntae tha iverlastin fire that's readie an waitin fer tha Deil an hïs angels!  Fer A wus hung'rie an yis gien me naethin tae ait; A haed a druith on me, an yis gien me naethin tae drïnk;  A wus a ootsider an yis dïdnae tak me ïn; A haednae a dud an yis dïdnae gie me onie; A wus seeck an ïn jail an yis dïdnae luk eftèr me.’  An thaim yins wull say as weel, ‘Loard, whan dïd we see ye hung'rie or wi a druith, or an ootsider, or needin claes, or seeck or ïn jail, an we dïd naethin tae halp ye?’  An he'll repone, ‘A tell ye tha truith, whutiver yis dïdnae dae fer yin o tha laist impoartin o these brithers o mine, yis dïdnae dae ït fer me.’  Then awa the'll gae ïntae iverlastin punishment, but fer tha righteous fowk ït'll be ïntae iverlastin life.” Whaniver Jesus haed daen sayin aa these thïngs, he saed tae hïs follaers,  “Ye ken tha Passower ïs tha day eftèr themorra, an tha Sinn o Man wull be hannit ower fer tae be nailt tae a cross.” Then tha heid preeshts an tha eldèrs o tha fowk gethert thegither ïn tha palace o tha Heich Preesht, a man bi tha name o Caiaphas,  an the' cumpluthèrt fer tae git tha houl o Jesus bi some sleekit wye, an pit hïm tae deith.  “But no whan tha Faist's on,” the' saed, “or we'll hae a garevitch on oor hans!” Aa tha while, Jesus wus ïn Bethanie ïn tha hoose o Simon tha Leper,  an a wumman cum up tae hïm wi a wee crock o scent - perfume that wus wile dear - that she poored ower hïs heid as he wus restin at tha boord.  But whaniver tha follaers saen thïs, the' wur wile ang'rie. “Why thïs waste?” the' axt.  “Thïs perfume cud hae bin soul fer a bïg price, an tha siller gien tae tha puir.”  Knowin weel whut the' wur sayin, Jesus saed tae thaim, “Dïnnae bother tha wumman! Thïs ïs a guid thïng she haes daen fer me.  Fer ye'll aye hae tha puir wi yis, but ye'll no aye hae me.  Whaniver she poored thïs perfume on ma bodie, she daen ït fer tae mak me readie fer ma buryin.  A'm tellin ye tha truith, whariver ïn tha hale warl thïs Guid News ïs praicht, hir storie wull be toul sae as she'll niver be fergot.” Then yin o tha Twal - tha yin caad Judas Iscariot - went tae tha heid preeshts  an he axt thaim, “Whut ir yis wullin tae gie me ïf A han Jesus ower tae yis?” Sae the' settelt fer thurtie siller coins.  Frae then on Judas wus lukkin fer a chaunce tae han hïm ower. On tha furst day o tha Faist o Bairmless Breid, tha follaers cum tae Jesus an axt hïm, “Whar dae ye want iz tae mak tha Passower mail readie fer ye?”  He saed, “Gang ïntae tha cïtie, an ye'll see thïs man. Tell hïm, ‘Tha Maistèr says, Ma time ïs nearhan, an A'm gaun tae celebrate tha Passower wi ma follaers at yer hoose.’ ”  Sae hïs follaers daen jist as Jesus haed bïd thaim, an the' made readie tha boord fer tha Passower mail. Whan tha evenin wus weel on, Jesus wus at tha boord alang wi tha Twal.  An while the' wur aitin, he saed, “A tell ye tha truith, yin o yis ïs fer bethrayin me.”  The' wur aa fu o sorra whaniver the' heerd thïs, an yin eftèr tha ither stairtit tae say tae hïm, “Shairlie ït's no me ye main, Loard?”  Jesus saed, “Thair's yin that's dïppt hïs han ïn tha boul wi me wull bethray me.  Tha Sinn o Man maun follae tha róad tha Scrïptures foretoul lang syne. But wile sorra tae tha yin that bethrays hïm! It wud be faur bettèr fer that man ïf he haed niver bin boarn.”  Then Judas, tha yin that wus gaun tae bethray hïm, saed, “Shairlie ït's no me ye main, Rabbi?” Jesus answert hïm, “It's you haes saed ït.” While the' wur aitin, Jesus tuk breid ïn hïs hans, an whaniver he haed gien thenks tae God, he brauk ït, an hannit ït tae hïs follaers, sayin, “Tak thïs an ait ït; thïs ïs ma bodie.”  Then he tuk a bicker o wine, he gien thenks tae God fer ït, an he hannit ït roon, sayin, “Al o yis drïnk frae thïs.  Thïs ïs ma bluid; ït's a sign o God's new coveynant, an ït's poored oot tae forgie monie thair wrangdaeins.  A tell ye, A'll no drïnk o thïs fruit o tha vine agane, na, no til tha day A drïnk a new wine alang wi you ïn ma Faither's Kïngdom.” Wi that, the' sung tha Passower psaum, an the' went oot on tae tha Moont o Olives.  An then Jesus toul thaim, “Thïs verie nicht al o yis wull faa awa on accoont o me, fer as ït's writ: ‘A wull strike tha shepherd, an tha sheep o tha flock wull be scattèrt.’  But eftèr A hae ris frae tha deid, A'll tak tha foreróad o ye ïntae Galilee.”  An Petèr spauk oot, “Tha mair tha rest'll faa awa becas o ye, A niver wull!”  “A tell ye tha truith,” Jesus saed bak, “thïs verie nicht, afore tha roostèr craas, ye'll say thrie times ower that ye dïnnae ken me.”  But Petèr spauk oot agane, “E'en ïf A hae tae dee alang wi ye, A wull niver deny ye!” An aa tha ither follaers vood tha same. Then Jesus gaed wi hïs follaers tae a place caad Gethsemane, an he toul thaim, “Sït here while A gang ower thair an pray.”  He tuk Petèr an tha twa sinns o Zebedee alang wi hïm, an he begun tae be wile sorrafu an gye troublet.  Then he saed tae thaim, “Ma hairt's brekkin wi ang'uish, near tae deith. Yous bide here an stye awaak wi me.”  He gan forrit a weethin, then he bood doon wi hïs face tae tha grun an he prayed, “Ma Faither, ïf ït ïs poassible, may thïs cup o sufferin be tuk awa frae me. Yit ït's your wull A'm wantin, an no ma ain.”  Then he cum bak tae hïs follaers an he fun thaim sleepin. “Cud you men no keep watch fer yin oor wi me?” he axt Petèr.  “Watch an pray sae ye dïnnae gie ïn tae temptation. Tha spïrit's wullin, but tha bodie's waik.”  He went awa a saicont time an he prayed, “O ma Faither, ïf thair's naethin else fer ït, an ïf A hae tae drïnk thïs cup o sufferin, may your wull be daen.”  An whaniver he cum bak, yinst mair he fun thaim sleepin, fer the' cudnae keep thair een apen.  Sae he left thaim, an he gan awa agane an prayed tha thurd time, sayin tha same thïng.  Then he cum bak tae hïs follaers an he saed tae thaim, “Ir yis still sleepin an takkin yer rest? But luk here - tha time haes cum. Tha Sinn o Man ïs bethrayed ïntae tha hans o wrangdaers.  Git up noo, an we'll be aff! Luk, ma bethrayer's here!” Tha wurds wus harlie oot o hïs mooth, whan up cum Judas, yin o tha Twal. Alang wi hïm wus a bïg thrang airmed wi swords an stavs, sent oot frae tha heid preeshts an tha eldèrs o tha fowk.  Noo tha bethrayer haed warkt oot a sign wi thaim: “Tha yin A kïss ïs tha man ye'r lukkin; tak tha houl o hïm.”  Sae Judas gaed strecht up tae Jesus, an he saed, “Greetins, Rabbi!” an he kïsst hïm.  Jesus saed, “Freen, dae whut ye cum here fer.” Then tha men cum forrit, the' tuk houl o Jesus an arrestit hïm.  Wi that, yin o tha men wi Jesus raxt fer hïs sword, he pu'ed ït oot an hut tha sarvint o tha Heich Preesht, an he sneddit aff hïs lug.  “Pit yer sword awa,” Jesus saed tae hïm, “fer aa that draas tha sword wull dee bi tha sword.  Dae ye no ken that ïf A wantit tae, A cud caa on ma Faither, an he wud senn thoosans  o angels tae halp me?  But hoo then wud tha Scrïptures be fülfilled that say ït maun cum aboot tha wye we'r seein noo?”  At that time Jesus saed tae tha crood, “Am A some soart o a reiver, that yis hae cum oot agin me wi swords an stavs fer tae tak me? Shair A sut ïn tha Hoose o God iverie day taichin, an yis niver layed a han on me!  But thïs haes aa tuk place sae that whut wus writ bi tha proaphits micht cum aboot.” Then aa hïs follaers left hïm an run awa. Tha yins that haed lïftit Jesus tuk hïm awa tae Caiaphas, tha Heich Preesht, whar tha maistèrs o tha Laa an tha eldèrs o tha fowk haed gethert thegither.  But Petèr follaed hïm a brave wye behin, richt up tae tha coortyaird o tha Heich Preesht. He went ïntae ït an sut doon wi tha gairds tae see whut wud happen.  Noo tha heid preeshts an tha hale Cooncil wus lukkin fer men that wud wutness agin Jesus, sae the' cud pit hïm tae deith.  But the' dïdnae fin onie wi stories that wud dae, tha mair monie fauss wutnesses spauk oot. Bye an bye twa steppit forrit,  sayin, “Thïs fella saed, ‘A be able tae desthroy tha Hoose o God an big ït up agane ïn thrie days.’ ”  Then tha Heich Preesht ris tae hïs feet an saed tae Jesus, “Hae ye nae answer tae these chairges? Whut hae ye tae say fer yersel?”  But Jesus hel hïs tung. An tha Heich Preesht saed tae hïm, “A chairge ye unnèr oath bi tha leevin God - tell iz ïf ye ir tha Christ, tha Sinn o God.”  “It's as ye say,” Jesus answert. “But A'm tellin yis aa, that In a day tae cum yis'll see tha Sinn o Man sïttin at tha richt han o tha Michtie Yin, an cumin on tha cloods o heiven.”  Then tha Heich Preesht tore hïs claes an saed, “He haes spauk blesphemie! Whut dae we need onie mair wutnesses fer? Luk noo, ye hae aa heerd hïs blesphemie fer yersels.  Whut dae ye thïnk?” “He desarves tae be püt tae deith!” the' answert.  Then the' sput ïn hïs face an hut hïm wi thair fïsts. Ithers hut hïm wi tha flet o thair hans  an the' saed, “Weel, Messiah, tell iz wha skelpt ye!” Noo Petèr wus sïttin oot ïn tha coortyaird, an thïs wee sarvin lass cum up til hïm. “You wur wi Jesus o Galilee as weel,” she saed.  But he denied ït afore thaim aa. “A dïnnae ken whut ye'r taakin aboot,” qo he.  Then he slipt oot tae tha gate, whar anither lass saen hïm an saed tae tha fowk stannin roon, “Thïs fella wus alang wi Jesus o Nazareth.”  Yinst mair he denied ït, an wi an oath: “A dïnnae ken tha man!”  Eftèr a wee while, tha yins that wur stannin thair went up tae Petèr an saed, “Shairlie ye maun be yin o thaim, fer tha wye ye taak gies ye awa.”  Then he stairtit cursin an sweerin, an sayin, “A dïnnae ken tha man!” An at that verie mïnit a roostèr craad.  Then Petèr haed mine o tha wurds Jesus haed spauk: “Afore tha roostèr craas, ye'll deny me thrie times.” An he went oot o tha coortyaird, greetin sair. At tha scraich o day, aa tha heid preeshts an tha eldèrs o tha fowk collogued thegither as tae hoo the' wud pit Jesus tae deith.  Sae the' tyed hïm up, the' maircht hïm aff an the' hannit hïm ower tae Pilate, tha Guviner. Noo Judas, that haed bethrayed hïm, whaniver he saa that Jesus wus condemned, he sairlie rued whut he'd daen, an he gien tha thurtie siller coins bak tae tha heid preeshts an tha eldèrs.  “A hae daen wrang,” saed he, “fer A hae bethrayed tha bluid o an innocent man.” “Whut's that tae us?” the' saed. “On yer ain heid be ït!”  Sae Judas throwed tha siller doon ïn tha Hoose o God. Then he gan oot o tha Temple, an he went an hung hissel.  Tha heid preeshts gethert up tha coins an saed, “It ïs agin tha Laa tae pit thïs ïntae tha Temple kïst, seein as ït's tha price o bluid.”  Sae the' agreed amang thairsels tae uise tha siller fer tae buy tha potter's fiel, as a buryin grun fer strangers.  An that's tha raison tae thïs verie day ït's caad “Tha Fiel o Bluid”.  In thïs wye tha wurd spauk bi Jeremiah tha proaphit cum aboot: “The' tuk tha thurtie siller coins, tha amoont pit on hïs heid bi Israel,  an the' uised thaim tae buy tha potter's fiel, jist as tha Loard commaundit.” While aa thïs wus gaun on, Jesus stud afore tha Guviner, an tha Guviner axt hïm, “Ir you tha Kïng o tha Jews?” Jesus answert, “You hae saed ït.”  But whaniver he wus accused bi tha heid preeshts an tha eldèrs, he gien nae answer ava.  Then Pilate axt hïm, “Dae ye no hear whut the'r chairgin ye wi?”  But Jesus niver saed a wurd bak tae hïm regairdin onie o tha chairges agin hïm, an tha Guviner wus stoondit. Noo ït uist tae be at tha Passower Faist, tha Guviner wud aye let a prisner oot o jail: whutiver yin tha fowk axt fer.  An that year the' haed a prisner iveriebodie haed heerd tell o, bi tha name o Barabbas.  Sae whaniver tha crood haed gethert thegither, Pilate axt thaim, “Whutch yin dae yis want me tae let oot tae ye: Barabbas, or Jesus, that ïs caad Christ?”  Fer he knowed richt weel ït wus jist oot o spite the' haed hannit Jesus ower tae hïm.  Noo as Pilate wus sïttin on tha judge's sait, hïs wife sent hïm thïs message: “Hae naethin tae dae wi thon innocent man, fer A'm tellin ye, A'm sair tormentit thïs day bi a draim A haed aboot hïm!”  But tha heid preeshts an tha eldèrs taakt tha crood roon, sae as the' wud ax fer Barabbas an hae Jesus püt tae deith.  “Whutch o tha twa dae yis want me tae let oot tae yis then?” axt tha Guviner. “We want Barabbas!” the' answert.  “Sae whut am A tae dae wi Jesus that's caad tha Christ?” Pilate axt. An the' aa saed bak, “Tae tha cross wi hïm!”  “But whut fer? Whut's he daen wrang?” axt Pilate. But tha thrang jist roared aa tha mair, “Tae tha cross wi hïm!” Whaniver Pilate saen that he wus gettin naewhar, but that he wus aboot tae hae a riot on hïs hans, he got some wattèr an waasht hïs hans afore tha crood o fowk. “A'm no guiltie o thïs man's bluid,” saed he. “On your heids be ït!”  Aa tha fowk saed, “Let hïs bluid be on us an on oor childèr!”  Then he lut Barabbas oot tae thaim. But he got Jesus whuppt, an he hannit hïm ower fer tae be crucyfied. Then tha Guviner's sodgers tuk Jesus ïntae tha Praetorium  an the' gethert tha hale regiment roon hïm.  The' strïpt hïm an püt a scarlet robe on hïm,  an then the' plettit thoarns thegither tae mak a croon, an the' set ït on hïs heid. The' püt a stav ïn hïs richt han an the' got doon on thair knees afore hïm, mockin hïm an sayin, “Lang leeve tha Kïng o tha Jews!”  The' sput on hïm, an the' tuk tha stav an hut hïm ower tha heid agane an agane.  An eftèr the' haed daen mockin hïm, the' tuk tha robe aff hïm, an the' püt hïs ain claes bak on hïm. Then the' tuk hïm awa fer tae crucyfie hïm. An whaniver the' wur on thair wye oot, the' run ïntae a man frae Cyrene, bi tha name o Simon, an the' gart hïm tae cairrie tha cross.  The' cum tae a place caad Golgotha (mainin “Tha Place o tha Skull”).  Thair the' raxt wine up tae Jesus, mixt wi gall; but eftèr tastin ït, he wudnae drïnk onie mair.  Noo whaniver tha sodgers haed nailt hïm tae tha cross, the' gemmelt amang thairsels tae dïvide hïs claes. [Thïs brocht aboot whut tha proaphit saed wud happen: “The' dïvïd ma dishables amang thaim an the' cloddit dice fer ma claes.”] An sïttin doon, the' kep watch ower hïm thair.  Abain hïs heid the' püt up tha chairge agin hïm, that saed: THIS IS JESUS, THA KING O THA JEWS.  Twa robbers wur crucyfied alang wi hïm, yin on hïs richt han side, an tha tither on hïs left.  Thaim at waakt bye yellt abuse at hïm, shakin thair heids,  an sayin, “Hey, you that saed ye wur gaun tae desthroy tha Hoose o God, an big ït agane ïn thrie days - save yersel! If you ir tha Sinn o God, cum doon aff that cross!”  An tha heid preeshts, tha maistèrs o tha Laa an tha eldèrs, the' daen tha same, an the' mockt hïm.  “He saved ithers,” the' saed, “but he cannae save hissel! Is he no tha Kïng o Israel? Then jist let hïm cum doon aff tha cross, an we'll believe ïn hïm!  He trusts ïn God. Let God rescue hïm noo ïf he wants hïm, fer he saed, ‘A be tha Sinn o God.’ ”  Tha robbers that wur crucyfied wi hïm hurlt abuse at hïm as weel. Frae nuin tae thrie ïn tha eftèrnuin , dairkness cum ower tha hale lan.  An roon aboot thrie Jesus caad oot wi a lood voice, “Eli, Eli, lama sabachthani?” - that mains: “O God, ma God, why hae ye forsook me?”  Whaniver some o thaim stannin bye heerd thïs, the' saed, “He's caain oot fer Elijah.”  An richt awa yin o thaim run an got a sponge. He fïllt ït wi soor wine, püt ït on a lang stïck, an raxt ït up tae Jesus fer hïm tae drïnk.  But tha ithers saed, “Jist lea hïm alane. We'll see noo ïf Elijah cums fer tae save hïm.” Then Jesus cryed oot agane wi a lood voice, an he gien up hïs spïrit. At that verie mïnit tha curtin ïn tha Halie o Halies wus tore ïn twa frae tap tae bottom. Tha irth shuk an tha roaks splït.  Tha graves apent, an tha bodies o monie halie fowk that haed deed wur ris tae life.  The' cum oot o thair tombs, an eftèr Jesus wus ris frae tha deid the' went ïntae tha halie cïtie an appeart tae a lock o fowk.  Tha centurion  an thaim alang wi hïm that wus gairdin Jesus, whaniver the' saa tha irthquake an aa that haed happent, the' wur hairt-scarred, an the' saed, “Thair can be nae doot, thïs wus tha Sinn o God!” Noo monie weemen wur thair as weel, stannin awa bak takkin ït aa ïn. The' haed follaed Jesus frae Galilee fer tae luk eftèr hïm.  In amang thaim thair wus Mary Magdalene, an Mary tha mither o Jeames an Joses, an thair wus tha mither o Zebedee's sinns. Whan ït cum evenin, thair wus thïs weel-aff man frae Arimathea, bi tha name o Joseph, wha hissel haed becum a follaer o Jesus.  An he gan tae Pilate, an he axt fer tha bodie o Jesus, an Pilate oardèrt thaim tae gie ït tae hïm.  Joseph tuk tha bodie, an he lapt ït ïn a clain lïnen claith,  an he layed ït ïn hïs ain new tomb he haed cut oot o tha roak. He rowlt a bïg stane agin tha mooth o tha tomb an then he gaed awa.  Mary Magdalene an tha ither Mary wur sïttin thair fornent tha tomb. Tha nixt day, tha yin eftèr tha Day o Preparation, tha heid preeshts an tha Pharisees went tae Pilate.  “Sïr,” the' saed, “whaniver that deceiver wus still leevin, we mine hïm sayin, ‘Eftèr thrie days A wull rise agane.’  Sae wud ye gie tha oardèr fer thaim tae shut that tomb weel tae tha thurd day, less hïs follaers cum an steal tha bodie an tell tha fowk he haes ris frae tha deid. Then that deception wud be waur ner tha furst.”  “Tak gairds wi ye,” saed Pilate. “Awa an shut up tha tomb as weel as ye can.”  Sae the' gaed an made tha tomb safe bi sealin tha stane an leain tha gaird tae keep watch. It wus eftèr tha Sabbath, at daylicht on tha furst day o tha week, an Mary Magdalene an tha ither Mary cum tae luk at tha tomb.  Aa o a suddent, thair wus a michtie irthquake, fer an angel o tha Loard cum doon frae heiven! He gaed tae tha tomb, an he rowlt bak tha stane an he sut on ït.  He wus bricht as lichtnin, an hïs claes wus white as snaa.  Whaniver the' saa hïm, tha gairds at tha tomb shuk wi fear an the' becum laik deid men.  But tha angel saed tae tha weemen, “Dïnnae be feart, fer A ken that ye'r lukkin fer Jesus, that wus crucyfied.  He's no here; he's ris, jist as he saed he wud. Cum an see tha place whar he  wus layed oot.  Quïck! Gae an tell hïs follaers, ‘He haes ris frae tha deid an he's awa on aheid o ye ïntae Galilee. Ye'll see hïm thair.’ Noo mine whut A hae toul ye.”  Sae tha weemen hurriet frae tha tomb; the' wur afeart, yit fu o joy. The' run tae tell hïs follaers,  whan aa o a suddent Jesus appeart fornent thaim. “Fair faa ye!” saed he. An the' went tae hïm, tuk houl o hïs feet an wurshipt hïm.  Then Jesus saed tae thaim, “Dïnnae be feart. Gae an tell ma brithers tae gae ïntae Galilee, an the'll see me thair.” While tha weemen wur on thair wye, some o tha gairds went ïntae tha cïtie an toul tha heid preeshts aa that haed cum aboot.  An whaniver tha heid preeshts haed gethert thegither wi tha eldèrs, the' collogued amang thairsels, an the' gien tha sodgers a bïg amoont o siller,  an the' toul thaim, “Ye'r tae say, ‘Tha follaers o Jesus cum ïn tha nicht an stole hïm awa whan we wur sleepin.’  If tha Guviner hears tell o thïs, we'll taak hïm roon, an keep ye oot o bother.”  Sae tha sodgers tuk tha siller an daen as the' wur toul. An thïs storie haes gan roon amang tha Jews tae thïs verie day. Then tha eleiven follaers gaed tae Galilee, tae tha muntin whar Jesus haed toul thaim.  Whaniver the' saen hïm, the' wurshipt hïm; but some aye haed thair doots.  Then Jesus cum tae thaim an saed, “Aa thortie haes bin gien tae me ïn heiven an on irth.  Sae gang an mak follaers o aa nations, baptisin thaim ïn tha name o tha Faither an o tha Sinn an o tha Halie Spïrit,  taichin thaim tae keep aa tha commauns A hae gien ye. An know thïs: A be wi ye iverie day, ay, tae tha verie enn o time.” Thïs ïs tha stairt o tha Guid Wittins aboot Jesus Christ, tha Sinn o God.  Jist as ït wus writ doon ïn Isaiah tha proaphit: “Lïsten, A'll senn oot ma messenger aheid o ye, an he wull mak readie yer wye fer ye;  thair's a voice cryin oot ïn tha wiles: ‘Mak readie tha wye o tha Loard, mak hïs pads strecht fer hïm!’ ”  An sae ït cum aboot. Tha messenger appeart, an ït wus Jhone tha Baptiser. He leeved oot ïn tha wiles, praichin an tellin tha fowk the' shud be baptised fer tae show the' haed turnt awa frae thair sïns, an tae show the' haed turnt tae God fer hïm tae forgie thaim.  Aa tha fowk frae tha kintrie roon aboot Judea, an aa tha fowk frae tha cïtie o Jerusalem trevelt oot tae hïm on tha muir; an Jhone baptised ïn tha rïver Joardan thaim at confesst thair sïns.  Noo Jhone wore claes made o kemel's hair, wi a leather belt roon hïs mïddle, an he leeved bi aitin gresshoppers an wile honey.  An tha message he gien wus thïs: “Eftèr me, thair wull cum yin that ïs michtier ner me. A am no fït tae lowse hïs buits fer hïm.  A hae baptised yis wi wattèr, but yin wull cum that wull baptise yis wi tha Halie Spïrit.” At thon time, Jesus cum frae Nazareth ïn Galilee, an Jhone baptised hïm ïn tha Joardan.  An whaniver Jesus wus cumin oot o tha wattèr, tha heivens apent up, an tha Spïrit cum doon on hïm laik a doo.  An a voice cum frae tha heivens, sayin, “Ye ir ma sinn, ma hairt's delicht, an A'm weel plaised wi ye.” An at yinst tha Spïrit püt hïm awa ïntae tha wuldèrness.  He wus oot ïn tha wiles fer fowertie days, aa tha time bein tempit bi Satan. He wus surroonded wi wile anymals, an tha angels lukt eftèr hïm. Noo a while latèr, eftèr Jhone wus püt ïntae jail, Jesus cum ïntae Galilee, praichin tha Guid News o God.  “Tha time haes noo cum,” he saed, “an tha Kïngdom o God ïs nearhan. Turn awa frae yer wrangdaeins, an believe tha Guid News!” Yin day, whan Jesus wus waakin alang tha loch shore o Galilee, he saen Simon an hïs brither Andra throwin a neyt ïntae tha wattèr, fer the' wrocht at tha fïshin.  “Cum an follae me,” saed Jesus, “An A wull mak ye ïntae fïshers o men!”  An at yinst the' layed doon thair neyts, an the' follaed eftèr hïm.  Whan he went on a wee bït, he saa Jeames an hïs brither Jhone, tha sinns o Zebedee, ïn a bóat mennin thair neyts.  An at yinst Jesus caad thaim tae, an the' cum awa wi hïm as weel, leain thair faither Zebedee wi tha hired hans on tha bóat. An the' gaed ïntae Capernaum. An whan tha Sabbath day cum roon, he went ïntae tha Meetin Hoose, an begun tae taich.  Tha fowk that heerd hïm wur aa thunnèrstruck wi hïs taichin, fer he taicht thaim laik a bodie wi thortie, an no laik tha maistèrs o tha Laa.  Noo thair wus thïs man ïn thair Meetin Hoose wi an ïll spïrit,  an he scraicht oot lood, “Lea iz alane! Whut dae ye want wi iz, Jesus o Nazareth? Hae ye cum here tae dae awa wi iz? A ken richt weel wha ye ir. Ye ir tha Halie Yin o God.”  But Jesus chackt hïm an saed, “Houl yer wheesht, an cum oot o hïm!”  An tha ïll spïrit made tha man trimmle an shake, then ït gie a scraich, an cum oot o hïm.  The' wur aa thunnèrstruck, an the' axt yin anither, “Whut's thïs noo? Is thïs a new taichin? Fer e'en tha ïll spïrits dae as he tells thaim!”  An afore lang tha hale kintrie roon aboot Galilee wus hotchin wi tha news. An the' left tha Meetin Hoose rael quïck, an the' went alang wi Jeames an Jhone til tha hoose whar Simon an Andra leeved.  Noo Simon's ma-ïn-laa wus doon wi a faivir, an as shuin as Jesus cum ïn, the' toul hïm aboot hir.  Sae he gaed til hir bedside, tuk hir han an puud hir up. Strecht awa she coolt doon an she stairtit tae sarve an luk eftèr thaim. An that evenin, whan tha sin haed set, the' brocht til hïm aa tha seeck, an aa tha yins wi demons.  Tha hale toon wus gethert at tha dure.  An Jesus cured a quare lock o seeck fowk o thair monie ailments, an he driv oot a brave wheen o demons. But he wudnae let tha demons spake oot, fer the' kent wha he wus. Wile earlie tha nixt moarnin, whan ït wus still dairk, Jesus got up an left tha hoose, an went awa tae a place whar he cud be on hïs ain, fer tae pray.  An Simon an tha yins wi hïm went oot tae luk fer hïm.  Whaniver the' fun hïm, the' saed tae hïm, “Iverie yin's lukkin fer ye!”  An Jesus cum bak wi, “Cum on an we'll gang awa frae here tae tha toons roon aboot! A hae tae praich thair as weel, fer that's whut A cum here fer tae dae.”  Sae he trevelt aa roon aboot Galilee, praichin ïn thair Meetin Hooses, an drivin oot demons. An thïs leper cum tae Jesus, got doon on hïs knees, an begged hïm, “If ye hae a mine tae, ye can mak me clain!”  Feelin wile sorrie fer tha man, Jesus püt hïs han oot an toucht hïm, sayin, “A am wullin; ye'r bettèr!”  Richt awa tha leprosie quït hïm, an he wus weel agane.  Sae Jesus sent hïm awa, sayin tae hïm, “A'm warnin ye noo, awa ye gang, but tell naebodie. Jist show yersel tae tha preesht, an gie an offerin fer yer cleansin as Moses telt iz ïn tha Laa, fer a wutness tae yin an aa that ye'r weel agane!”  But insteed, tha man went an toul al roon whut Jesus haed daen fer hïm. Thïs meent that Jesus cudnae be saen gaun ïntae a toon; he haed tae stay oot ïn tha kintrie. But fowk still cum frae aa roon tae see hïm. Eftèr a wheen o days, Jesus cum bak tae Capernaum. An wurd went roon that he wus bak hame.  An monie fowk gethert thegither, an thair wus sitch a thrang, thair wus nae mair ruim, even ootbye tha dure. An Jesus wus praichin tha wurd tae thaim.  Then fower men cum tae tha hoose, cairryin a paralysed man.  An as the' cudnae git near tae Jesus fer tha thrang, the' dïgged a hole ïn tha ruif abain hïm; then the' lut doon tha mat throu tha hole the' haed made, wi thair seeck freen lyin on ït.  An whan Jesus saa whut faith the' haed, he saed tae tha paralysed man, “Ma sinn, yer sïns ïs aa forgien!”  Noo some maistèrs o tha Laa wus sïttin thïnkin thïs ower.  “Hoo cum thïs man dars tae taak laik thïs?” the' thocht. “It's naethin but blesphemie. Wha can forgie sïns but God alane?”  But Jesus knowed thair thochts an cud read thaim laik a buik. He saed tae thaim, “Hoo cum yis ir thïnkin laik thïs?  Is ït aisier tae tell a paralysed man, ‘Yer sïns ïs forgien ye’, or tae tell hïm, ‘Get up an waak, an tak yer mat wi ye’.  But jist sae as ye'll ken that tha Sinn o Man haes tha pooer tae forgie sïns here on irth...” - he saed tae tha paralysed man -  “A'm tellin ye, get up on yer feet, tak yer mat an awa hame tae yer ain hoose.”  Richt awa, up he got, gethert up hïs mat an waakit oot ïn front o thaim aa. Iveriebodie thocht that thïs wus a wunnèrfu sicht an gien glorie tae God, an saed, “We hae niver saen tha laik o thïs afore!” Yinst mair Jesus gaed doon tae tha loch shore. A bïg crood gethert roon hïm, an he stairtit taichin tha fowk.  Whan he wus waakin alang, he saa Alphaeus's sinn, Levi, sïttin ïn tha tex man's hut. “Follae me”, Jesus telt hïm, an Levi ris up an follaed hïm. Sae ït cum aboot, whan Jesus wus haein a bite tae ait at Levi's hoose, monie tex getherers an “sïnners” wus aitin alang wi Jesus an hïs follaers, fer thair wus aye a hale crood alang wi hïm.  Whaniver tha taichers o tha Laa an tha Pharisees saen hïm alang wi tha sïnners an tex men, the' axt hïs follaers, “Whut's he daein aitin wi tex getherers an sïnners?”  Whan Jesus heerd thïs, he saed tae thaim, “It's no tha fowk that's weel that haes need o a doctèr, but thaim that's seeck. A hinnae cum fer tae caa guid leevin fowk; ït's sïnners A hae cum tae caa.” Noo Jhone's follaers an tha Pharisees wur keepin a fast. An some fowk cum tae Jesus an axt hïm, “Hoo cum tha follaers o Jhone an tha Pharisees keep a fast, but your yins dïnnae?”  Sae Jesus cum bak wi thïs: “Dae ye thïnk fowk wud sït doon at tha spreed ïn a waddin faist alang wi tha bridegruim, an no tak a bite tae ait? Na, as lang as tha bridegruim ïs wi thaim, the' cannae fast!  But tha day wull cum, whaniver tha bridegruim wull be tuk awa frae thaim, an cum that day, the'll keep a fast.  Eftèr aa, ye wudnae shew a bït o new claith, that haesnae bin shrunk, on tae an oul cóat. If ye dae, tha patch wull teer awa tha sides o tha hole, an mak ït waur.  Nether wud ye pit new wine ïntae oul wineskïns. Fer ïf ye dae, tha skïns wull brust, an tha wine'll be skailt. An baith tha wine an tha skïns wull be ruint. But ye maun pit new wine ïntae new skïns.” Yin Sabbath day, Jesus wus waakin throu tha coarnfiels, an as the' wur makkin thair wye, hïs follaers stairtit tae pluck tha heids aff tha coarn.  An tha Pharisees saed tae Jesus, “Luk, the' shudnae be daein that! That's agin tha Laa on tha Sabbath day!”  Jesus saed tae thaim, “Hae ye no read aboot whut Davit daen whaniver hïm an hïs freens wus hung'rie an ïn want?  Dïd he no gang ïntae tha Hoose o God, whan Abiathar wus tha Heich Preesht, an dïd he no ait tha halie showbreid an gie ït tae tha ithers wi hïm forbye? Shair that wus agin tha Laa, fer naebodie but tha preeshts cud ait ït!”  An Jesus went on tae say, “Tha Sabbath wus made fer man; man wusnae made fer tha Sabbath!  Sae tha Sinn o Man ïs Loard o tha Sabbath anaa.” An Jesus went bak ïntae tha Meetin Hoose agane, an thair wus a man thair an hïs richt han wus wuthert.  An tha Pharisees kep thair een on hïm, tae see wud he hail tha man on a Sabbath day, fer ïf he dïd, the' cud hae sumthin agin hïm.  Jesus saed tae tha man wi tha baad han, “Stan up whar we can aa see ye!”  Then he saed tae tha fowk roon hïm, “On tha Sabbath, ïs ït richt tae dae guid or tae dae ïll, tae save life or tae dae awa wi ït?” But the' hel thair wheesht.  He turnt roon an gien thaim an ang'rie luk, an at tha same time he wus vext the' wur that haird-hairtit. He saed tae tha man, “Streetch oot yer han!” Sae he streetcht ït oot, an hïs han cum as guid as tha ither yin.  Richt awa tha Pharisees went oot an collogued wi Herod's follaers tae see hoo the' cud dae awa wi Jesus. But Jesus tuk hissel aff wi hïs follaers tae tha loch, alang wi a wile thrang o fowk that cum frae Galilee, Judea, Jerusalem an Idumea, frae tha ither side o tha Joardan, an even frae Tyre an Sidon, fer wurd o hïs mïracles haed trevelt faur an wide.  Tha crood wus that bïg, jundyin roon hïm on tha shore, that he toul hïs follaers tae mak a wee bóat readie fer hïm.  Fer he haed hailt that monie fowk, that aa tha yins wi an ailment püsht forrit tae touch hïm.  An whaniver fowk wi ïll spïrits saa Jesus, the' faad doon afore hïm, an tha spïrits cryed oot, “You ir tha Sinn o God!”  An he aye chairged thaim no tae tell oniebodie wha he wus. Then Jesus went ontae a muntin, an he caad tha yins he wantit wi hïm, an the' cum tae hïm.  An he pïckt oot twal tae be wi hïm, that he cud senn oot tae praich, an tae hae tha pooer [tae hail tha seeck] an tae drive oot demons. He gien tha twal tha name o “Possels”.  An thïs ïs whut the' wus caad: Simon (that Jesus caad Petèr), Jeames an Jhone, tha sinns o Zebedee (Jesus caad thaim “Boanerges”, mainin “Sinns o Thunnèr”), Andra, Phïlip, Bartholomew, Mattha, Tammas, Jeames (tha sinn o Alphaeus), Thaddaeus, Simon tha Zealot, an Judas Iscariot (tha yin that bethrayed Jesus). Sae Jesus went bak ïntae tha hoose whar he wus stappin ower, an thair wus that monie fowk croodin roon aboot thaim, that the' cud get nae peace tae hae oniethin tae ait.  Becas o whut wus happenin, Jesus' freens tried tae tak tha houl o hïm, fer the' thocht he wus oot o hïs mine.  An some maistèrs o tha Laa cum frae Jerusalem saed, “Beelzebul haes taen hïm ower. It's tha heidyin o tha demons that's giein hïm tha pooer tae cast oot ither demons!”  An Jesus caad thaim ower tae hïm an raisoned wi thaim, sayin, “Hoo can Satan cast hissel oot?  If a kïngdom ïs divïd agin ïtsel, ït maun faa sinnerie.  An ïf a femlie ïs divïd agin ïtsel, ït cannae stan.  Sae ïf Satan rises up agin hissel, an ïs divïd, then he cannae stan, an that's tha enn o hïm!  Shair naebodie can brek ïntae a strang man's hoose an ramseck ït, afore he haes tyed up tha strang man. Eftèr that, he can plunner awa!  A tell ye thïs, men can be forgien blesphemies an aa ither kines o wrangdaeins. Thair'll be nae forgiein fer hïm that spakes blesphemies agin tha Halie Spïrit, but! Fer that sïn, an tha guilt o ït, bides fer iver an aye.”  Noo Jesus saed aa thïs, becas tha fowk cum frae Jerusalem wur chairgin hïm wi haein an ïll spïrit. An tha mither an brithers o Jesus cum lukkin hïm at tha hoose whar he wus stappin, an the' caad fer hïm tae cum oot.  Summodie ïn tha crood sïttin lïstenin tae hïm toul hïm, “Yer mither an yer brithers [an sïstèrs] ir ootbye. The' ir wantin ye!”  An Jesus cum bak wi, “Wha's ma mither, an wha's ma brithers?”  An he lukt at tha crood sïttin aa roon hïm an saed, “These yins here ir ma mither an brithers!  Fer thaim at daes tha wull o God, them's ma brither, ma sïstèr, an ma mither.” Yinst mair Jesus begun lairnin fowk alang tha loch shore. A wile thrang o fowk haed gethert roon aboot hïm, sae he got ïntae a bóat that wus oot on tha wattèr. He sut doon an toul tha yins on tha shore a hale wheen o thïngs bi parables. Amang thaim wus thïs yin.  “Lïsten here [noo]! Thair wus thïs fairmer went oot tae saa seed.  Whan he wus scattèrin tha seed, some drapt doon alang tha pad an tha burds flew doon an peckt ït up.  An some fell on roakie grun whar thair wusnae much clye. It sprung up quïck, becas tha clye wus shalla,  but as shune as ït brairdit an tha sin cum oot, tha plants wus scorcht, an the' deed aff acause the' haed nae ruits.  Ither seed faad doon amang thoarns, an tha thoarns sprung up, tuk ower an chokt ït. Sae thair wus nae yiel.  But a lock drapt on tae guid grun. It daen weel an gien a guid hairst: thurtie, sïxtie or a hunnèr times mair.”  An Jesus saed, “Let hïm that haes ears ïn hïs heid tak tent!” An whan he wus on hïs ain, some o tha fowk that wus alang wi tha Twal axt hïm aboot hïs parables.  “Tha saicret o tha Kïngdom o God haes bin gien tae ye,” saed Jesus, “but tae thaim that's ootside tha Kïngdom, A taak ïn parables;  sae that ‘The' micht aye be lukkin, but niver see, an aye lïstenin, yit niver unnèrstan; less the' micht turn an [thair sïns] be forgien.’ ” An Jesus saed, “If ye dïnnae unnèrstan thïs parable, hoo ir ye gaun tae unnèrstan aa tha rest?  Tha bodie that scattèrt tha seed wus sowin tha wurd o God.  Then some fowk ïs laik tha seed that faad doon nixt tha pad. As shune as the' hear tha wurd, alang cums Satan an taks ït oot o thair hairts.  An ït's jist tha same wi tha seed that fell on tha staney grun. The' hear tha wurd an richt awa tak ït ïn wi a gled hairt.  But the' hae nae ruit sae the' cannae houl on tae ït whan haird times an trouble cums acause o God's wurd, an sae the' jist gie up.  An thair's ither fowk akin tae tha seed that wus sowed amang tha thoarns.  The'r aye worryin, rinnin eftèr money an hung'rin fer thïngs the' hinnae got. An sae thair's nae crap, fer tha wurd haesnae a chaunce tae growe.  Ither fowk ïs laik tha seed sowed on guid grun. The' hear tha wurd, tak ït tae thair hairts, an ït gies a guid yiel: thurtie, sïxtie an a hunnèr times mair.” An Jesus saed tae thaim, “Wud ye iver thïnk o brïngin ïn a lamp an pittin ït unnèr a boul or tha bed? Na. Ye wud pit ït up on a stan.  Fer thair's naethin hïd that'll no be brocht oot ïntae tha licht, an thair's nae saicret that'll no be brocht oot ïntae tha apen.  Let hïm that haes ears ïn hïs heid tak tent!”  An he saed tae thaim, “Mine hoo yis lïsten. Fer tha misure yis gie wull be tha misure yis get. Ay, an ït'll be even mair.  Fer hïm that haes plentie wull be gien mair. An hïm that haes lïttle, even whut he haes wull be tuk awa frae hïm.” An Jesus saed, “Tha Kïngdom o God ïs jist laik thïs. Tha fairmer scattèrs seed on tha grun.”  “Day an nicht, nae mettèr ïf he's up an aboot or sleepin, tha seed sprouts up an growes, tha mair he daesnae unnèrstan whut maks ït growe.  Tha seed growes ïn tha clye ïtsel, furst tha braird shows, then tha staaks, an then tha heids cums on tha tap o tha staaks.  Then whan tha crap ïs ripe, tha fairmer taks tha heuk tae ït, fer hairvest time ïs cum.” An agane he saed, “Whut d'ye thïnk tha Kïngdom o God ïs laik? Noo, whut storie cud A tell that wud pit ït ower tae ye?  It ïs laik a wee bït mustèrt seed plantit ïn tha grun, tha weeest seed o aa.  But whan ït growes, ït gets bïgger an bïgger, tae ït's tha bïggest plant ïn tha gairden, wi a spreed o brenches tha burds can roost unnèr, ïn oot o tha sin.”  An Jesus toul a hale wheen o parables laik these tae tha fowk, tae halp thaim unnèrstan.  He niver saed ocht tae thaim wi'oot uisin parables. But whan hïm an hïs follaers wur on thair ain, he toul thaim whut ït aa mained. Whan evenin cum roon, he saed tae hïs follaers, “C'mon an we'll gang ower tae tha ither side o tha loch”.  Whaniver tha thrang wus sent hame, Jesus wus aareadie ïn tha bóat, sae the' stairtit oot alang wi some ither wee bóats fer tha faur side.  Aa at yinst, a bïg wun ris up. Thair wus a pooerfu stoarm an tha waves wus batin ower tha side o tha bóat tae ït wus near fu o wattèr.  Jesus wus sleepin ïn tha bak o tha bóat, on a pïlla. Hïs follaers ris hïm yellin, “Maistèr, dae ye no care ïf we aa droon?”  Up he got, he chackt tha wun an he saed tae tha waves, “Be quait! Lown doon!”. Then tha wun drapt an ït wus aa peace an quaitness.  An Jesus saed tae thaim, “Hoo cum yis ir sae feart? Hae ye nae faith yit?” Eftèr aa thïs,  the' wur hairt-scarred an saed tae yin anither, “Whut kine o a man ïs thïs? Even tha wun an tha waves daes as he bïds thaim!” Sae the' went iver tae tha ither side o tha loch, tae tha lan whar tha Gerasenes leeved.  An whaniver Jesus wus gettin oot o tha bóat, [richt awa] a man wi an ïll spïrit cum oot frae tha graveyaird fer tae meet hïm.  Thïs man leeved amang tha tombs an naebodie cud houl hïm doon, no e'en wi chains.  Fer the' wud langelt hïm han an fit, but he puud tha chains sinnerie an tha fettèrs he brauk apairt. Naebodie wus strang eneuch tae curb hïm.  An he wud sprachle aboot nicht an day amang tha tombs an braes, scraichin, an cuttin hissel wi stanes.  Whaniver he saen Jesus a lang róads aff, he run an he faad doon on hïs knees afore hïm.  He guldèrt at hïm, “Whut ïs ït ye ir eftèr wi me, Jesus, sinn o tha maist heich God? In tha name o God, wud ye quït tormentin me!”  Fer Jesus haed aareadie saed tae hïm, “Cum oot o tha man, ye ïll spïrit.”  An Jesus axt, “Whut dae the' caa ye?” “Ma name's Legion,” cum tha answer, “fer thair's a hale lock o iz.”  An he kep on beggin Jesus no tae senn thaim awa oot o thon kintrie.  Noo nearhan on tha braeside wus a bïg herd o pïgs hokin fer food.  An tha spïrits plaidit wi Jesus, “Senn iz owerbye tae tha pïgs, let iz gang ïntae thaim.”  An sae Jesus allooed thaim. An tha ïll spïrits cum oot o tha man, an the' went ïntae tha pïgs, an tha herd - aa twa thoosan o thaim - tuk aff doon tha hïll, heid furst ïntae tha loch, an tha hale lock o thaim wus droont ïn tha wattèr. Tha yins mindin tha pïgs run aff an toul whut haed tuk place tae tha fowk ïn tha toon an kintrie roon aboot. An the' aa cum oot tae see ït fer thairsels.  Whaniver the' cum tae Jesus, the' saen tha man that haed bin taen ower wi tha legion o ïll spïrits sïttin thair quait, wi hïs claes on hïm, an richt ïn tha heid. An the' wur hairt-scarred.  Thaim at haed saen ït toul tha fowk tha ïns an oots o whut haed happent tae tha man wi tha ïll spïrits, an aboot tha pïgs forbye.  An tha fowk begun plaidin wi Jesus tae quït thair kintrie.  Whaniver Jesus wus gettin aboord tha bóat, tha man that haed bin tuk iver wi ïll spïrits rhymed on an on at hïm, tae let hïm gang wi hïm.  But Jesus wudnae alloo hïm, an he saed tae hïm, “Awa hame tae yer ain yins, an tell thaim tha much tha Loard haes daen fer ye, an hoo he's haed mercie on ye.”  Sae aff tha man went, an stairtit tellin fowk roon tha Ten Toons whut aa Jesus haed daen fer hïm. An the' wur aa dumfoonèrt. Noo whaniver Jesus went bak ïn tha bóat tae tha ither side o tha loch, a hale thrang o fowk gethert roon hïm on tha shore.  An thair wus thïs man bi tha name o Jairus, yin o tha heidyins o tha Meetin Hoose, cum up tae Jesus, an he faad doon on hïs knees afore hïm.  He plaidit sair wi Jesus, sayin, “Ma wee dochtèr ïs deein. Cud ye no cum an lay yer hans on hir, sae she'll get bettèr an no dee?”  An Jesus went alang wi hïm. A bïg thrang o fowk follaed hïm, croodin ïn on hïm.  Thair wus thïs wumman amang thaim, that haed bother wi bleedin fer twal year.  She haed tholed a hale lock unnèr monie doctèrs, an eftèr spennin aa she haed, she wus nae bettèr but jist gettin tha waur.  Noo she haed heerd aboot Jesus. She cum up behin hïm ïn tha thrang, an toucht hïs cloke,  becas she thocht: “If A cud jist touch hïs claes, A wull be made weel agane!”  Sae she dïd ït, an strecht aff tha bleedin stapt. An she felt ïn hir bodie that she wus rïd o hir bother.  Richt awa, Jesus kent tha pooer haed gan oot o hïm. He turnt roon tae tha crood, an he axt, “Wha toucht ma claes?”  An hïs follaers cum bak wi thïs: “Shair luk at aa tha fowk croodin roon ye, an ye ir axin, ‘Wha toucht me?’ ”  But Jesus kep lukkin roon tae see wha haed daen ït.  Then tha wumman, knowin fine weel whut haed happent tae hir, cum an faad doon at hïs feet, trimmlin wi fear, an toul hïm tha hale truith.  “Dochtèr,” he saed til hir, “yer faith haes made ye weel. Gang ïn peace; ye ir redd o yer trouble.” While Jesus wus still taakin, some men cum up frae tha hoose o Jairus. “Yer dochtèr ïs deid,” the' saed tae hïm. “Ye neednae bother tha maistèr onie mair.”  Takkin nae heed o whut the' saed, Jesus toul Jairus, “Dïnnae be feart; jist believe.”  Jesus wudnae alloo oniebodie tae gang wi hïm apairt frae Petèr, Jeames an Jhone, Jeames' brither.  Whaniver the' cum tae tha hame o tha heidyin o tha Meetin Hoose, Jesus saa a hale stïr amang tha fowk, wi thaim aa roarin an greetin.  He went ïn an saed tae thaim, “Whut's aa thïs narration an yowlin aboot? Tha wee lass ïs no deid, she's jist sleepin.”  But the' lacht at hïm. Sae he püt thaim aa oot, an he tuk tha wean's mither an faither an tha follaers that wur wi hïm, an he went ïn whar tha wee lass wus.  Takkin hir bi tha han, he saed tae hir, “Talitha cumi!” (mainin, “Wee lass, A say tae ye, up ye get!”).  Richt awa tha wee lass got up on hir feet an waakt aboot. She wus twal yeir oul. At thïs the' wur aa clain flebbergestit.  He bïd thaim on nae accoont tae tell oniebodie ocht aboot ït, an he toul thaim tae gie hir a bite tae ait. Eftèr thïs Jesus quït thaim pairts an went on bak tae hïs hametoon , alang wi hïs follaers.  An whaniver tha Sabbath day cum roon, he stairtit taichin tha fowk thair ïn tha Meetin Hoose, an monie that heerd hïm wur stoondit. “Whar dïd he get aa thïs frae?” the' axt. “Whut's aa thïs wusdom that he's bin gien, that sitch mïracles ir wrocht bi hïs hans!  Is thïs no jist tha cairpentèr? An he's Mary's sinn, ïsn't he, an tha brither o Jeames, Joseph, Judas an Simon? Is hïs sïstèrs no here wi iz?” An the' tuk umrage at hïm.  But Jesus saed tae thaim, “A proaphit's niver weel thocht o ïn hïs hametoon, amang hïs freens or ïn hïs ain hoose.”  He cudnae dae onie mïracles thair, apairt frae layin hïs hans on twarthie seeck fowk an makkin thaim bettèr.  An he wus tuk bak wi thair want o faith. Then Jesus went roon aa tha vïllages lairnin tha fowk. An caain hïs twal follaers roon hïm, he sent thaim oot ïn twas an gien thaim pooer ower tha ïll spïrits.  Thïs wus hïs bïddin: “Tak naethin fer tha róad apairt frae a stav - nae breid, nae baag, nae copper coins ïn yer girthpooch.  Pit sannals on yer feet an tak jist tha claes on yer bak.  Whutiver hoose yis ir stappin ïn,” he saed, “bide yer time ïn ït til yis tak yer lave o tha toon.  An ïf tha fowk ïn onie place wull no mak yis walcum or gie yis a hearin, dicht tha stour aff yer feet as yis ir leain, as a wutness an warnin tae thaim.”  An sae the' went oot, praichin that fowk shud turn frae thair sïns.  The' driv oot monie ïll spïrits, an the' anointit monie seeck fowk wi oiyle an made thaim bettèr. Kïng Herod Antipas got wun o thïs, fer tha hale kintrie wus taakin aboot Jesus. Some fowk wur sayin that Jhone tha Baptiser wus ris frae tha deid, an that wus hoo he cud dae sitch michtie warks.  Ithers thocht ït wus tha proaphit Elijah. An yit ithers thocht he maun be a proaphit laik yin o tha proaphits o tha oulden days.  Whaniver Herod heerd thïs he saed, “Thon Jhone that A haed tha heid tuk aff, he's cum bak tae life agane!”  Fer afore thïs, Herod haed gien oardèrs tae hae Jhone brocht ïn, tyed up, an püt ïn jail. He daen thïs acause o Herodias that he haed merriet, tha mair she wus hïs brither Phïlip's wife.  An Jhone haed saed tae Herod, “It's agin tha laa fer ye tae tak yer brither's wife fer yersel.”  Sae Herodias haed ït ïn fer Jhone. She wud hae kïllt hïm but she cudnae get at hïm.  Fer Herod haed a guid regaird fer Jhone; he kent he wus a strecht an halie man, sae he kep hïm oot o hairm's wye. Whan he heerd Jhone, ït bothert hïm, but aa tha same he aye lïstened tae hïm wi a gled hairt.  At lang last Herodias got hir chaunce on Herod's birthday. He wus houlin a bïg spreed fer aa tha heidyins o tha palace, tha genèrls, an tha tap men o Galilee.  Whan Herodias' dochtèr cum ïn an daunced, ït plaised Herod an thaim that sut alang wi hïm. Tha kïng saed tae hir, “Ax fer ocht ye want an A'll gie ït tae ye.”  He gien hir hïs wurd on oath; “Ax whut ye wull, an A'll gie ït tae ye, up tae a half o ma kïngdom.”  An she went oot an saed tae hir mither, “Whut'll A ax fer?” An tha mither saed bak tae hir, “Ax fer tha heid o Jhone tha Baptiser!”  Wi that, tha dochtèr run bak ïn afore tha kïng an she saed, “Whut A want ïs tha heid o Jhone tha Baptiser, richt noo, on a plattèr!”  Tha kïng wus wile sorrie, but becas o tha oath he haed tuk, an acause o tha yins wi hïm roon tha table, he dïdnae dar gae bak on hïs wurd.  Sae richt awa tha kïng sent aff a sodger, tae gang an brïng tha heid o Jhone tha Baptiser bak wi hïm. Tha man went awa, an he tuk Jhone's heid aff ïn tha jail.  He brocht ït bak on a plattèr, gien ït tae tha lassie, an she gien ït tae hir mither.  An whaniver Jhone's follaers heerd tell o ït, the' cum an tuk hïs bodie, an the' layed ït oot ïn a tomb. Noo tha possels cum bak tae Jesus frae thair trevelin, an the' toul hïm aa the' haed daen, an whut the' haed lairnt tha fowk.  An whar the' wur at, thair wus that monie cumin an gaun, that the' cudnae even get peace tae hae ocht tae ait. Sae Jesus saed tae thaim, “Cum awa on yer lane tae a quait place, an tak ït aisie fer a bït.”  Sae the' went awa ïn a bóat bi thair lane tae a quait place.  Noo monie fowk saa thaim as the' wur gaun aff, an kent wha the' wur, sae the' run on aheid on thair fit frae oot o aa tha toons, an the' got thair afore thaim.  An whan Jesus cum tae lan, he fun a hale thrang o fowk fornent hïm; an hïs hairt went oot tae thaim, fer the' wur laik sheep wannèrin wioot a herd tae luk eftèr thaim. An he begun tae lairn thaim monie thïngs.  An whan ït wus wearin late, hïs follaers cum an saed tae hïm, “It's dailygan, an thïs ïs a richt oot o tha wye place.  Senn these fowk awa tae tha fairm hooses an clachans roon aboot, tae buy thairsels a bite tae ait!”  But Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “Yous gie thaim sumthin tae ait!” An the' saed, “Whut wud we buy ït wi? It wud tak a wee foartune  tae buy fer thaim aa!”  “Whut hae ye tae ait?” qo Jesus. “Awa an fin oot!” Sae awa the' gan tae fin oot, an the' cum bak an toul hïm, “We hae five bannocks an twa fïsh.”  Sae Jesus bïd thaim aa sït doon ïn locks on tha green gress.  An the' sut doon ïn groups o hunnèrts an fïfties.  An takkin tha five bannocks an tha twa fïsh, he lukt up tae heiven, he blisst an brauk tha bannocks, an he kep giein thaim tae hïs follaers tae han oot tae tha fowk. An he divïd tha twa fïsh amang thaim aa as weel.  The' aa et thair fïll,  an the' gethert up aa tha wee bïts o breid an fïsh, eneuch tae fïll twal creels.  Thaim five bannocks haed fed five thoosan men! Richt awa, Jesus toul hïs follaers tae get aboord tha bóat, an tae gang on aheid o hïm tae tha ither side fornent Bethsaida, while he toul tha thrang o fowk tae gang hame.  An eftèr leain thaim, he went up tha muntin fer tae pray.  At dailygan, tha bóat wus oot ïn tha mïddle o tha loch, an Jesus wus on hïs lane on tha lan.  He saen tha follaers pu'in haird on tha oars, fer tha wun wus blaain agin thaim. An aboot tha fowerth watch o tha nicht he gaed oot tae thaim, waakin on tha wattèr! He wus aboot tae pass bye thaim,  but whaniver the' saen hïm waakin on tha wattèr, the' jaloused he wus a wraith. An the' yellt oot,  fer the' aa saen hïm an the' wur hairt-scarred. Strecht awa he spauk oot tae thaim, an he saed, “Tak hairt! It's masel. Dïnnae be feart!”  Then he climmed up ïntae tha bóat alangside o thaim, an tha wun deed doon. The' wur aa dumfoonèrt, an thocht ït wus ower ocht,  fer the' cudnae mak onie sense o tha mïracle o tha bannocks the'd wutnesst. Thair hairts jist wurnae apen tae ït. An whan the' gaed bak ower tha loch agane, the' cum tae lan at Gennesaret, an the' drapt enchor thonner at tha shore.  Noo whaniver the' steppit oot o tha bóat, richt awa tha fowk kent wha Jesus wus.  The' run roon tha hale kintrieside, an the' stairtit tae cairrie tha seeck on mats tae whariver the' heerd he wus at.  An noo iveriewhar he went - ïntae tha clachans, tha toons, or oot ïn tha kintrie - the' püt tha seeck oot on tha grun ïn an apen place, whar he cud see thaim. The' besocht hïm tae let thaim touch even tha enn o hïs robe; an aa that toucht ït wus makkit weel agane. Noo thair wus some Pharisees, an maistèrs o tha Laa, that haed cum frae Jerusalem, an the' gethert roon Jesus.  An the' fun faut whaniver the' saa some o hïs follaers aitin breid wi hans that wurnae clain, that's tae say, the' haednae waasht thaim.  (Tha Pharisees an aa tha Jews dïnnae ait afore waashin thair hans, houlin tae tha tradeetion o tha eldèrs.  Whan the' cum frae tha mairket, the' dïnnae ait oniethin less the' gie ït a waash furst. An monie anither thïng the' houl tae as weel, sitch as tha richt wye tae clain thair bickers an jugs, thair copper kettles [an tables].)  Then tha Pharisees an tha maistèrs o tha Laa axt Jesus, “Fer why dae yer follaers leeve wioot onie regaird tae tha wye ït wus hannit doon frae oor eldèrs, aitin breid wi thair hans no waasht?”  He saed bak tae thaim, “Isaiah got ït richt whan he proaphesied aboot yous hippycrates; as ït's writ doon: ‘Thïs nation honours me wi thair mooth,’ says God, ‘but thair hairt ïs faur awa frae me.
