Thair woarship's nae use ava; thair taichins ir naethin but man-made rules an regulations.’ Fer yis lea aside tha commauns o God, an houl on tae tha tradeetions o men [laik tha waashin o pots an bickers; an monie anither thïng yis dae.]” An he went on tae tell thaim, “Yis hae a quare wye o pittin aside tha laas o God, sae as ye can houl tae yer ain tradeetions!  Fer Moses saed, ‘Honour yer faither an yer mither’, an, ‘Oniebodie that miscaas thair faither or mither maun be püt tae deith’.  But yous say that ït's aa richt fer a bodie tae say tae hïs faither or mither: ‘A cannae gie yis onie halp becas A hae vood tae gie whut A hae tae God.’ ,  An yous let hïm dae naethin mair fer hïs faither or mither.  Sae becas o thïs yis mak a nonsense o tha wurd o God bi yer tradeetion hannit doon. An monie anither thïng yis dae laik that.” Jesus caad tha thrang tae hïm agane an saed, “Lïsten tae me, iverie yin o yis, an unnèrstan thïs:  whut gaes ïntae ye frae tha ootside daesnae sullie ye, but ït's whut cums oot o yer hairt that sullies ye.  [Let hïm that haes ears ïn hïs heid tak tent!]”  Eftèr he left tha crood o fowk an gan ïntae tha hoose, hïs follaers axt hïm aboot thïs parable.  “Ir yous as slow on tha uptake as tha ithers?” he axt. “Dae yis no see that ït's no whut yis ait that'll sullie ye?  Fer ït daesnae gae ïntae yer hairt, but ïntae yer belly, an then passes on oot doon tha drain.” (Bi thïs, Jesus wus sayin that onie soart o mait wus “clain”.)  He went on tae say, “It's whut cums oot o yer hairt that sullies ye.  Fer ït's frae wi'in yer hairt aa tha wïckit thochts cum: lustin an thievin, murdèr an adultèrie,  greed, doonricht baadness, deceit, fïlthynis, blekinin fowk's cherectèr, blesphemin, pride, an iverie kine o fuilishnis.  Aa these wïckit thïngs cum frae tha inside; ït's thaim that sullies a bodie.” Eftèr that Jesus left Galilee, an went awa tae tha dïstrict roon Tyre [an Sidon]. He stapt ïn a hoose, an dïdnae want oniebodie tae ken ït; but fer hïm thair wus nae hidin.  Fer richt awa, a wumman that haed a wee lass wi an ïll spïrit cum tae hïm as shune as she heerd he wus thair. She faad doon on hir knees afore Jesus, an plaidit wi hïm tae drive tha ïll spïrit oot frae hir dochtèr. Tha wumman wus a Greek, wi nae Jewish breedin, frae tha region o Syrophoenicia.  “A shud gie tha weans thair fïll furst,” he saed tae hir, “fer ït's no richt tae tak tha weans' breid an clod ït tae tha wee dugs!”  “Ay, Loard,” saed she, “but still wi aa, e'en tha wee dugs unnèr tha table gits aitin tha weans' crumbs.”  “That's a guid answer, an becas o ït,” qo he til hir, “whan ye gae bak hame ye'll fin tha ïll spïrit haes left yer dochtèr.”  An whaniver tha wumman cum hame, richt eneuch she fun tha wee lass lyin quait ïn hir bed, an tha ïll spïrit gan awa. Eftèr that Jesus left tha dïstrict o Tyre an he went bak doon tae tha Loch o Galilee, passin throu Sidon an tha Ten Toons on hïs wye.  Some fowk brocht tae hïm a man that wus deef an cud harlie taak, an the' plaidit wi hïm tae lay hïs han on hïm.  Eftèr takkin hïm tae tha side, awa frae tha thrang, Jesus püt hïs fïng'rs ïntae tha man's ears. Then he sput an toucht tha man's tung wi hïs spïttle.  He lukt up tae heiven, an giein a bïg seich he saed tae tha man, “Ephphatha!” (tha Aramaic mainin, “Be apent!”).  Wi that, tha man's ears wus apent, hïs tung wus lowst an he stairtit tae spake laik ither fowk.  Jesus gien thaim oardèrs no tae tell oniebodie. But tha mair he warnt thaim, tha mair the' kep on taakin aboot ït.  Fowk wur flebbergestit. “He haes daen aa thïngs weel,” the' saed. “He even maks tha deef tae hear an tha dum tae spake.” Roon aboot thon time, whaniver a bïg thrang o fowk haed gethert thegither an the' haed naethin tae ait, Jesus caad hïs follaers tae hïm, an he toul thaim,  “Ma hairt gaes oot tae these fowk, acause the' hae bin here wi me thïs thrie days an the' hae naethin lef tae ait;  If A senn thaim awa hame, the'll drap wi hung'r alang tha róad. Fer some o thaim haes cum a lang wye.”  “Oot here ïn tha wiles, hoo cud we fin eneuch tae fïll thaim?” axt hïs follaers.  “Whut feck o breid hae ye?” axt Jesus. An the' saed, “Seiven loafs.”  Then Jesus bïd tha crood o fowk sït thairsels doon on tha grun. An he tuk tha seiven loafs, gien thenks tae God fer thaim, brauk thaim up ïn bïts, an gien thaim tae hïs follaers tae han oot tae tha crood. An that's whut the' daen.  An summodie haed twarthie wee fïsh. Sae he blisst thaim tae, an toul hïs follaers tae gie thaim oot as weel.  An eftèr tha fowk haed et thair fïll, tha follaers gethert up tha fu o seiven creels o leains.  In aa, thair wus aboot fower thoosan fowk thair that day. An the' wur aa sent bak hame.  An richt awa Jesus got ïntae a bóat alang wi hïs follaers, an the' crosst ower tae tha kintrieside roon bi Dalmanutha. Thair wus some Pharisees cum oot, an the' stairtit tae quïz hïm, an axt hïm tae gie thaim a sign frae heiven. The' wur jist tryin tae ketch hïm oot.  Jesus gien a bïg seich frae deep doon, an saed, “Fer why daes fowk ïn thïs day an age keep lukkin fer a sign? A'm tellin yis, thair wull be nae sign gien tae thaim!”  An he got ïntae tha bóat an left thaim, an went ower tae tha ither side o tha loch. Noo tha follaers dïdnae mine tae tak breid wi thaim, an the' haed nae mair than yin loaf atween thaim on tha bóat.  An Jesus chairged thaim, sayin, “Luk oot fer tha yeast o tha Pharisees, an tha yeast o Herod.”  An the' taakt amang thairsels, sayin, “Thïs ïs aa becas we hae brocht nae breid.”  Jesus knowed whut the' wur thïnkin, an he axt thaim, “Why ir yis taakin aboot haein nae breid? Dae yis no see? Dae yis no unnèrstan yit? Is yer hairts still that haird?  Yis hae een - ir yis blin? Yis hae ears - ir yis deef? Dae yis no mine ocht ava?  Whaniver A divïd tha five loafs amang tha five thoosan, hoo monie baskets o leains dïd yis lïft?” “Twal,” the' saed.  “An whan A divïd tha seiven loafs amang tha fower thoosan, hoo monie creels fu o leains dïd yis lïft?” “Seiven,” the' answert.  An Jesus saed tae thaim, “Then hoo cum yis still dïnnae unnèrstan?” The' cum tae Bethsaida, an some fowk brocht a blin man tae Jesus, an plaidit wi hïm fer tae pit hïs hans on hïm.  He tuk tha blin man bi tha han an waakt hïm oot o tha vïllage. An whan he haed sput on tha man's een an püt hïs hans on hïm, Jesus axt, “Dae ye see ocht?”  Tha man lukt up an saed, “A can see fowk, but the' luk laik trees waakin aboot.”  Yinst mair Jesus püt hïs hans on tha man's een. Then hïs een apent wide, an hïs sicht cum bak. An he saa iveriethin roon hïm, clear an plain.  An Jesus sent hïm awa hame, sayin, “Dïnnae even be gan near tha vïllage, [an dïnnae be tellin oniebodie thair]!” Jesus an hïs follaers gaed on up tae tha vïllages roon Caesarea Phïlippi. An on tha wye thair, he axt hïs follaers thïs: “Wha dae fowk say that A am?”  “A wheen wud say Jhone tha Baptiser,” the' answert. “Some wud say Elijah; an ithers, yin o tha proaphits.”  “But whut aboot yersels?” Jesus axt. “Wha dae you say that A am?” An Petèr answert, “You ir tha Christ, sae ye ir!”  An Jesus gien thaim a warnin tae mak shair an tell naebodie aboot hïm. Then he begun taichin hïs follaers that tha Sinn o Man wud hae tae suffer monies a thïng. He wud be gien tha coul shoodèr bi tha eldèrs, tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa; he maun be püt tae deith an eftèr thrie days he wud rise agane frae tha deid.  Jesus spauk oot apenlie aboot thïs, an Petèr tuk hïm tae tha yin side an stairtit tae scoul hïm fer ït.  But turnin roon an lukkin at hïs follaers, Jesus chackt Petèr. “Git ahint me, Satan!” saed he. “Fer ye gie nae thocht tae tha thïngs o God. Yer heid's fu o tha thïngs o men!” Then he caad tha crood thegither alang wi hïs follaers an saed, “If oniebodie's lukkin tae follae me, he maun ferget aboot hissel aathegither, tak up hïs cross an stïck clase tae me.  Fer whaiver wants tae save hïs life wull loass ït, but hïm that loasses hïs life on accoont o me an tha Guid News wull save ït.  Whut guid ïs ït fer a bodie tae get tha hale warl, an yit tae loass hïs ain sowl?  Thair's naethin a man cud gie tae get bak hïs ain sowl, shair thair's no?  Fer ïf oniebodie ïs no wullin tae stan up fer me an ma wurds ïn thïs wïckit an godless day an age, then tha Sinn o Man wull no stan up fer hïm whan he cums ïn hïs Faither's glorie wi tha halie angels.” Jesus saed tae thaim, “Lïsten, thair's yins stud here theday that fer sartin wull no dee afore the' see tha Kïngdom o God cum wi pooer.” An eftèr sïx days haed gan bye, Jesus tuk Petèr, Jeames an Jhone alang wi hïm up ïntae a heich muntin tae be bi thairsels, an richt afore thair verie een, tha hale luk o hïm wus changed.  Hïs claes aa stairtit shinin, [white as snaa], faur whiter than onie bleacher cud iver mak thaim.  An lo an behoul, Elijah an Moses appeart, taakin thegither wi Jesus.  An Petèr saed tae Jesus, “Rabbi, A'm gled we ir here tae see thïs. Cum on an we'll big thrie shiltèrs, yin fer you, yin fer Moses an yin fer Elijah!”  Fer he dïdnae know whut else tae say, becas the' wur scarred oot o thair wuts.  An a clood cum doon an hïd thaim, an a voice cum oot o tha clood an saed, “Thïs ïs ma Sinn that A love, lïsten tae hïm!”  An aa o a suddent, whaniver the' lukt roon, thair wus naebodie thair but thairsels an Jesus. An on tha wye doon frae tha muntin, he oardèrt thaim no tae tell oniebodie whut the' haed saen til tha Sinn o Man haed ris up frae tha deid.  Sae the' daen as the' wur toul, but the' kep wunnèrin amang thairsels whut thïs risin frae tha deid wus aa aboot.  An the' axt hïm, “Hoo cum tha maistèrs o tha Laa tell iveriebodie that Elijah haes tae cum furst, afore tha Messiah?”  An he saed bak tae thaim, “Deed ay, Elijah wus tae cum furst tae get aa readie fer tha Messiah. Then ïf that's tha wye o ït, hoo cum ït's writ doon ïn tha Guid Buik, that tha Sinn o Man , maun suffer monie thïngs, an the' wud aa turn agin hïm.  But A'm tellin ye, Elijah haes aareadie bin an gan , an the' daen jist whutiver the' laikt wi hïm, as tha Guid Buik saed the' wud.” An whaniver the' cum bak doon tae hïs ither follaers, the' saa a wile crood roon thaim, an some maistèrs o tha Laa thrawin wi thaim.  An tha crood o fowk wus aa bye thairsels wi excitement whaniver the' saa Jesus, an the' run up tae bïd hïm walcum.  Jesus axt tha maistèrs o tha Laa, “Whut's thïs thraw aboot?”  An yin o tha crood saed bak tae hïm, “Maistèr, A hae brocht ma sinn tae ye, fer he haes an ïll spïrit an cannae taak.  An whan ït taks hoult o hïm, he gangs ïntae a fït an he faas doon, foamin at tha mooth an scringein hïs teeth, an he's jist wastin awa. A axt yer follaers tae rïd hïm o tha spïrit, an the' cudnae dae ït!”  An he saed, “O you faithless fowk, hoo lang wull A be wi ye afore yis believe? Hoo lang dae A hae tae pit up wi ye? Brïng tha wee lad tae me!”  Sae the' brocht hïm, an whaniver tha spïrit saa Jesus, ït sent tha lad ïntae a fït, an he faad tae tha grun, rowlin aboot an foamin at tha mooth.  “Hoo lang haes he bin laik thïs?” Jesus axt tha faither. An he saed, “Since he wus a wean.  An monies tha time ït haes throwed hïm ïntae tha fire an ïntae tha wattèr as weel, tae dae awa wi hïm; sae ïf You can dae oniethin ava, tak peetie on iz an halp iz.”  Jesus saed, “Whut dae ye main bi ‘If A can’? Oniethin ïs poassible whan a bodie believes!”  An richt awa tha wee lad's faither cryed oot, “Loard, A dae believe, but tak awa tha doots A hae!”  Jesus saa that tha crood wus gettin bïgger, an he gien tha wïckit spïrit a richt barjin, sayin, “Cum oot o hïm, ye deef an dum spïrit, an stye oot!”  An tha spïrit gien a scraich an ït throwed tha lad tae tha grun ïn anither fït, jist afore ït cum oot o hïm. Tha wee fella lukt as ïf he haed deed, an sae tha crood saed, “He's deid.”  But Jesus tuk hïm bi tha han an halpt hïm tae hïs feet, an he wus fït tae stan.  A while latèr, whaniver Jesus wus ïn tha hoose on hïs ain wi hïs follaers, the' axt hïm, “Whut fer cud we no cast tha ïll spïrit oot?”  An he saed, “Ye can onlie git rïd o thïs kine bi prayer [an fastin].” Sae the' left thair an went on throu Galilee. An Jesus dïdnae want oniebodie tae know whar he wus;  fer he wantit tae hae time tae taich hïs follaers. He toul thaim, “Tha Sinn o Man'll be hannit ower tae men that wull kïll hïm. Eftèr thrie days but, he'll rise frae tha deid.”  But the' cudnae unnèrstan whut he wus mainin, an the' wur feart tae ax hïm aboot ït. An he cum tae Capernaum, an whan he wus ïn tha hoose the' wur stayin at, he axt thaim, “Whut wur ye argyin aboot on tha wye here?”  But the' dïdnae say ocht, becas the' haed bin argyin aboot wha amang thaim wus tha maist thocht o.  An he sut doon an caad thaim ower, an saed tae thaim, “Whaiver wants tae be furst maun tak tha hinmaist place, an be tha sarvint o iverie ither bodie.”  An he tuk a wean an stud hïm amang thaim; then he tuk hïm ïn hïs airms an saed tae thaim,  “Whaiver walcums yin o these weans ïn ma name, bïds me walcum, an whaiver bïds me walcum, walcums no me alane, but hïm that sent me as weel.” An Jhone saed tae hïm, “Taicher, we saa a bodie drivin oot demons ïn your name, an we made hïm stap, fer he wusnae yin o us.”  But Jesus saed, “Dae nae sitch thïng, fer oniebodie that daes a mïracle ïn ma name wull no be quïck tae spake agin me.  Fer whaiver's no agin iz ïs wi iz.  Whaiver gies ye a bicker o wattèr ïn ma name becas ye belang tae Christ - A tell ye, he'll no be wantin fer a reward, that's fer shair! But ïf oniebodie leads asthray yin o these weans that believes ïn me, ït wud be bettèr fer hïm ïf he wus throwed ïntae tha sea, wi a mïllstane roon hïs neck!  An ïf yer han maks ye dae wrang, cut ït aff, fer ït wud be bettèr tae gae tae heiven wi tha yin han, than tae hae twa hans an gae tae hell,  [‘whar tha worm niver dees an tha fire keeps on a-burnin.’]  An ïf yer fit maks ye dae wrang, cut ït aff, fer ït wud be bettèr tae hae jist tha yin fit an gae tae heiven, than tae hae twa feet an be throwed ïntae hell, whar tha fire niver dees.  [‘Thair tha worm niver dees an tha fire keeps on a-burnin’.]  An ïf yer ee maks ye dae wrang, pu ït oot, fer ït's bettèr tae gae ïntae tha Kïngdom o God half blin, than tae hae twa een an be throwed ïntae hell,  [‘whar tha worm niver dees an tha fire keeps on a-burnin.’] Fer iveriebodie wull be purified wi fire, [jist as a secryfice ïs purified wi saut.]  Saut ïs guid, but ïf ït loasses ïts strenth, hoo dae ye mak ït saltie agane? Hae saut ïn yersels, dïnnae loass yer strenth, an leeve at peace wi yin anither.” Jesus then left Capernaum an went ïntae Judea, an he crosst ower tha rïver Joardan. Thair a crood o fowk gethert up agane, an he taicht thaim as he aye dïd.  An some Pharisees, tae pit hïm tae tha test, axt hïm, “Is ït allooed fer a husban tae pit awa hïs wife?”  An he answert, “Whut dïd Moses tell yis tae dae?”  The' saed, “Moses allooed a man tae write a notysh o divorce tae pit hir awa.”  An Jesus saed tae thaim, “It wus becas yer hairts wus haird that Moses gien ye thïs laa.  But frae tha stairt o Creation God made men an he made weemen. Sae a man wull lea hïs faither an mither an be joint tae hïs wife.  An tha twa wull becum as yin, nae mair twa seprit fowk.  Sae whut God haes püt thegither, let nae man püll sinnerie.”  But whan the' wur bak ïn tha hoose, hïs follaers brocht up tha mettèr agane.  An he saed tae thaim, “Whaiver pits awa hïs wife, an merries anither, he commïts adultèrie agin hir.  An ïf a wumman pits awa hir man, an gits merriet tae anither, she commïts adultèrie as weel.” An the' brocht weans fer hïm tae pit hïs hans on thaim tae bliss thaim, but hïs follaers chackt tha yins that brocht thaim.  Whan Jesus saen thïs, he wus wile ang'rie, an saed tae thaim, “Alloo tha weans tae cum tae me, an dïnnae stap thaim, fer tha Kïngdom o God belangs tae tha laik o these.  A'm tellin ye tha truith, whaiver daesnae tak tha Kïngdom o God ïntae hïs hairt laik a wean daes, wull no get ïn ava.”  An he tuk tha weans up ïn hïs airms, püt hïs hans on thaim an gien thaim hïs blissin. Noo as Jesus wus settin oot agane, thair wus thïs man cum rinnin tae hïm. He bood doon afore Jesus an axt hïm, “Guid Maistèr, whut maun A dae tae be shair A get tae heiven an leeve fer iver?”  An Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “Why ir ye caain me guid? Thair's naebodie guid apairt frae God.  Ye weel ken tha commauns: ‘Dïnnae murdèr’; ‘dïnnae commït adultèrie’; ‘dïnnae tak whut's no yer ain’; ‘dïnnae tell lees aboot ither fowk’; ‘dïnnae be daein fowk oot o ocht’; an ‘gie respeck tae yer faither an yer mither’.”  An tha man saed tae Jesus, “Maistèr, A hae daen aa thaim thïngs since A wus nae age.”  Jesus lukt at tha man wi love, an he toul hïm, “Yin thïng ye hinnae daen. Gae awa an sell aa ye hae, an gie tha siller tae tha puir. An ye'll hae walth ïn heiven. [An then tak up yer cross] an cum eftèr me.”  Whaniver he heerd thïs, he wus vext, an he went awa doon ïn tha mooth, fer he wus quare an weel-aff. An Jesus turnt roon, an he saed tae hïs follaers, “Hoo verie haird ït wull be fer weel monied fowk tae enter ïntae tha Kïngdom o God!”  Whan he saed thïs, hïs follaers wus aa tuk bak. But Jesus saed tae thaim agane, “Freens, hoo verie haird ït ïs [fer thaim at pits thair trust ïn thair siller] tae git ïntae tha Kïngdom o God!  It wud be aisier fer a kemel tae gae throu tha ee o a needle, ner fer a monied man tae git ïntae tha Kïngdom o God.”  An hïs follaers wur thunnèrstruck. “Then wha ïn aa tha warl can be saved?” the' axt hïm.  Jesus lukt strecht at thaim an saed, “Man cannae dae ït bi hissel! But God can dae ït. Fer wi God aa thïngs ir poassible.”  Then Petèr begun tae spake an he saed tae Jesus, “Mine, we hae left iveriethin behin, an cum eftèr ye!”  An Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “A tell ye thïs, thair's naebodie that haes left behin hïm hïs hoose, or brithers, or sïstèrs, or mither, or faither, [or wife] or weans, or fairm o lan fer ma sake an tha sake o tha Guid News,  but he'll get a hunnèr times mair ïn tha here an noo o hooses, brithers, sïstèrs, mither, weans, or fairm o lan, as weel as a lock o persecution; an he'll hae life iverlastin ïn tha warl tae cum.  An monies a bodie that's foremaist noo wull be last then, an monie that's last noo wull be foremaist then.” An the' wur noo on tha róad up tae Jerusalem wi Jesus waakin aheid o hïs follaers; an the' wur ïn awe o hïm, an tha fowk cumin behin wur wile feart. An he tuk tha Twal tae tha side agane, an he begun tae tell thaim whut wus gaun tae happen tae hïm.  He saed, “Luk, we'r gaun tae Jerusalem whar tha Sinn o Man wull be hannit ower tae tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa, that wull sentence hïm tae dee, an gie hïm ower tae thaim that's no Jews .  An the' wull jeer hïm, gie hïm a whuppin, spït on hïs face an kïll hïm, but eftèr thrie days, he'll rise tae life agane.” Jeames an Jhone, tha sinns o Zebedee, cum an saed tae Jesus, “Maistèr, thair's sumthin we want ye tae dae fer iz.”  An he saed, “Whut ïs ït yis want?”  The' answert, “Let yin o iz sït doon on yer richt han side, an tha ither yin on yer left, whaniver ye tak yer throne ïn glorie!”  But Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “Yis dïnnae ken whut yis ir axin. Cud yis thole tae drïnk tha cup o sufferin that A maun drïnk, or tae be baptised wi tha baptisin that A'll be baptised wi?”  An the' saed tae hïm, “Ay, that we can.” An Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “Yis shairlie wull drïnk frae ma cup, an be baptised wi ma baptisin.  But ït's no up tae me tae alloo yis tae sït on ma richt han side, or on ma left. It's up tae God tae gie thaim saits tae tha yins the' wur meent fer.”  Noo whaniver tha ither ten follaers heerd whut Jeames an Jhone haed axt fer, the' stairtit tae get wile ang'rie wi thaim.  Sae Jesus caad thaim thegither an saed tae thaim, “Yis aa ken that tha yins that rule ower tha Gentiles laird ït ower thair ain fowk, an thair heidyins aye lets thaim know wha's tha boss.  Thïs ïs no tha wye ït shud be amang you but, fer whaiver wants tae be foremaist amang ye, haes tae be laik a sarvint.  An whaiver wants tae be tha heid man haes tae slave fer aa tha rest!  Fer even tha Sinn o Man dïdnae cum tae be tendit tae, but fer tae sarve ithers, an tae gie hïs life as a ransom fer monie fowk.” Jesus an hïs follaers trevelt tae Jericho. An as the' wur leain tha toon wi a bïg crood follaein thaim, the' saen blin Bartimaeus, tha sinn o Timaeus, sïttin beggin on tha bunker o tha róad.  Whan Bartimaeus heerd that Jesus o Nazareth wus gaun bye, he begun tae caa oot, “Jesus, Sinn o Davit, tak peetie on me!”  Tha fowk chackt hïm an the' toul hïm tae be quait, but he guldèrt aa tha looder, “Jesus, Sinn o Davit, tak peetie on me!”  Jesus stapt ïn hïs step, an toul thaim tae caa tha blin man ower. Sae the' caad hïm an saed tae hïm, “Tak hairt! Git up, fer he's caain ye!”  Wi that, he aff wi hïs cóat, lep up an cum tae Jesus.  An Jesus axt, “Whut dae ye want me tae dae fer ye?” “Rabboni” answert tha blin man, “A want tae be able tae see agane.”  An Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “Gang yer wye, yer faith haes made ye hale!” An al at yinst he wus able tae see agane, an he went aff doon tha róad eftèr Jesus. An whaniver the' got near tae Bethphage an Bethanie on tha ootskirts o Jerusalem nixt tha Moont o Olives, Jesus bïd twa o hïs follaers tae gang on aheid.  He saed, “Gae ïntae tha clachan fornent ye, an as shuin as ye gae ïn, ye'll fin a cowlt tyed up, that naebodie haes iver sut on. Lowse ït, an brïng ït here!  If oniebodie axes ye, ‘Whut ir ye daein?’, jist tell thaim, ‘Tha Loard haes need o ït, an ye'll get ït bak afore lang.’ ”  Sae aff the' went, an fun tha cowlt tyed tae a dure ootbye on tha street. An the' lowsed ït.  Noo some o tha yins stannin roon axt thaim, “Whut ir ye daein, lowsin that cowlt?”  Tha twa follaers answert whut Jesus haed toul thaim tae say, an tha fowk lut thaim gang on aheid.  Sae the' brocht tha cowlt tae Jesus, an throwed thair claes ower ïts bak. An Jesus got up on ït.  An a lock o fowk stannin alang tha róad spreed thair claes on tha pad, an ither yins cut doon leafie brenches oot o tha fiels an the' strewed thaim afore hïm.  An afore an behin fowk wur cryin oot, “Hosanna! Blisst be tha Yin that cums ïn tha name o tha Loard! Blisst be tha cumin Kïngdom o oor faither Davit. Hosanna ïn tha heichest heiven!” Sae Jesus went ïntae Jerusalem, an on ïntae tha Hoose o God. An whan he haed lukt roon, an haed tuk iveriethin ïn, he left fer Bethanie agane wi hïs twal follaers, becas ït wus gettin late on ïn tha day. Tha nixt day, whan the' wur leain Bethanie, Jesus wus hung'rie.  An he notyshed a fïg tree a guid wye aff wi leafs on ït, sae he went tae see ïf ït haed onie fruit; but ït haed naethin on ït apairt frae leafs, fer ït wusnae tha richt time o yeir.  An hïs follaers heerd hïm sayin tae tha tree, “Nae man wull iver ait fruit frae you agane!” The' cum tae Jerusalem. An Jesus went strecht ïntae tha Hoose o God, an he begun reddin oot tha dailers that wus buyin an sellin ïn tha coortyaird. He coupt tha tables o tha siller changers, an whammelt tha saits o thaim that wus sellin doos.  He wudnae alloo fowk tae cairrie oniethin ïntae tha Hoose o God fer tae be soul.  An he gien thaim thïs lesson. Saed he, “Is ït no writ doon, ‘Ma hoose wull be caad a hoose o prayer fer aa nations’? But yous hae turnt ït ïntae a den o robbers!”  An whaniver tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa heerd thïs, the' wantit tae dae awa wi hïm, fer the' wur feart o hïm, becas aa tha fowk wur wile taen on wi hïs taichin.  An at dailygan the' went oot o tha cïtie. An ïn tha moarn, whaniver the' passt tha fïg tree, ït wus aa wuthert, ay, richt doon tae tha ruits.  An Petèr mindit tha day afore an saed, “Luk, Rabbi, tha fïg tree ye curst ïs aa weezened up an deid!”  Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “Hae faith ïn God.  Fer A tell yis thïs, whaiver wull say tae thïs muntin, ‘Be shïftit frae whar ye ir, an cast yersel ïntae tha sea!’; ïf tha same man haesnae onie doot ïn hïs hairt, but believes ïn hissel that thïs wull raelie cum aboot, then God wull dae ït fer hïm!  Sae A say tae yis, aa tha thïngs yis ax fer ïn prayer, believe yis wull hae thaim, an shair eneuch, yis wull.  An whan yis stan up tae pray, forgie oniebodie that haes daen yis wrang, sae that yer heivenlie Faither wull forgie you tha wrangs yous hae daen.  [If yis dïnnae forgie ither fowk, nether wull yer heivenlie Faither forgie yous!]” An the' went bak agane tae Jerusalem an ïntae tha Hoose o God. An as he wus waakin aboot, tha heid preeshts, tha maistèrs o tha Laa an tha eldèrs cum up tae hïm an saed, “Bi whut thortie ir ye daein these thïngs, an wha gien ye ït?”  An Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “A want tae ax ye yin question, an whaniver yis gie me tha answer, A wull tell yis bi whut thortie A dae these thïngs.  Whaniver Jhone wus baptisin, wus thïs frae heiven or jist a notion o man? Answer me that!”  Noo the' taakt thïs ower amang thairsels, an the' thocht: “If we say ‘Frae heiven’, then he'll say, ‘Sae hoo cum yis dïdnae believe hïm?’  But ïf we say, ‘It wus frae men’, whut then?” Fer the' wur feart tha fowk wud turn on thaim, becas they aa thocht Jhone wus a proaphit.  Sae the' saed, “We cannae tell.” An whaniver Jesus heerd thïs, he saed, “Then A'll no be tellin yis ether bi whut thortie A dae these thïngs!” An Jesus begun tae taak tae thaim bi parables. “Thair wus thïs man that plantit a vineyaird,” saed he, “an he fenced ït aa roon. He dug a pit fer a winepress, bigged a luk-oot tooer, an he set tha vineyaird tae a wheen o tenant-fairmers tae rin. Then he tuk aff tae anither kintrie.  Whaniver hairvest time cum roon, he sent yin o hïs sarvints tae tha fairmers, tae collect hïs share o tha fruit.  An the' tuk houl o tha sarvint, bate hïm up, an chaist hïm awa empie-hannit.  Sae tha owner sent anither sarvint, that wus traitit ïn tha same shamefu wye, onlie a lock waur, fer the' peltit hïs heid wi stanes.  Then he sent anither an the' kïllt hïm, an he sent a wheen mair an the' ether bate thaim up or kïllt thaim as weel.  Bi noo tha laird haed naebodie lef tae senn apairt frae hïs ain dear sinn. Sae ïn tha enn he sent hïm tae thaim, thïnkin tae hissel, ‘He's ma ain sinn, shairlie the'll hae regaird fer hïm!’  An tha tenant-fairmers saed tae yin anither, ‘Thïs boy wull tak ower whan hïs da dees. If we dae awa wi hïm, aa thïs wull be oors!’  Sae the' tuk houl o hïm, kïllt hïm, an throwed hïs bodie oot o tha vineyaird.  Whut dae yis thïnk tha laird wull dae?” axt Jesus. “Wull he no cum an desthroy thaim fairmers, an set hïs vineyaird tae ithers?  Hae yis no read tha Scrïpture whar ït says: Tha verie stane tha masons turnt doon ïs noo tha coarner stane. Tha Loard hissel haes wrocht thïs, An a wunnèrfu sicht ït ïs!” Tha releejus heidyins wantit tae hae Jesus arrestit, but the' wur feart o tha thrang. The' knowed that tha parable he toul wus agin thairsels. Sae the' went awa an left hïm alane. Latèr on, the' sent some Pharisees an men o Herod's pairtie fer tae ketch Jesus oot ïn whut he saed.  Whaniver the' cum, the' saed tae hïm, “Maistèr, we ken ye spake tha truith, wioot onie thocht o whut ither fowk thïnks o ye. Ye dïnnae mak o yin mair ner tha ither, an ye taich tha true wye o God. Answer thïs: ïs ït richt tae pye texes tae Caesar or no?  Wull we gie or wull we no gie?” The' wur twa faced, but Jesus saa throu thaim an axt, “Fer why ir ye tryin tae ketch me oot? Brïng me a denarius  til A see!”  An whaniver the' brocht ït, he axt thaim thïs, “Whase name an laikness ïs on ït?” “It's Caesar's”, the' answert.  An Jesus saed, “Gie Caesar whut belangs tae Caesar, an gie God whut belangs tae God.” An the' wur dumfoonèrt wi hïs answer. Tha nixt tae cum alang wur tha Sadducees, thaim that say thair ïsnae onie risin frae tha deid. An thïs ïs whut the' püt tae hïm:  “Maistèr, Moses writ doon fer iz, that ïf a man's brither dees an leas a guidwife wi nae weans, then tha brither maun merrie tha weeda an hae childèr fer hïs deid brither.  Noo whut ïf thair wus seiven brithers an tha oulest taks a wife, an he dees afore the' hae onie weans.  Then tha saicont yin merries hir, an he dees wioot haein onie weans ether, an tha thurd brither tha same.  An lo an behoul, tha hale seiven merries hir wioot haein onie weans. An bye an bye tha wumman, she deed as weel.  Sae tell iz thïs, at tha risin frae tha deid, whase guidwife wull she be, seein she wus merriet on tha hale seiven o thaim?” An Jesus cum bak wi thïs: “Ye ir no richt ava, sae ye'r no, fer ye dïnnae ken tha Scrïptures an ye dïnnae ken tha pooer o God!  Fer whaniver fowk rise frae tha deid, thair wull be nae mair merryin; the' wull jist be laik tha angels ïn heiven.  An consarnin tha risin frae tha deid - dae yis no mine readin whut Moses writ aboot tha burnin büsh, whan God taakt tae hïm an saed, ‘A be tha God o Abraham an tha God o Isaac an tha God o Jacob’? An God saed thïs lang eftèr tha thrie o thaim wus deid!  God's no tha God o tha deid, he's tha God o tha leevin. Yis ir aa wrang!” An stannin, lïstenin tae whut wus gaun on, wus yin o tha maistèrs o tha Laa. He heerd whut a guid answer Jesus haed gien, an he axt hïm thïs: “O aa tha commauns, whut yin ïs tha maist impoartin?”  An Jesus answert bak, “Tha maist impoartin ïs thïs: ‘An tak heed, O Israel, tha Loard oor God ïs tha yin an onlie God, an ye maun love tha Loard yer God wi aa yer hairt an yer sowl, an aa yer mine, micht an main!’ [Thïs ïs tha furst commaun.]  An tha saicont yin ïs thïs: ‘Ye maun love yer nighber jist as much as yersel.’ Nae ither commaun ïs abain these twa.”  An tha maistèr o tha Laa saed tae hïm, “Weel saed, Maistèr, ït's tha truith ye spake, fer thair ïs yin God, an nane ither but hïm!  An tae love God wi aa yer hairt an mine, micht an main, an yer nighber as yersel, ïs mair impoartin than aa tha brunt offerins an secryfices ye cud mak!”  Whaniver Jesus heerd tha sense tha man wus taakin, he saed tae hïm, “Ye ir no faur awa frae tha Kïngdom o God!” Eftèr that, naebodie wud dar pit onie mair questions tae hïm. An whan Jesus wus taichin ïn tha Hoose o God, he axt tha fowk thïs: “Hoo cum tha maistèrs o tha Laa say that tha Messiah  ïs tha sinn o Davit?  Tha Halie Spïrit promptit Davit tae say: ‘Tha Loard saed tae ma Loard: Sït doon at ma richt han, tae A pit yer enemies unnèr yer feet.’ Noo Davit hissel caad tha Messiah ‘ma Loard’, sae hoo then can he be hïs sinn as weel?” An tha fowk wur gye gled tae lïsten tae Jesus. An as he taicht thaim Jesus went on tae say, “Watch oot fer thaim maistèrs o tha Laa, paradin aboot ïn thair fancie robes, wantin fowk tae touch thair keps tae thaim at tha mairket.  The' laik tha best saits ïn tha Meetin Hooses, an tae be at tha tap table at faists.  The' halp thairsels bi daein weeda weemen oot o aa the' hae. An the' mak lang screeds o prayers jist fer show. But ye can be shair ït wull gang waur wi thaim on tha Day o Reckonin.” An Jesus sut doon fornent tha kïst ïn tha Hoose o God, whar he cud hae sicht o tha fowk pittin thair money ïntil ït. An tha weel-aff yins gien weel, nae doot aboot ït!  Then alang cum a weeda wumman, an she drapt ïn twa wee coins, amuntin tae verie lïttle .  Jesus caad hïs follaers ower tae hïm an saed, “A'm tellin yis tha truith, thïs puir weeda haes gien mair ner onie o tha ithers that gien offerins.  Fer the' hae aa gien onlie a pïttance oot o thair pruch, but thïs weeda, puir an aa that she ïs, haes gien aa she haed tae leeve on!” Yin day, as Jesus wus gaun oot o tha Temple gruns, yin o hïs follaers saed tae hïm, “Maistèr, wud ye jist luk at thon stanewark, an thaim wunnèrfu biggins!”  Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “Dae ye see these great biggins? No yin stane here wull be left abain tha ither, that'll no be tummelt doon!”  An Jesus wus sïttin on tha Moont o Olives fornent tha Hoose o God, whan Petèr, Jeames, Jhone an Andra axt hïm on tha quait:  “Tell iz, whan wull aa thïs cum aboot? Wull thair be onie sign ït's gaun tae happen?”  An Jesus saed tae thaim, “Tak heed an dïnnae let oniebodie lead yis aglee.  Fer monies a yin wull cum ïn ma name, sayin, ‘A be tha Christ’, an the'll lead monie fowk aglee.  Whan ye hear tell o wars an o taak aboot wars, dïnnae be püt aboot. Fer sitch thïngs maun happen, but tha enn ïs no near jist yit.  Nations wull mak war on ither nations, an kïngdoms wull rise up agin ither kïngdoms; thair wull be irthquakes ïn monie pairts, an thair wull be dirths ower tha lan tae. But aa thïs ïs onlie tha stairt o tha bairin pains cumin on.  Ye maun tak heed. The' wull han yis ower tae tha cooncils, an gie yis a whuppin ïn tha Meetin Hooses. On ma accoont ye wull be stud afore guviners an kïngs, as a wutness tae thaim.  But afore thïs, tha Guid News maun be praicht tae aa tha nations.  Noo whaniver yis ir lïftit, an brocht tae thrial, dïnnae be ower enxious aboot whut yis ir gaun tae say, but whan tha time cums jist say whutiver God tells yis tae. Fer then ït'll no be yous that'll be taakin, but ït'll be tha Halie Spïrit.  Brithers wull han ower thair brithers tae be kïllt, an faithers thair weans. An weans wull rise up agin thair faithers an mithers, an hae thaim püt tae deith as weel.  Ye'll be haitit bi aa fowk on accoont o me, but tha yin that tholes tae tha enn wull be saved. But whaniver yis see ‘tha abomination o desolation’, [spauk aboot bi Daniel tha proaphit] stannin whar ït shudnae be, then thaim at's ïn Judea maun tak tae tha hïlls (Reader, ye'll unnèrstan ma mainin here.) Naebodie that's on hïs ruiftap , shud be gaun bak doon tae get ocht oot o ït;  an naebodie that's awa oot ïntae hïs fiel shud be gaun bak fer hïs cóat.  In thaim days ït'll be tarrible fer weemen that's expectin, an fer mithers wi weans at tha breesht.  Pray tae God that thïs daesnae happen ïn tha wuntèr.  Fer ïn thaim days thair'll be sitch wile sufferin  - faur waur ner thair iver wus frae tha time God made tha warl til noo - an ye'll niver see tha laik agane.  Gin tha Loard daesnae cut thaim days shoart, thair's naebodie wud be saved; but ït's on accoont o hïs ain chosen yins, that he's cut tha days shoart.  An ïf oniebodie shud say tae ye at that time, ‘Luk! Here ïs tha Messiah!’, or, ‘Thair he's thonner!’, dïnnae tak onie heed.  Fer fauss messiahs an fauss proaphits wull rise up an dae signs an wunnèrs, an fowk wull be tuk ïn bi thaim, ay, an e'en tha chosen yins micht be tuk ïn tae.  But tak heed, A hae toul ye aa thïs aheid o time, sae as ye'll know. But ïn thaim days, eftèr tha time o sufferin, ‘tha sin wull be mirkit, an tha muin wull no gie onie licht;  tha starns wull be faain oot o heiven, an tha pooers o tha lïft wull be dinnelt.’  An then aa fowk wull see tha Sinn o Man cumin ïn tha cloods, ïn michtie pooer an glorie.  An then he wull senn hïs angels oot, tae gether thegither [hïs] chosen yins frae tha fower wuns, frae tha ootermaist pairt o tha irth tae tha ootermaist pairt o heiven.” “Noo, lairn thïs lesson frae tha fïg tree. As shuin as ïts brenches stairts tae bud, an ïts leafs cum oot, ye ken tha simmer ïs no faur aff.  In tha same wye, whaniver ye see these thïngs happenin, ye'll ken tha time ïs nearhan, ay, at tha verie dure ïtsel.  A'm tellin ye tha truith, thair's fowks leevin noo that'll no dee, afore aa these thïngs haes cum aboot!  Heiven an irth wull pass awa, but ma wurds wull niver pass awa. Naebodie kens tha day or oor whan aa thïs wull happen, nether tha angels ïn heiven, ner tha Sinn hissel. Tha Faither alane kens.  Tak heed, keep a luk-oot, [an pray], fer ye dïnnae ken whan that time wull be.  Fer tha cumin o tha Sinn o Man ïs laik a man gaun tae a faur-awa lan, that haes left hïs hoose ïn tha chairge o hïs sarvints. He gien thaim aa thair ain wark tae dae, an he toul tha dureman tae be on tha luk-oot fer hïm cumin bak.  Sae yous be on tha luk-oot tae, fer ye dïnnae ken whan tha Laird wull be bak - whuther at tha gloamin, or at mïdnicht, or ïn tha wee smaa oors, or at tha scraich o day,  less cumin on ye o a suddent he'll fin ye sleepin.  Whut A say tae ye, A say tae yin an aa: ‘Be on tha luk-oot!’ ” It wus twa days afore tha Passower an tha Faist o Bairmless Breid, an tha heid preeshts, an tha maistèrs o tha Laa wus colloguin thegither tae git tha houl o Jesus bi some sleekit wye, fer tae pit hïm tae deith.  “But no whaniver tha Faist's on,” the' saed, “or we'll hae a garevitch on oor hans.” Yin day, whan Jesus wus ïn Simon tha Leper's hoose ïn Bethanie, he wus at tha boord fer a bite tae ait, whan a wumman cum ïn wi a wee crock o scent: ït wus oyle o pure nard an coast bïg money. Brekkin aff tha tap o tha stoup, she poored tha oyle ower hïs heid.  But some o thaim that wus thair wus sair ïll-plaised, an saed yin tae tither, “Whut fer wus thïs waste o guid nard?  Fer ït cud hae bin soul fer mair ner thrie hunnèr siller coins  an tha catter gien tae tha puir.” Sae the' turnt an yaukt tha wumman.  But Jesus saed, “Lea hir alane. Dïnnae bother hir, fer thïs ïs a guid thïng she's daen fer me.  Fer ye'll aye hae tha puir wi yis, an ye can be guid tae thaim whaniver ye want. But ye'll no aye hae me wi ye.  She haes daen aa she cud, fer she haes cum aforehan tae anoint ma bodie fer buryin.  A'm tellin ye tha truith, whariver tha Guid News ïs praicht ower tha hale warl, hir storie wull be toul sae as she'll niver be fergot.” An Judas Iscariot, yin o tha Twal, gaed awa tae tha heid preeshts fer tae bethray Jesus ïntae thair hans.  An whan the' heerd ït, the' wur richt gled, an gien thair wurd tae gie hïm siller fer hïs wark. Sae he lukt oot fer a guid chaunce tae han Jesus ower. On tha furst day o tha Faist o Bairmless Breid, whan the' aye kïllt tha Passower lamb, Jesus' follaers axt hïm, “Whar dae ye want iz tae gang tae mak readie fer tha Passower mail?”  Sae Jesus sent oot twa o hïs follaers ïntae Jerusalem wi thair oardèrs. “As ye gang ïntae tha cïtie,” he toul thaim, “a man cairryin a crockerie jar o wattèr wull meet ye. Follae hïm,  an say tae tha guidman o tha hoose he gangs ïntae, ‘Tha Maistèr says, Whar ïs ma ruim whar A can ait tha Passower wi ma follaers?’  An he wull show yis a bïg upstair ruim, plenisht an aa. Ye ir tae mak ït readie fer iz thair.”  Tha follaers gan oot, an awa ïntae tha cïtie, an the' fun ït jist as he haed saed. Sae the' made readie tha boord fer tha Passower mail.  Whan ït wus weel on ïn tha evenin, Jesus cum wi tha twal possels.  As the' wur lyin at tha boord an aitin, Jesus saed, “A tell ye tha truith, yin o yis that's suppin wi me noo ïs fer bethrayin me.”  The' wur aa sorrie whaniver the' heerd thïs, an yin bi yin the' axt hïm, “Is ït me ye ir taakin aboot?” [An anither yin saed, “Is ït me?”]  He saed bak tae thaim, “It's yin o yous twal that's dïppin hïs han ïn tha boul wi me;  fer A, tha Sinn o Man, maun follae tha róad tha Scrïptures foretoul lang syne. But wile sorra tae tha yin that bethrays me. Faur bettèr fer that man ïf he haed niver bin boarn!” An as the' wur aitin, Jesus tuk breid ïn hïs hans an gien thenks tae God. Then he brauk ït, an he hannit ït tae hïs follaers sayin, “Tak ït; thïs ïs ma bodie.” An he tuk a bicker o wine an gien thenks tae God fer ït. Then he hannit ït roon, an the' aa drunk frae ït.  An he saed tae thaim, “Thïs ïs ma bluid, a sign o God's new coveynant, sealed wi ma bluid poored oot fer monie.  Mairk thïs, A'll drïnk nae mair o tha fruit o tha vine, tae A drïnk a new wine ïn tha Kïngdom o God.”  Then the' sung tha Passower psaum, an the' went oot on tae tha Moont o Olives. “Yis'll aa faa awa on accoont o me [tha nicht],” Jesus saed tae thaim. “Fer as ït's writ, ‘A wull strike tha shepherd an tha sheep'll be scattèrt.’  But eftèr A hae ris frae tha deid, A'll tak tha foreróad o ye ïntae Galilee.”  An Petèr saed tae hïm, “Tha mair tha rest'll faa awa, A'll no!”  “Petèr,” Jesus saed tae hïm, “A tell ye tha truith, afore thïs verie nicht's oot an tha roostèr craas twice, ye'll say thrie times ower that ye dïnnae ken me.”  “Na,” saed Petèr aa tha mair earnest, “no e'en ïf A hae tae dee wi ye! A wull niver deny ye!” An aa alang wi hïm vood tha same. An the' cum tae a place bi tha name o Gethsemane, an he saed tae hïs follaers, “Sït doon here til A gang an pray.”  An he tuk Petèr, Jeames an Jhone wi hïm, an a wile dhread an pooerfu hairt-sorra cum ower hïm.  An he saed tae thaim, “Ma hairt's brekkin wi ang'uish, near tae deith. Yous bide here an stye awaak.”  An gaun forrit a weethin he cast hissel tae tha grun, an he prayed that, ïf poassible, tha oor o sufferin micht gang bye hïm.  “Abba, Faither,” he saed, “Aa thïngs ir poassible wi you. Nocht's abain yer pooer. Tak awa thïs cup o sufferin frae me. Nane tha less, ït's your wull A'm wantin, an no ma ain.”  An he cum bak an he fun thaim sleepin, sae he saed tae Petèr, “Simon, ir ye sleepin! Cud ye no stye awaak even tha yin oor?  Watch an pray, sae ye dïnnae gie ïn tae temptation. Tha spïrit's wullin, but tha bodie's waik.”  An agane he gaed awa an he prayed tha same wurds,  an whaniver he cum bak, yinst mair he fun thaim sleepin, fer the' cudnae keep thair een apen, an the' dïdnae ken whut answer tae gie hïm.  Yit a thurd time he cum bak, an he saed tae thaim, “Ir yis aye sleepin, an aye takkin yer rest? That's eneuch noo! Luk, tha oor haes cum, an tha Sinn o Man ïs bethrayed ïntae tha hans o wrangdaers.  Git up noo, an we'll be aff! Here cums ma bethrayer!” Tha wurds wusnae richt aff hïs tung, whan up cum Judas, yin o tha Twal, an alang wi hïm wus a hale thrang o fowk wi swords an stavs, sent oot frae tha heid preeshts [an maistèrs o tha Laa] an tha eldèrs.  An tha traiter haed gien thaim a sign: “Hïm that A kïss,” saed he, “ïs tha man ye'r lukkin. Tak tha houl o hïm, an keep hïm weel gairded.”  As shuin as Judas cum, he gaed strecht up tae Jesus an he saed, “Rabbi!” an he kïsst hïm.  Then tha ithers tuk houl o Jesus an arrestit hïm.  An yin o thaim that stud bye tuk oot a sword an he hut tha sarvint o tha Heich Preesht, an he sneddit aff hïs lug.  Jesus saed tae thaim, “Am A some soart o a reiver that ye hae cum oot agin me wi swords an stavs fer tae tak me?  Shair A wus wi yis iverie day ïn tha Hoose o God, taichin ye, yit ye niver layed a han on me. But whut's writ ïn tha halie Scrïptures maun cum aboot.”  An tha hale lock o thaim left hïm an run awa. But thair wus a young man follaein hïm, wi nocht on hïm but a linen claith wrapt roon hïs nakit bodie, an the' tuk houl o hïm.  But he run aff scuddybare, leain tha claith ïn thair hans. An the' tuk Jesus awa tae tha Heich Preesht; an aa tha heid preeshts, tha eldèrs o tha fowk, an tha maistèrs o tha Laa wus gethert thegither.  An Petèr follaed hïm a lang wye behin, richt ïntae tha palace yaird; an he sut doon alang wi tha gairds, an wairmed hissel at tha apen fire.  Noo tha heid preeshts an tha hale Cooncil wus lukkin fer men at wud wutness agin Jesus, sae the' cud pit hïm tae deith. But the' cudnae fin onie.  Fer tha mair monies a yin wutnesst agin hïm, whut the' cum oot wi dïdnae cumpluthèr.  In tha enn, some o tha wutnesses stud up an saed, “We heerd hïm oorsels. He saed, ‘A'll pu doon thïs Hoose o God bigged bi man. An ïn thrie days A'll big anither yin, an ït'll no be tha han o man that bigs ït.’ ”  But thair stories dïdnae cumpluthèr.  An tha Heich Preesht ris tae hïs feet ïn tha mïddle o thaim aa. An he axt Jesus, “Hae ye nae answer tae these chairges? Whut hae ye tae say fer yersel?”  But Jesus hel hïs tung. Sae tha Heich Preesht püt anither question tae hïm, “Ir ye tha Christ, tha Sinn o tha Blissit Yin?”  An Jesus saed, “A am. An ye wull see me, tha Sinn o Man, saitit at tha richt han o tha Michtie Yin, an cumin ïn tha cloods o heiven.”  Wi that, tha Heich Preesht tore hïs claes, an saed, “Whut need hae we o onie mair wutnesses?  Yis hae aa heerd hïs blesphemie fer yersels. Whut dae yis jalouse o ït?” An the' aa saed he desarved tae be püt tae deith.  An some o thaim fell tae spïttin on hïm. The' püt a blinfoul on hïm, an hemmert hïm wi thair fïsts, sayin, “Tell iz wha hut ye!” An even tha gairds tuk tae slappin hïm wi tha flet o thair hans. Noo aa thïs time Petèr wus doon ïn tha coortyaird, an yin o tha Heich Preesht's sarvin lasses cum bye.  Seein Petèr wairmin hissel at tha fire, she tuk a guid luk at hïm an saed, “You wur wi Jesus frae Nazareth tae, sae ye wur!”  But Petèr wudnae own up tae ït. “A dïnnae ken whut ye'r taakin aboot,” saed he, an he slipt oot ïntae tha entrie. Jist then a roostèr craad.  An tha sarvin lass saen hïm agane, an yinst mair she stairtit tellin tha ithers hingin aboot, “Thair's nae doot thïs man's yin o thaim!”  Petèr denied ït yinst mair. An a wee while eftèr, tha yins roon aboot saed tae Petèr agane, “Ye maun be yin o thaim, fer [bi tha wye ye taak] ye ir frae Galilee.”  “As God's ma wutness,” saed Petèr, “A sweer A dïnnae ken thïs man!”  At that verie minnit, tha roostèr craad tha saicont time. An richt awa Petèr haed mine o tha wurds Jesus spauk tae hïm: “Afore tha roostèr craas twice, ye wull deny me thrie times.” At tha verie thocht o ït, he brauk doon an wep sair. At tha scraich o day, tha heid preeshts got thegither wi tha eldèrs an maistèrs o tha Laa, an tha hale Cooncil  taakt aboot whut the' wud dae nixt. The' tyed Jesus up an maircht hïm aff, an hannit hïm ower tae Pilate.  An Pilate axt hïm, “Ir you tha Kïng o tha Jews?” Jesus answert, “You hae saed ït.”  An tha heid preeshts brocht forrit monie chairges agin hïm, [but he niver saed a wurd bak.]  Sae Pilate axt hïm agane, “Ir ye no fer sayin ocht? Whut aboot aa these chairges brocht agin ye?”  But whaniver Jesus wud say naethin mair, Pilate wus quare an tuk bak. Noo iverie yeir at tha Passower Faist, Pilate uist tae let yin o tha prisners oot, whaiver tha fowk axt fer.  Yin o thaim at tha time, a man bi tha name o Barabbas, wus ïn fer murdèr alang wi ither rebels frae tha Risin agin tha Romans.  Tha thrang gaed up an the' axt Pilate tae let a prisner oot, as he aye daen yinst a yeir.  Pilate axt thaim, “Dae yis want me tae let oot tha ‘Kïng o tha Jews?’ ”  Fer he knowed richt weel ït wus jist oot o spite that tha heid preeshts haed hannit Jesus ower tae hïm.  But tha heid preeshts egged tha thrang on tae say, “Na, no Jesus! Let Barabbas oot!”  “Sae whut wull A dae then wi tha yin yis caa ‘Kïng o tha Jews’?” axt Pilate agane.  “Crucyfie hïm!” the' cryed oot.  “Whut fer? Whut's he daen wrang?” Pilate axt thaim. But tha thrang jist roared aa tha mair, “Crucyfie hïm!”  Noo, Pilate wus wantin tae plaise tha crood, sae he lut Barabbas oot tae thaim. He haed Jesus gien a guid whalin wi a whup, an then he hannit hïm ower fer tae be crucyfied. Tha sodgers tuk Jesus awa tae tha coortyaird o tha Guviner's Bïg Hoose , an the' brocht thegither tha hale regiment.  An the' rigged hïm oot ïn a purple robe, an the' plettit thoarns thegither ïntae a croon an the' püt ït on hïs heid.  An the' begoud tae salute hïm, cryin oot, “Lang leeve tha Kïng o tha Jews!”  The' hut hïm ower tha heid agane an agane wi a stav, an sput on hïm. The' got doon on thair knees afore hïm an lut on tae woarship hïm.  An eftèr the' haed daen makkin a mockerie o hïm, the' tuk tha purple robe aff hïm, an püt hïs ain claes bak on, an tuk hïm oot fer tae crucyfie hïm. Thair wus thïs man the' caad Simon frae Cyrene, tha faither o Alexander an Rufus, makkin hïs wye ïn frae tha kintrie. An the' gart hïm tae cairrie tha cross.  An the' brocht Jesus tae a place bi tha name o Golgotha, mainin “Tha Place o tha Skull.”  Then the' püt wine mixt wi myrrh tae hïs mooth, but he wudnae tak ït.  An tha sodgers nailt hïm tae tha cross. Then the' divïd hïs claes amang thaim bi cloddin dice, tae see wha wud get whut. It wus nine ïn tha moarnin whaniver the' crucyfied hïm.  An the' püt a signboord abain hïm wi tha chairge, “THA KING O THA JEWS” writ on ït.  The' crucyfied twa robbers alang wi hïm, yin on hïs richt han side, an tha tither on hïs left.  [An sae ït cum aboot laik tha Scrïptures saed aforehan: “He wus coontit amang tha laa brekkers.”]  Thaim at waakt bye yellt abuse at hïm, shakin thair heids an sayin, “Hey you, ye saed ye wur gaun tae desthroy tha Hoose o God, an big ït agane ïn thrie days,  sae cum doon aff that cross noo an save yersel!”  In tha same wye tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa mockt hïm an saed amang thairsels, “He saved ithers, but he cannae save hissel.  Thïs Christ, thïs kïng o Israel, shud cum doon aff that cross noo! Then we'll believe!” An tha twa that wus crucyfied alang wi Jesus hurlt abuse at hïm forbye. An dairkness cum ower tha hale lan frae nuin tae thrie ïn tha eftèrnuin.  An jist then, Jesus gien a lood cry, “Eli, Eli, lama sabachthani,” mainin, “Ma God, ma God, why hae ye forsook me?”  An some o tha yins stannin nearhan heerd thïs an saed, “Lïsten, he's caain oot fer Elijah!”  Yin o thaim run an wat a sponge wi soor wine, püt ït on a lang stïck, an hel ït up fer Jesus tae drïnk. “Lea hïm alane an we'll see ïf Elijah cums tae tak hïm doon,” qo he.  An wi anither lood cry Jesus gien hïs last breath.  Tha curtin ïn tha Halie o Halies wus tore ïn twa frae tap tae bottom.  An whaniver tha centurion  that stud fornent Jesus heerd hïm cryin oot an saen tha wye he deed, he saed, “Thair can be nae doot; thïs man wus tha Sinn o God!” Some weemen wus stannin awa bak takkin ït aa ïn; amang thaim wus Mary Magdalene, an Mary tha mither o young Jeames an o Joses, as weel as Salome.  These wur tha weemen that uist tae follae Jesus an luk eftèr hïm whaniver he wus bak ïn Galilee. An monie ither weemen that haed cum up wi hïm tae Jerusalem wur thair forbye. It wus Preparation Day - tha day afore tha Sabbath. Sae, as ït wus wearin on tae evenin,  Joseph o Arimathea, a man weel up ïn tha Cooncil, wha wus waitin on tha Kïngdom o God hissel, tuk hïs courage ïn hïs hans, an he went up tae Pilate fer tae ax fer tha bodie o Jesus.  Pilate wus fair tuk bak whan he heerd that Jesus wus aareadie deid. He caad tha centurion an axt hïm wus that richt.  Whaniver he heerd frae tha centurion that Jesus wus aareadie deid, he lut Joseph hae tha bodie.  Sae Joseph bocht some lïnen claith, tuk doon tha bodie, happt ït ïn tha claith, an layed ït ïn a tomb cut oot o tha roak. Then he rowlt tha stane agin tha apenin o tha tomb.  An Mary Magdalene, an Mary tha mither o Joses saa whar the' layed oot hïs bodie. Tha nixt evenin, whan tha Sabbath wus iver, Mary Magdalene an Salome an Mary tha mither o Jeames bocht sweet smellin oyles fer tae pit on Jesus' bodie.  On tha furst day o tha week, at tha scraich o day, jist as tha sin wus risin, the' cum tae tha tomb.  The' axt amang thairsels, “Wha's gaun tae rowl awa tha stane fer iz frae tha mooth o tha tomb?”  Whan the' lukt up, the' saa tha stane haed bin rowlt awa. It wus a pooerfu bïg stane.  Whaniver the' went ïntae tha tomb, the' saen a young man wi a white robe on hïm sïttin on tha richt han side, an the' wur thunnèrstruck.  “Dïnnae be sae feart!” he saed. “ Yis ir lukkin fer Jesus o Nazareth that the' crucyfied. He's ris. He's no here! Luk fer yersels - thïs ïs tha place whar the' layed hïm oot.  But gae noo an tell hïs follaers, an tell Petèr, that Jesus ïs awa on aheid o yis ïntae Galilee. Ye'll see hïm thonner, jist as he toul ye.”  Tha weemen cum oot frae tha tomb an tuk aff, trimmlin an dumfoonèrt. An the' niver saed ocht tae oniebodie, fer the' wur that feart. Noo whan Jesus ris on tha furst day o tha week, he showed hissel furst tae Mary Magdalene that he haed driv seiven wïckit spïrits oot o.  An she went an toul thaim that haed bin wi hïm that wur sair-hairtit an greetin.  Whan the' heerd that Jesus wus leevin agane, an that she haed saen hïm, the' dïdnae believe ït. An eftèr thïs Jesus appeart, lukkin dïffernt, tae twa o thaim waakin oot ïntae tha kintrie.  The' cum bak an toul tha ithers tae, but the' wudnae tak thair wurd fer ït ether. Latèr on, Jesus showed hissel tae tha Eleiven that wur aitin roon tha boord, an he chackt thaim fer no haein mair faith, an fer no bein wullin tae believe thaim that haed saen hïm eftèr he wus ris frae tha deid.  An he saed tae thaim, “Gang oot ïntae tha hale warl an praich tha Guid News tae aa mankine.  Oniebodie that believes an ïs baptised wull be saved, but oniebodie that daesnae believe wull be condemned.  Whariver believers gangs, these mïraclis signs wull gae alang wi thaim: ïn ma name the' wull drive oot ïll spïrits, an the'll spake wi ither leids;  the'll lïft snakes up wi thair hans, an ïf the' drïnk onie deidlie puzhion, ït'll no dae thaim onie hairm ava. The'll pit thair hans on seeck fowk an the'll get bettèr agane.” Eftèr tha Loard haed spauk tae thaim, he wus taen up ïntae heiven, an sut doon at tha richt han o God.  Then hïs follaers went oot praichin iveriewhar, an tha Loard wrocht alang wi thaim, an thair message wus bakt up wi mïraclis signs. Amen. Maist warthie Theophilus, A hale lock o fowk haes taen ït ïn han tae draa up an accoont o aa tha thïngs that haes cum aboot amang iz.  The' hae brocht thegither whut wus hannit doon tae iz frae yins that saa ït aa wi thair ain een richt frae tha stairt, an that becum sarvints o tha Wurd o God.  An sae, haein lukt ïntae ït aa masel richt frae whaniver tha hale storie begun, A thocht ït wud be a guid thïng fer me tae pit doon a trig accoont fer ye forbye, Theophilus, tae mak ye shair o tha truith o whut ye hae bin lairnt. Whaniver Herod wus Kïng o Judea, thair wus thïs preesht caad Zechariah. Noo he belanged til tha preeshtlie connection o Abijah; an hïs wife Lïzbeth, hir femlie went bak til tha dochtèrs o Aaron as weel.  An the' wur baith upricht ïn tha Loard's sicht, keepin aa tha commauns an laas o tha Loard.  But the' haed nae femlie, fer Lïzbeth cudnae hae weans; an tha baith o thaim wus weel up ïn yeirs. Yin time whan ït wus tha turn o Zechariah's connection fer daein thair dutie ïn tha Hoose o God,  Zechariah wus pïckt oot bi tha draain o lots - laik tha preeshts aye daen ïn thaim days - tae gang ïntae tha Halie o Halies an burn ïncense.  Noo whaniver tha time cum roon fer burnin tha ïncense, aa tha fowk wus ootbye, prayin.  An aa o a suddent an angel o tha Loard appeart, stannin on tha richt han side o tha althar o ïncense!  Zechariah wus tuk bak whan he saen tha angel an he wus hairt-scarred.  But tha angel saed, “Dïnnae be feart, Zechariah, fer God haes heerd yer prayer, an yer wife Lïzbeth wull gie ye a wee sinn! An ye maun caa hïm Jhone. Ye'll be quare an gled whan he's boarn, an sae wull a brave wheen o ither fowk alang wi ye. Fer he wull be ootstannin ïn tha sicht o tha Loard. He's no tae tak wine or onie ither kine o strang drïnk, an he'll be fu o tha Halie Spïrit richt frae hïs mither's wame. An he'll gether monie an Israelite bak tae tha Loard thair God. He wull be laik Elijah, fu o God's Spïrit an pooer; he wull saffen tha hairts o tha faithers tae thair weans, turnin contrairie yins tae a richt wye o thïnkin; an he wull gang afore tha Loard tae mak tha fowk readie fer hïm.” Zechariah axt tha angel, “Hoo cud A be shair whut ye'r sayin's richt? Fer baith me an tha wife ïs weel up ïn yeirs!”  Then tha angel saed, “A'm Gabriel. An A'm cum strecht frae God hissel fer tae gie ye thïs guid news.  Mairk thïs weel! Seein as ye niver believed whut A toul ye, ye'll be struck dum an no be fït tae taak tae tha wean's boarn. But thïs'll cum aboot ïn tha richt time.” Aa tha while, tha yins ootbye wus wunnèrin hoo cum Zechariah wus takkin sae lang ïn tha Loard's Hoose.  Whaniver he cum oot he cudnae say ocht ava, ner taak tae tha fowk. The' knowed bi tha signs he wus giein, he maun hae saen a vïsion ïn tha Hoose o tha Loard, but aa tha while he cudnae taak.  Bye an bye, whaniver he haed hïs turn at tha althar daen, he went bak hame. No lang eftèr that, Lïzbeth fun oot she wus gaun tae hae a wean, an sae she stapt ïn tha hoose oot o sicht fer five month.  “Tha Loard haes bin mair ner guid tae me,” Lïzbeth saed, “an A'm no affrontit onie lang'r wi haein nae femlie.” Whan Lïzbeth wus sïx month gan, God sent tha angel Gabriel tae tha toon o Nazareth ïn Galilee,  tae a virgin bi tha name o Mary that wus trystit tae a man caad Joseph, descendit frae Kïng Davit.  Tha angel saed til hir, “Fair faa ye, blisst amang weemen, tha Loard ïs wi ye.”  Mary wus aa throu hirsel as she tried tae mak sense o whut tha angel haed telt hir. “Dïnnae be feart, Mary,” tha angel saed, “fer ye hae fun favour wi God.  Tak tent, ye ir fer haein a wean, a sinn, an ye maun caa hïm Jesus. He wull be ootstannin, an be caad tha Sinn o tha Maist Heich God. An God wull gie hïm tha throne o hïs forefaither Davit, an he wull rule ower Israel fer iver an aye, an thair'll be nae enn tae hïs Kïngdom.” Mary axt tha angel, “Hoo can A hae a wean, wi me a virgin an niver bin wi a man?” Tha angel toul hir, “Tha Halie Spïrit an tha pooer o God wull cum doon on ye. An sae tha wean boarn tae ye wull be halie, an wull be caad tha Sinn o God. An yer cousin Lïzbeth ïs fer haein a sinn ïn hir oul age as weel, tha mair fowk thocht she cudnae hae onie; but she's ïn hir sïxth month.  Fer thair's naethin ava God cannae dae.”  Mary saed, “Weel, A'm tha sarvint o tha Loard an A'll dae whutiver he wants. Sae, jist let ït aa cum aboot laik ye say.” An then tha angel went awa frae hir. Eftèr thïs, Mary got hirsel readie, an heidit aff ïn a bïg hurrie tae a toon ïn tha hïlls o Judea.  Up she cum thonner tae Zechariah's hoose, an toul Lïzbeth ït wus guid tae see hir.  Whaniver Lïzbeth heerd tha soon o Mary's voice, tha bairn gien a lep ïn hir wame, an she wus fu o tha Halie Spïrit.  Lïzbeth caad oot wi a gled cry tae Mary, “Amang aa weemen ye'r blisst bi God, an blisst be tha wean ye'r fer haein!  But hoo cum ït's me haes bin gien sae bïg an honour, wi tha mither o ma Loard cumin tae vïsit me?  Tha mïnit A heerd yer wairm wurds, A cud feel tha bairn ïn ma wame giein a lep fer joy.  Ye ir ïn fer a blissin, Mary, fer ye dïdnae doot tha Loard wud dae jist whut he toul ye.” Then Mary saed, “Ma sowl gies praise tae tha Loard, an ma spïrit ïs gled ïn God ma Saviour! Fer he haes tuk notysh o me, a puir sarvin lass, an aa genèrations frae noo on wull caa me blisst. Tha Michtie Yin haes daen wunnèrfu thïngs fer me, an Halie ïs hïs name. Hïs mercie bides wi thaim that houls hïm ïn reverence, richt doon tha genèrations. Hoo pooerfu hïs michtie airm ïs, that can skail thaim that's fu o thairsels. He haes brocht doon tha michtie frae thair heich saits o pooer, an lïftit up tha doon-an-oots. He haes fed tha hung'rie wi guid thïngs, an he's turnt tha weel-aff yins bak empie-hannit. He haes lukt eftèr hïs sarvint Israel, an he niver fergets tae be merciefu. Fer he promist thïs tae oor faithers - tae Abraham an aa hïs childèr - fer iver an aye.” Then Mary stapt ower wi Lïzbeth fer aboot thrie month afore gaun bak hame. Noo whan Lïzbeth's time cum fer tha wean tae be boarn, she haed a wee sinn.  Wurd wusnae lang gaun roon o hoo guid tha Loard haed bin til hir, an hir freens an nighbers wus aa wile plaised.  Whaniver tha wean wus echt day oul, thair wus a guid turnoot o freens an nighbers at tha circumcisin, an the' wur aa wantin tae caa hïm eftèr hïs faither.  But “Na!” Lïzbeth saed, “He maun hae tha name o Jhone.”  “Whut!” the' saed, “Nane o yer femlie wus iver a Jhone.”  Sae the' axt tha wean's faither, bi makkin signs, whut he thocht tha name shud be.  He waved fer thaim tae get hïm sumthin tae write on, but the' wur aa tuk bak whan he püt thïs doon: “Hïs name ïs Jhone!”  Strecht aff Zechariah fun hïs tung an he stairtit giein praise tae God.  Aa tha fowk roon aboot wus dumfoonèrt, an ït wus tha taak o tha hale kintrieside o Judea.  An iveriebodie that heerd aboot ït wus wunnèrin whut wye thïs wee fella wud turn oot. Oniebodie cud see that tha han o tha Loard wus upon hïm. Then hïs faither Zechariah, fu o tha Halie Spïrit, stairtit makkin a proaphesie: “Praise tha Loard God o Israel, fer he haes cum doon amang hïs fowk an pyed tha coast o settin thaim free. Frae tha line o Davit's croon, he haes brocht iz a michtie Saviour, jist laik he saed he wud throu tha mooth o hïs halie proaphits, a lang while bak. Noo we wull be saved frae thaim that's agin aa we dae, an frae thaim that cannae stan iz. He haes showed mercie tae Abraham an tae aa oor forefaithers, bi haein mine o hïs halie coveynant. Sae noo we can sarve hïm wi'oot bein feart o thaim that's wantin tae hairm iz, wi us bein halie an ïn guid stannin ïn tha ee o tha Loard as lang as we leeve. An you, ma wee sinn, ye'll get caad ‘Tha proaphit o tha maist heich God’, fer ye'll mak tha wye readie fer tha cumin o tha Loard. Ye'll tell tha fowk hoo the' can get saved bi haein thair sïns forgien. Heiven's risin sin ïs jist aboot tae brek on iz, oot o tha guidness o God's hairt, giein licht tae thaim that sïts ïn tha dairk shedda o deith, an róadin iz ïntae tha pad o peace.” Jhone wus raired an he becum strang ïn spïrit, an he leeved oot ïn tha wuldèrness tae tha time cum tae stairt praichin tae Israel. Roon aboot thïs time tha Emperor, Caesar Augustus, gien oardèrs that a heid-coont wus tae be taen o aa tha fowk ïn iverie pairt o hïs empire.  Thïs wus tha furst coont daen whaniver Quirinius wus tha Guviner o Syria.  An iveriebodie wus haein tae gang tae whar the' wur boarn tae pit thair names doon fer ït.  Noo acause Joseph's femlie went bak tae Kïng Davit, he haed cum frae Nazareth ïn Galilee tae Bethlehem ïn Judea, whar Davit wus frae.  Mary, hïs wife tae be, trevelt wi hïm, tha mair o bein near hir time.  But whan the' wur thair, hir time cum tae hae tha wean.  An she haed hir furst babbie, a sinn. She rowlt hïm up ïn bïts o claith an püt hïm ïn a manger wi tha fother, acause thair wus nae ruim fer thaim ïn tha ludgin hoose. That nicht a wheen o herdmen wus oot ïn tha fiels mindin thair sheep.  Aa o a suddent, an angel o tha Loard cum amang thaim, an tha hale kintrie wus lichtit up bi tha glorie o tha Loard, an the' wur wile feart.  But tha angel saed, “Dïnnae be feart, fer A'm brïngin yis tha best news iver; an ït's fer tha hale warl!  Tha Saviour, ay, tha Christ, tha Loard, haes thïs nicht bin boarn ïn Bethlehem, tha toon o Davit.  An thïs ïs hoo ye'll ken hïm. Ye'll fin a babbie, rowlt ïn bïts o claith, lyin amang tha fother ïn a manger.”  An aa o a suddent thair wus a hale thrang o angels, tha airmies o heiven, praisin God an sayin,  “Glorie tae God ïn tha maist heich heiven, an peace on irth tae aa fowk that plaises hïm.” Whaniver tha angels went bak tae heiven, tha herdmen saed yin tae anither, “Cum on, we'll gang tae Bethlehem an see thïs wunnèrfu thïng that haes happent, that tha Loard haes toul iz aboot.”  The' hurriet aff an the' fun Mary an Joseph. An thair wus tha babbie lyin ïn tha manger!  Whaniver the' saen hïm, tha shepherds toul whut tha angel haed saed aboot thïs wean, an aa that haed happent.  An the' wur aa thunnèrstruck bi whut the' heerd frae tha shepherds.  Mary dïdnae say much, but she kep turnin these thïngs ower an ower ïn hir hairt.  Tha shepherds went bak tae hirdin thair sheep ïn tha fiels, praisin an giein glorie tae God fer whut the' haed saen an heerd. It haed bin jist tha wye tha angel haed toul thaim. Echt days on, whaniver the' circumcised tha wean, he wus gien tha name Jesus, tha name that tha angel saed tae caa hïm lang afore he wus boarn. Whan tha time cum roon fer Mary an Joseph tae dae whut tha Laa o Moses saed tae dae eftèr a wean's birth, the' tuk hïm tae tha Hoose o God ïn Jerusalem tae mak thair offerin an tae present hïm tae tha Loard.  Tha Laa o tha Loard saed that tha furst boarn wee fella aye belangs tae tha Loard.  As weel as thïs, tha Laa o tha Loard saed that the' haed tae offer a secryfice o twa turtle doos or twa young pïgeons. Noo thair wus thïs man ïn Jerusalem caad Simeon, that wus a guid, God-fearin man, fu o tha Halie Spïrit an lukkin forrit tae tha cumin o tha Messiah,  acause tha Halie Spïrit haed toul hïm that he wudnae dee afore he haed saen Christ tha Loard.  That day he wus guidit bi tha Halie Spïrit tae gang tae tha Hoose o God whan Mary an Joseph wus thair tae dae whut tha Laa saed. Whaniver he saa tha wean, he tuk hïm up ïn hïs airms an praised God an saed, “Noo A can dee contentit, fer A hae saen hïm jist as Ye saed. Fer ma een haes saen tha Saviour o tha warl, that ye sent fer yin an aa. Hïs licht wull shine on aa tha Gentiles, an he wull be tha glorie o Israel.” Jesus' faither an mither wus wile tuk bak at whut Simeon saed aboot thair wean.  Then Simeon gien thaim a blissin, an toul Mary tha mither tae tak heed o thïs: “Tha wean wull hae a pooerfu effect on monie a bodie ïn Israel. Some'll rise up an some wull faa. He ïs a sign frae God, but a lock o fowk wull hae naethin tae dae wi hïm.  Thïs wye aa tha thochts ïn fowks' hairts wull be oot ïn tha apen, an as fer you, Mary, sorra as shairp as a sword wull stab yer hairt.” Then thair wus a wee weeda wumman, echtie-fower yeir oul, caad Anna, that wus a proaphitess. She haed bin merriet tae hir man fer seiven yeir afore he deed. She wus a dochtèr o Phanuel o tha tribe o Asher. She wud stap ïn tha Hoose o God, prayin an fastin nicht an day,  an tae aa thaim that wus lukkin forrit tae Jerusalem bein set free, she kep on tellin thaim aboot tha wean. Eftèr Mary an Joseph haed cairriet oot aa that needit daen tae keep tha Laa, the' went bak hame tae tha toon o Nazareth ïn Galilee.  An as tha wean wus growein up, he wus strang, fu o wusdom an blisst bi God. Noo iverie yeir hïs faither an mither went tae Jerusalem fer tha Faist o tha Passower.  An whan he wus twal yeir oul, the' went up tae Jerusalem fer tha Faist, laik the' aye daen.  Whaniver tha Faist wus ower, hïs mither an faither set oot fer hame alang wi ither femlies, no knowin that Jesus haed styed behin ïn tha cïtie. The' jaloused he wus ïn tha companie, an the' trevelt on a hale day afore the' mïsst hïm.  Whan the' cudnae fin hïm amang thair femlie an freens, the' went bak tae Jerusalem tae luk fer hïm.  Sae ïn tha enn ït wus thrie days afore the' fun hïm. An thair he wus, sïttin ïn tha coortyaird o tha Hoose o God, takkin ïn whut tha taichers wur sayin, an quïzzin thaim.  Aa that heerd hïm cudnae believe tha wye he wus answerin an tha much he knowed.  Whan Mary an Joseph saen hïm the' wur dumfoonèrt, an hïs mither saed, “Wean dear, why hae ye daen thïs tae iz? Me an yer faither haes bin worriet seeck lukkin fer ye.”  “Why wur ye lukkin fer me?” he axt. “Dïd ye no ken that A maun be aboot ma Faither's bïzness here ïn hïs Hoose?”  But the' dïdnae unnèrstan whut he wus taakin aboot.  Jesus went bak doon tae Nazareth wi thaim an aye daen as he wus bïd, but Mary kep aa these thïngs ïn hir hairt. An Jesus growed up, wise an strang an weel plaisin tae God an man. Noo, whan Tiberius Caesar haed rult fer tha maist pairt o fïfteen yeir, Pontius Pilate wus tha Guviner o Judea, Herod wus tha Tetrarch ower Galilee, hïs brither Phïlip wus tha Tetrarch ower Iturea an Trachonitis, an Lysanias wus tha Tetrarch ower Abilene. An Annas an Caiaphas wus tha Heich Preeshts. At thïs time, God spauk tae Jhone, tha sinn o Zechariah, oot on tha muirs. Jhone gaed aa roon tha rïver Joardan, praichin an tellin tha fowk the' shud be baptised fer tae show the' haed turnt awa frae thair sïns, an tae show the' haed turnt tae God fer hïm tae forgie thaim.  Laik ye'll fin ïn tha buik o Isaiah tha proaphit, he spauk o Jhone whan he saed, “A voice ïs cryin oot ïn tha wiles: ‘Mak readie tha wye o tha Loard, mak hïs pads strecht fer hïm! Iverie glen wull be fïllt ïn; an iverie muntin an knowe levelt oot; an tha crookit wyes wull be makkit strecht, an tha reuch wyes makkit flet. An aa leevin fowk wull see tha savin pooer o God!’ ” Sae Jhone spauk tae tha thrang o fowk that cum oot tae get baptised wi hïm: “Ye sleekit shooer o vipers, wha telt ye tae rin frae tha wrath o God that's cumin?  Ye maun show bi tha wye ye leeve that ye hae turnt awa frae yer sïns. Dïnnae stairt sayin tae yersels, ‘We hae Abraham fer oor faither’, an hae daen wi that! Fer A tell ye that oot o thon stanes God can mak weans fer Abraham.  God's hatchit ïs noo hoverin at tha ruit o tha trees, an thaim that dïnnae gie guid fruit wull be fellt an pïtcht ïntae tha fire.” “Whut'll we dae then?” tha thrang wus axin hïm.  Jhone telt thaim, “Tha yin that haes twa shïfts shud gie yin tae hïm that haes nane, an tha yin that haes mait shud dae tha same.”  Tha tex men cum tae be baptised as weel, an the' axt Jhone, “Maistèr, whut ir we tae dae?”  An Jhone telt thaim, “Dïnnae ax fowk fer mair ner ye shud.”  An tha sodgers axt hïm, “Whut shud we dae?” Jhone saed til thaim, “Dïnnae squeeze tha last pennie oot o fowk, ner blekmail thaim fer thair siller; an mak dae wi whut ye get pyed an be gled o ït!” Aa tha fowk wus waitin an wunnèrin wus Jhone mebbe tha Christ.  But Jhone toul thaim aa, “A'm onlie baptisin wi wattèr. But yin'll cum that wull baptise ye wi tha Halie Spïrit an wi fire. He ïs michtier ner me. A'm no fït tae lowse hïs buits fer hïm.  Wi hïs winnowin fork ïn hïs han, he'll redd up hïs thrashin-flure, an gether tha wheat ïntae hïs barn; but he'll burn tha caff wi a fire ye cannae pit oot!” Jhone praicht tha Guid News ïn monies a wye tae aa tha fowk.  But he telt Herod tha Tetrarch ït wusnae richt tha wye he haed tuk Herodias, hïs brither Phïlip's guidwife, an he toul hïm aff fer aa tha ither wrang thïngs he haed daen as weel.  An warst o aa, Herod püt Jhone ïn jail. Whan aa tha fowk wus gettin baptised bi Jhone, Jesus wus baptised as weel. An whaniver he wus gettin baptised, he wus prayin, an tha heivens apent.  Tha Halie Spïrit cum doon on hïm laik a doo, an a voice cum frae heiven sayin, “Ye ir ma sinn, ma hairt's delicht, an A'm weel plaised wi ye.” An Jesus wus roon aboot thurtie yeir oul whan he stairtit hïs praichin an taichin. He wus - fowk thocht - tha sinn o Joseph, that wus tha sinn o Heli. An Heli wus tha sinn o Matthat. Matthat wus tha sinn o Levi. Levi wus tha sinn o Melki. Melki wus tha sinn o Jannai. Jannai wus tha sinn o Joseph. Joseph wus tha sinn o Mattathias. Mattathias wus tha sinn o Amos. Amos wus tha sinn o Nahum. Nahum wus tha sinn o Esli. Esli wus tha sinn o Naggai. Naggai wus tha sinn o Maath. Maath wus tha sinn o Mattathias. Mattathias wus tha sinn o Semein. Semein wus tha sinn o Josech. Josech wus tha sinn o Joda. Joda wus tha sinn o Jonan. Jonan wus tha sinn o Rhesa. Rhesa wus tha sinn o Zerubbabel. Zerubbabel wus tha sinn o Shealtiel. Shealtiel wus tha sinn o Neri. Neri wus tha sinn o Melki. Melki wus tha sinn o Addi. Addi wus tha sinn o Cosam. Cosam wus tha sinn o Elmadam. Elmadam wus tha sinn o Er. Er wus tha sinn o Joshua. Joshua wus tha sinn o Eliezer. Eliezer wus tha sinn o Jorim. Jorim wus tha sinn o Matthat. Matthat wus tha sinn o Levi. Levi wus tha sinn o Simeon. Simeon wus tha sinn o Judah. Judah wus tha sinn o Joseph. Joseph wus tha sinn o Jonam. Jonam wus tha sinn o Eliakim. Eliakim wus tha sinn o Melea. Melea wus tha sinn o Menna. Menna wus tha sinn o Mattatha. Mattatha wus tha sinn o Nathan. Nathan wus tha sinn o Davit. Davit wus tha sinn o Jesse. Jesse wus tha sinn o Obed. Obed wus tha sinn o Boaz. Boaz wus tha sinn o Salmon. Salmon wus tha sinn o Nahshon. Nahshon wus tha sinn o Amminadab. Amminadab wus tha sinn o Admin. Admin wus tha sinn o Arni. Arni wus tha sinn o Hezron. Hezron wus tha sinn o Perez. Perez wus tha sinn o Judah. Judah wus tha sinn o Jacob. Jacob wus tha sinn o Isaac. Isaac wus tha sinn o Abraham. Abraham wus tha sinn o Terah. Terah wus tha sinn o Nahor. Nahor wus tha sinn o Serug. Serug wus tha sinn o Reu. Reu wus tha sinn o Peleg. Peleg wus tha sinn o Eber. Eber wus tha sinn o Shelah. Shelah wus tha sinn o Cainan. Cainan wus tha sinn o Arphaxad. Arphaxad wus tha sinn o Shem. Shem wus tha sinn o Noah. Noah wus tha sinn o Lamech. Lamech wus tha sinn o Methuselah. Methuselah wus tha sinn o Enoch. Enoch wus tha sinn o Jared. Jared wus tha sinn o Mahalalel. Mahalalel wus tha sinn o Kenan. Kenan wus tha sinn o Enosh. Enosh wus tha sinn o Seth. Seth wus tha sinn o Adam. An Adam wus tha sinn o God. An Jesus, bein fu o tha Halie Spïrit, cum bak frae tha Joardan, an wus taen bi tha Spïrit ïntae tha wuldèrness.  Fer fowertie days he wus tempit bi tha Deil, an ïn aa thaim days he dïdnae ait ocht ava. An at tha enn o tha time, he wus gye hung'rie.  An tha Deil saed tae hïm, “If ye ir tha Sinn o God, tell that stane thair tae turn ïntae breid.”  An Jesus spauk bak tae hïm an saed, “It ïs writ doon, that man cannae leeve bi breid alane, [but bi iverie wurd o God].”  Then tha Deil tuk hïm up heich, an lut hïm see aa tha kïngdoms o tha warl ïn a weethin o time.  Tha Deil saed tae hïm, “Aa tha pooer o these kïngdoms A wull gie ye, an tha glorie that gangs wi thaim, fer ït's mine tae gie tae whaiver A laik.  Gin ye wull jist boo doon tae me, ït wull aa be yer ain.”  Jesus saed til hïm, “Awa or that, Satan! Fer tha Guid Buik says ye ir tae woarship tha Loard yer God, an tae sarve naebodie but hïm.”  An tha Deil brocht hïm tae Jerusalem, an tuk hïm up tae tha verie tap o tha Hoose o God, an saed tae hïm, “If ye ir tha Sinn o God, throw yersel doon frae here!  Fer tha Guid Buik says: ‘He wull tell hïs angels tae luk eftèr ye an keep an ee on ye.  Wi thair hans the' wull haud ye up, fer fear ye dunt yer fit agin a stane’.”  An Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “It's ïn tha Buik forbye: ‘Ye ir no tae temp tha Loard yer God!’ ”  An whan tha Deil haed stapt aa tha tempin, he tuk aff an lut hïm be fer a while. An Jesus cum bak ïn tha pooer o tha Spïrit ïntae Galilee; an he wus tha taak o tha hale kintrie roon aboot.  An he taicht ïn thair Meetin Hooses, an he haed a great name amang thaim aa. An he cum tae Nazareth, whar he haed bin raired; an as he aye daen, he went ïntae tha Meetin Hoose on tha Sabbath day, an stud up fer tae read.  The' gien hïm tha screed o tha proaphit Isaiah, an whan he haed apent tha buik, he fun tha place whar ït wus writ doon:  “Tha Spïrit o tha Loard ïs cum ower me, fer he haes anointit me tae tell oot tha Guid News tae tha puir; he haes sent me fer [tae hail tha hairtbrauk], tae lowse thaim that's bun, tae gie sicht tae tha blin, fer tae set free thaim that's trod doon,  an fer tae praich tha yeir o tha Loard's grace.” Whan Jesus haed rowlt up tha screed, he gien ït bak tae tha man ïn chairge, an he sut doon. An naebodie ïn tha Meetin Hoose cud tak thair een aff hïm.  An he stairtit aff bi tellin thaim, “Whut ye hae jist heerd frae tha Guid Buik haes cum aboot theday.”  An aa spauk weel o hïm, an the' cud harlie tak ïn tha wunsum wurds that cum oot o hïs mooth. “Is thïs no Joseph's sinn?” the' axt.  He telt thaim thïs, “Nae doot Ye wull quote tha oul saw at me - ‘Doctèr, hail yersel!’ An ye'll say, ‘Whut we heerd ye daen ïn Capernaum, dae ït here ïn yer ain hametoon as weel.’ ”  An he saed, “A warrant ye thïs: nae proaphit ïs iver walcum ïn hïs ain hametoon.  A'm tellin ye tha truith, ïn tha days o Elijah, tha heivens wus shut up fer thrie yeir an sïx month, an thair wus a bïg hung'r ower aa tha lan. An thair wus monie weedas ïn Israel at tha time.  Elijah wusnae sent til onie o thaim but, onlie tae a weeda wumman ïn Serepta, near tha toon o Sidon.  Forbye, thair wus monie lepers ïn Israel ïn tha time o Elisha tha proaphit, but nane o thaim wus makkit clain, apairt frae Naaman frae Syria.”  Whaniver the' heerd these thïngs, aa tha fowk ïn tha Meetin Hoose wus wile ang'rie.  An the' ris up, an the' driv hïm oot o tha toon, an the' tuk hïm up tae tha broo o tha hïll whar tha toon wus bigged, fer tae throw hïm doon heid furst.  But he passt richt throu tha mïddle o thaim, an gaed on hïs wye. Then Jesus went on doon tae Capernaum, a toon o Galilee. An he wus taichin tha fowk thair on tha Sabbath day.  An the' wur aa thunnèrstruck wi hïs taichin, fer tha wurds he spauk wus pooerfu.  An ïn tha Meetin Hoose, thair wus a man that haed a demon, an ïll spïrit, ïn hïm. An he scraicht oot lood,  “Hey! [Lea iz alane], Jesus o Nazareth! Whut dae ye want wi iz? Hae ye cum here tae dae awa wi iz? A ken richt weel wha ye ir. Ye ir tha Halie Yin o God!”  But Jesus chackt hïm an saed, “Houl yer wheesht, an cum oot o hïm!” An tha demon throwed hïm tae tha grun fornent thaim aa, an ït cum oot o hïm, an ït dïdnae hurt hïm ava.  An the' wur aa dumfoonèrt, an taakt amang thairsels, an saed, “Dïd ye iver hear tha laik o ït? Fer wi thortie an pooer he oardèrs tha ïll spïrits, an at hïs bïddin the' cum oot!”  Sae Jesus wus tha taak o tha hale kintrieside roon aboot. An he gaed oot o tha Meetin Hoose an on tae Simon's hame. Noo Simon's guidwife's mither wus wile baad wi a faivir, an the' axt Jesus fer tae mak hir bettèr.  He stud ower hir, an he chackt tha faivir, an ït left hir. She got up at yinst an stairtit tae sarve an luk eftèr thaim. Noo whan tha sin wus gaun doon, aa tha yins that haed seeck fowk wi aa kines o disaises brocht thaim tae Jesus; an he püt hïs hans on iverie yin o thaim, an hailt thaim.  Forbye, demons cum oot o monie o thaim, cryin oot, “Ye ir [Christ,] tha Sinn o God!” An he wud chack thaim, oardèrin thaim no tae spake, fer the' kent that he wus tha Christ. Whan ït wus daylicht, he depairtit an went tae a place he cud be on hïs ain. An tha fowk lukt fer hïm, an cum tae hïm, an axt hïm fer tae stye, fer the' dïdnae want hïm tae lea thaim.  But he saed tae thaim, “A maun praich tha Guid News o tha Kïngdom o God tae tha ither toons as weel; fer that's why A wus sent.”  Sae he kep on praichin ïn tha Meetin Hooses o Galilee Yin day, Jesus wus stannin bi tha Loch o Gennesaret , an aa tha fowk wus croodit roon hïm, püshin an shuvin fer tae hear tha Wurd o God.  An he saa twa bóats pued up bi tha wattèr's edge. But tha fïshermen wus awa oot o thaim, an the' wur waashin thair neyts.  An Jesus got ïntae yin o tha bóats, whut belanged tae Simon, an axt hïm tae pit oot a weethin frae tha lan. An he sut doon an taicht tha fowk frae tha bóat.  Noo whan he haed daen taakin tae tha fowk, he toul Simon, “Pit oot tae tha deep wattèr, an let doon yer neyts fer a haal.”  Simon saed, “Dominie, we hae wrocht aa nicht an tuk naethin. But nanethaless, A'll dae as ye bïd me an let doon tha neyts.”  An whan the' haed daen thïs, the' catched a pooerfu lock o fïsh. Thair wus that monie that tha nettin stairtit tae cum apairt.  Sae the' waved tae thair nighbers ïn tha ither bóat tae cum an gie thaim a han, an the' fïllt baith bóats sae fu that the' near sunk.  Whaniver Simon Petèr saa thïs, he faad on hïs knees afore Jesus an saed, “G'awa frae me, Loard, fer A'm a sïnfu man.”  Whaniver hïm an aa that wur wi hïm saa tha haal o fïsh, the' cud harlie tak ït ïn.  An nether cud Jeames an Jhone, tha sinns o Zebedee, that wur nighberin wi Simon. Jesus saed tae Simon, “Dïnnae be feart. Frae noo on, ït's men ye'll be ketchin.”  Whaniver the' haed brocht thair bóats tae lan, the' left aa an the' follaed eftèr Jesus. Anither time, whan Jesus wus ïn yin o tha toons, thair wus thïs man wile baad wi leprosie. Whaniver he saen Jesus he faad doon afore hïm an begged hïm, “Loard, ïf ye hae a mine tae, ye can mak me clain.”  An he püt hïs han oot an toucht hïm, sayin, “A wull shairlie. Be clain!” An richt awa tha leprosie wus gan frae hïm.  An he chairged hïm tae tell naebodie, but bïd hïm gang an show hissel tae tha preesht. “Gie an offerin fer yer cleansin,” saed Jesus, “as Moses telt iz ïn tha Laa, fer a wutness tae yin an aa that ye'r weel agane!”  But fer aa thïs, tha hale kintrieside taakt aboot hïm aa tha mair, an cum tae hear hïm ïn thair droves, an tae be cured o thair ailments.  Then Jesus tuk hissel awa frae thaim ïntae a quait place fer tae pray, as he wus ïn tha habit o daein. Anither day, as he wus lairnin tha fowk, thair wus Pharisees an taichers o tha Laa sïttin bye. The' haed cum frae aa tha vïllages roon aboot, oot o Galilee, an Judea an Jerusalem, an tha pooer o tha Loard wus thair fer tae hail thaim.  An luk see! - a wheen o men wus brïngin a paralysed man on a bed; an the' wur lukkin fer a wye fer tae brïng hïm ïntae tha hoose tae lay hïm doon afore Jesus.  An whan the' cudnae fin a róad ïn acause o aa tha thrang, the' went up on tae tha tap o tha hoose, an lut hïm doon on hïs bed throu tha ruif, ïn amang tha fowk, richt fornent Jesus.
