An whaniver he wus cum near til Bethphage an Bethanie, nixt tha hïll caad tha Moont o Olives, he sent on twa o hïs follaers,  sayin tae thaim, “Awa ïntae thon clachan fornent iz. Whan yis git thair, ye'll fin a cowlt tyed up, that naebodie haes iver sut on. Lowse ïts raip, an brïng ït til me.  If onie yin axes yis hoo cum yis ir lowsin tha cowlt, jist tell thaim, ‘Tha Loard haes need o ït!’ ”  Noo tha twa that went fun ït jist as the' haed bin toul.  An as the' wur lowsin tha cowlt, tha yins ït belanged tae axt thaim, “Whut ir ye daein, lowsin that cowlt?”  Saed tha twa, “Tha Loard haes want o ït!” An the' brocht ït tae Jesus. An pittin thair claes on tha cowlt's bak, the' tuk houl o ït tae Jesus got on.  Wi that, as Jesus made hïs wye alang, tha fowk spreed thair claes doon afore hïm on tha pad.  An whaniver he wus cumin nearhan tha pad doon frae tha Moont o Olives, hïs follaers stairtit shoutin oot wi joy tha hale lock o thaim, praisin God fer aa tha mïracles the' haed saen, an cryin oot,  “Blisst ïs tha Kïng that cums ïn tha name o tha Loard. Peace ïn heiven abain, an glorie ïn tha heichest!”  An some o tha Pharisees amang tha thrang saed tae Jesus, “Maistèr, scoul yer follaers an tell thaim tae quït ït!”  But he cum bak wi thïs: “A'm tellin yis, ïf they ir quait, e'en tha stanes thairsels wull cry oot!” Jesus wus cumin near tae Jerusalem noo, an whan he saa tha cïtie, he begun tae greet, an he saed,  “Och, ïf ye onlie haed hae knowed whut wud brïng ye peace tha day! But na, ye dïdnae, an noo ït's hïd frae yer een.  Fer tha time wull cum whan thaim that's agin ye wull big dykes aa roon ye, an fence ye ïn frae aa sides.  Ye'll be flettent ïntae tha grun, an aa yer fowk alang wi ye. The'll no lea yin stane on anither, fer ye dïdnae ken tha day that God cum tae ye.” An yinst he got tae Jerusalem, whut Jesus daen wus thïs: he went strecht ïntae tha Hoose o God, an he begun reddin oot tha dailers frae tha coortyaird.  “It ïs writ doon,” he saed tae thaim, “that ‘ma hoose wull be a hoose o prayer.’ But yous hae turnt ït ïntae a den o robbers!” An eftèr that, iverie day, Jesus stairtit lairnin tha fowk ïn tha Hoose o God. An tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa, alang wi tha heidyins amang tha fowk, the' wur oot tae get rïd o hïm,  but the' cud dae naethin aboot ït, fer he wusnae iver on hïs lane; an aa tha fowk hung on hïs iverie wurd. On yin o thaim days, as Jesus wus lairnin tha fowk that wur ïn tha Hoose o God, an praichin tha Guid News, tha heid preeshts, tha maistèrs o tha Laa, an tha eldèrs amang tha fowk cum up tae hïm  an saed, “Tell iz thïs, bi whut thortie ir ye daein these thïngs, an wha gien ye ït?”  An he cum bak wi, “A hae a question tae ax you as weel. Jist tell me thïs,  Jhone's baptisin, wus ït frae heiven, or wus ït jist a notion o man?”  An the' taakt aboot ït tae yin anither, an saed, “If we gie tha answer, ‘Frae heiven’, he wull say, ‘Hoo cum yis dïdnae believe hïm then?’  But ïf we say, ‘Frae men’, aa tha fowk wull clod iz wi stanes, fer the' hae nae doot that Jhone wus a proaphit!”  Sae the' toul hïm that the' cudnae tell whar Jhone's baptisin haed cum frae.  An Jesus saed tae thaim, “Then A'll no be tellin yis ether bi whut thortie A dae these thïngs!” He turnt tae tha fowk an toul thaim thïs parable: “Thair wus thïs man plantit a vineyaird an he set ït tae a wheen o tenant-fairmers tae rin, afore gaun awa fer a lang time tae anither kintrie.  An whaniver hairst time cum roon, he sent a sarvin man tae tha fairmers, tae get a taste o tha fruit frae thaim, but the' bate up tha sarvin man an chaist hïm awa empie-hannit.  Sae he sent anither sarvin man, but the' creesht hïm as weel, wur wile baad til hïm, an sent hïm awa wi naethin.  Agane he sent anither yin oot, an the' hurt hïm an flung hïm oot tae.  Then tha laird o tha vineyaird saed, ‘Whut wull A dae? A know, A'll senn ma ain sinn that A love. The' ir shair tae hae regaird fer hïm!’  But whaniver tha tenant-fairmers saen tha sinn, the' taakt ït ower an saed, ‘Thïs ïs tha boy that wull git aa thïs here whan hïs da dees. If we kïll hïm, aa thïs cud be oors!’  Sae the' püt hïm oot o tha vineyaird, an kïllt hïm.” An Jesus axt, “Whut dae yis thïnk tha laird wull dae on thaim noo?  A'll tell yis. He wull cum an desthroy thaim fairmers an set tha vineyaird tae ithers.” Whan tha fowk lïstenin tae Jesus heerd thïs, the' saed, “Thïs shud niver cum aboot!”  But Jesus lukt at thaim strecht ïn tha ee an axt, “Whut then ïs tha mainin o thïs Scrïpture: ‘Tha verie stane tha masons turnt doon Is noo tha coarner stane’? Aa tha yins that faa ower thon stane wull be smesht tae bïts; an whaiver ït faas on wull be grun tae poodèr.” Tha maistèrs o tha Laa an tha heid preeshts lukt fer a wye tae tak houl o hïm thair an then, fer the' kent he haed spauk agin thaim ïn thïs parable. But the' wur feart o whut tha fowk wud dae.  Keepin a quare clase ee on hïm, the' sent yins that lut on the' wur honest, fer tae spie on hïm. The' wur hopin tae ketch hïm oot ïn sumthin he saed, fer the' wantit tae be able tae han hïm ower tae tha pooer o tha Roman Guviner.  These yins that wur spiein on Jesus axt hïm, sayin, “Maistèr, ye taak an taich whut ïs richt. Ye dïnnae mak o yin mair ner tha ither, but ye taich God's wye an tha truith. Tell iz, ïs ït richt fer iz tae pye tex tae Caesar or no?”  But Jesus saa throu thaim an he saed, “[Dïnnae try me oot.] Let me see a denarius.  Noo, whase name an laikness ïs on ït?”  “It's Caesar's,” the' saed. “Then gie Caesar whut belangs tae Caesar,” saed he, “an gie God whut belangs tae God.”  That settelt thaim. The' wurnae able tae ketch hïm oot afore tha fowk fer whut he haed saed. An the' haed tae be quait, fer hïs answer flebbergestit thaim. An sartin Sadducees - thaim that say thair ïsnae onie risin frae tha deid - the' cum an pit a question tae Jesus.  “Maistèr,” the' saed, “Moses writ doon fer iz, that ïf a man's brither dees an leas a guidwife wi nae weans, then he maun merrie tha weeda an hae childèr fer hïs deid brither.  Noo, whut ïf thair wus seiven brithers. Tha oulest gets merriet, an he dees wi'oot haein onie weans.  Sae tha saicont brither, he merries tha weeda, an he dees as weel. Still nae weans.  An tha thurd merries hir, an ïn tha same wye aa seiven brithers merries hir an dees, leain nae femlie ava.  An ïn tha enn tha wumman, she deed as weel.  Noo at tha risin frae tha deid, whase guidwife wull she be, fer she wus merriet on tha hale seiven o thaim?” Jesus cum bak wi thïs: “Men an weemen o thïs warl get merriet.  But thaim that ir coontit fït tae be pairt o tha risin frae tha deid an tha nixt warl, thair wull be nae mair merryin fer thaim.  The'll be laik tha angels an the' cannae dee; the' ir childèr o God an childèr o tha risin frae tha deid.  But even Moses - whaniver he writ aboot tha burnin büsh - he showed that tha deid rises agane, fer he caas tha Loard ‘tha God o Abraham, an tha God o Isaac, an tha God o Jacob’, lang eftèr the' wur aa deid!  He's no tha God o tha deid; he's tha God o tha leevin, fer iveriebodie's leevin ïn God's een.”  An some o tha maistèrs o tha Laa saed, “Weel spauk, Maistèr!”  But naebodie ava wud dar ax hïm onie mair questions. Then Jesus axt thaim, “Hoo can the' mak oot that tha Messiah  ïs tha sinn o Davit?  Fer Davit hissel says ïn tha buik o Psaums: ‘Tha Loard saed tae ma Loard, Sït doon at ma richt han,  tae A mak o yer enemies a stool fer unnèr yer fit.’  Sae Davit caas tha Messiah ‘ma Loard’. Hoo can he be hïs sinn then?” Whaniver aa tha fowk wus lïstenin, Jesus saed tae hïs follaers,  “Dïnnae tak heed o tha maistèrs o tha Laa, fer the' ir fand o paradin aboot ïn fancie robes, an the' love fowk tae touch thair keps tae thaim ïn tha mairket places. The' laik tae hae tha best saits ïn tha Meetin Hooses, an tae be at tha tap table at faists.  The' halp thairsels bi daein weeda weemen oot o aa the' hae. An the' mak lang screeds o prayers jist fer show. But yis can be shair ït wull gang waur wi thaim on tha Day o Reckonin.” Jesus lukt up an saa tha weel-aff fowk pittin thair offerins ïntae tha kïst ïn tha Hoose o God.  Then he saen thïs puir weeda wumman drappin ïn twa pennies.  “A'm tellin yis tha truith,” qo he, “Thïs puir weeda haes gien mair ner onie o tha rest o thaim.  Aa these yins hae onlie gien a pïttance oot o thair pruch ïntae tha kïst, but thïs weeda, puir an aa that she ïs, haes gien aa she haed tae leeve on.” Some o thaimins that wur wi hïm wur taakin amang thairsels aboot tha wye tha Hoose o God wus aa daen up, wi ïts bricht bonnie stanes, an coastlie ornyments gien ïn bi fowk.  But Jesus saed, “Tha day wull cum whan aa these stanes wull be tummelt doon, an no yin stane wull be left abain tha ither.”  An the' axt hïm, “Maistèr, whan's aa thïs fer happenin then? An wull we hae onie sign o ït cumin?”  Jesus cum bak wi thïs: “Tak heed an dïnnae let oniebodie lead yis aglee, fer monies a yin wull cum ïn ma name sayin, ‘A be tha Christ’, or ‘Tha time ïs cum.’ Dïnnae pye thaim onie heed.  Whan yis hear tell o wars an fechtin, dïnnae be feart, fer sitch thïngs maun cum aboot furst, but tha enn ïs no near jist yit.” Then he saed tae thaim, “Nations wull mak war on ither nations, an kïngdoms wull rise up agin ither kïngdoms.  Thair wull be michtie irthquakes, dirths an plagues ïn dïffernt pairts, an fleysum sichts, an pooerfu signs frae heiven.  Hooaniver, afore aa thïs cums aboot, the'll be takkin houl o yis, persecutin yis an turnin yis ïn at tha Meetin Hooses. The'll clod yis ïntae jail an dreg yis up afore kïngs an guviners, jist fer bein ma follaers.  Thïs'll be yer chaunce tae wutness tae yin an aa.  Sae pit yer mine tae ït then, an dïnnae fash yersels aforehan aboot whut kine o answer yis ir gaun tae gie.  Fer A wull pit tha richt wurds ïn yer mooth, an gie yis tha wut tae uise thaim, sae nane o yer enemies wull be able tae stan up tae yis, or say a wurd agin yis.  Yis'll even be hannit ower bi thaim that ïs clase tae yis: yer mither an faither, yer brithers, yer freens an nighbers. An some o yis wull be kïllt.  An yis'll be haitit bi aa fowk on accoont o me.  But no e'en yin hair o yer heid wull cum tae onie hairm.  Dïnnae gie up, thole aa that cums at ye, an yis'll fin rael life. Noo whan yis see tha airmies gethert aa roon Jerusalem, then yis wull ken that tha time fer ït tae be tummelt doon ïs nearhan.  Then thaim at's ïn Judea maun tak tae tha hïlls, an thaim at's ïn Jerusalem maun flee oot o ït, an thaim at's ootside tha cïtie shudnae try tae get ïn.  Fer that'll be tha day o God's punishment, an whut wus foretoul bi tha proaphits maun cum aboot.  In thaim days ït'll be tarrible fer weemen that's expectin, an fer mithers wi weans at tha breesht. Thair'll be a wile baad time o sufferin aa ower tha lan, an God's ang'r wull be agin thïs fowk.  Some o thaim wull be kïllt bi tha sword; ithers'll be tuk awa an skailt amang aa tha nations o tha warl. An Jerusalem wull be thrampt doon bi haithen feet, tae tha time o tha Gentiles cums tae an enn. Thair'll be quare signs ïn tha sin an tha muin an tha starns. An doon here on tha irth, tha fowk o aa tha nations wull be hairt-scarred an at thair wuts' enn wi tha souch o tha roarin sea an tha waves.  Fowk'll be that feart, the'll be takkin dwams acause o whut the' see cumin on tha warl. Fer tha verie pooers o tha lïft wull be shuk oot o kïlter.  An then aa fowk wull see tha Sinn o Man cumin ïn a clood wi aa hïs pooer an muckle glorie.  Whaniver aa these thïngs stairts tae cum aboot, stan up strecht, lïft up yer heids, fer yis'll shuin be delïvert oot o hairm's wye.” An he toul thaim thïs parable: “Tak a luk at tha fïg tree, or onie ither tree.  Whan tha leafs cum oot, yis ken wi'oot bein toul, tha simmer's no faur aff.  Sae, whan yis see these thïngs happenin, yis can be shair tha Kïngdom o God ïs nearhan. A tell yis tha truith, thair's fowks leevin noo that'll no dee, afore aa these thïngs haes cum aboot!  Heiven an irth wull pass awa, but ma wurds wull niver pass awa. Tak care yis ir no bluthert, or yer heids turnt wi wile leevin. An dïnnae fash yersels aboot tha worries o thïs life. Dïnnae alloo that day tae cum doon on yis o a suddent, laik a thrap wud dae.  Fer thon day wull cum on iveriebodie leevin ïn tha hale warl.  Sae aye keep an ee oot then, an pray yis micht be strang eneuch tae stan afore tha Sinn o Man, an be spared aa these thïngs that ir gaun tae happen.” Iverie day, Jesus went tae tha Hoose o God tae taich tha fowk, but he spent iverie nicht on tha Moont o Olives.  An aa tha fowk cum at tha furst licht tae lïsten tae hïm ïn tha Hoose o God. Noo tha Faist o Bairmless Breid, caad tha Passower, wus nearhan.  An tha heid preeshts an maistèrs o tha Laa wus colloguin thegither hoo tae get rïd o Jesus on tha quait, fer the' wur feart o whut tha fowk micht dae. Then Satan cum ïntae tha hairt o Judas, tha yin caad Iscariot, that wus yin o tha Twal;  an Judas went tae tha heid preeshts an offyshers o tha Temple gaird an taakt aboot hoo he micht han Jesus ower tae thaim.  The' wur weel plaised, an struck a dail wi hïm, tae gie hïm siller fer hïs wark.  Sae Judas made a paction, an he lukt fer a guid apenin tae han Jesus ower tae thaim, whaniver thair wus nae crood aboot. Noo tha Day o Bairmless Breid cum alang, whan tha lambs wus kïllt fer tha Passower.  An Jesus bïd Petèr an Jhone tae gang on aheid, fer tae mak readie tha Passower mail fer thaim tae ait thegither.  The' axt hïm, “Whar wud ye hae iz mak ït readie?”  An he saed tae thaim, “Tha mïnit yis cum ïntae tha cïtie, a man cairryin a crockerie jar o wattèr wull meet yis. Follae hïm tae tha hoose he gangs ïntae,  an say tae tha guidman o tha hoose, ‘Tha Maistèr says: Whar ïs tha ruim whar A can ait tha Passower wi ma follaers?’  An he wull show yis a bïg upstair ruim, plenisht an aa. Yis ir tae mak ït readie thair.”  The' went an the' fun ït jist as he haed saed. An the' made readie tha boord fer tha Passower mail. An whaniver tha time cum tae stairt, Jesus tuk hïs place at tha boord, an tha possels alang wi hïm.  An he saed tae thaim, “A hae bin langin wi aa ma hairt tae ait thïs Passower mail wi yis, afore A suffer.  Fer A'm tellin yis aa noo, A'll no ait ït agane tae tha Kïngdom o God ïs cum.”  Then he tuk tha bicker ïn hïs hans, gien thenks tae God, an saed, “Tak thïs, an shair ït oot amang yis.  Fer A tell yis thïs: frae noo on, A'll no drïnk o tha fruit o tha vine afore tha Kïngdom o God haes cum.”  An he tuk tha breid as weel, an whaniver he haed gien thenks tae God, he brauk ït, an hannit ït tae thaim, an saed, “Thïs ïs ma bodie [gien fer you. Dae thïs ïn mine o me.”  In tha same wye, eftèr supper he tuk tha bicker o wine an saed, “Thïs bicker ïs a sign o God's new coveynant sealed wi ma bluid, poored oot fer you.]  But tak heed, tha yin that's gaun tae gie me up ïs at tha boord alang wi me.  Fer masel, tha Sinn o Man, A maun dee accoardin tae God's plan. But wile sorra tae tha yin that bethrays me!”  Then the' begun tae taak amang thairsels, axin whutch yin o thaim wud dae sitch an a thïng. An thair wus a thraw on amang thaim, as tae whut yin o thaim shud be tha maist heich.  Jesus toul thaim, “Amang tha Gentiles, kïngs laird ït ower thair ain fowk, an thair heidyins gets tha name o daein guid.  But wi yous, ït's no tae be laik that. Amang yous, tha maist heich shud be laik tha maist hummle, an a heidyin shud be laik a sarvint.  Fer whut yin's mair impoartin amang yis, hïm that's sïttin at tha boord, or tha yin that sarves hïm? Is ït no tha yin that's at tha boord? Ay, ye wud thïnk that wud be richt. But no here! Fer A am amang yis as yin that sarves. Yous ir tha yins that hae stud bye me ïn reuch times.  An jist as ma Faither haes gien a Kïngdom tae me, sae A masel wull gie you tha richt tae ait an drïnk at tha boord ïn ma Kïngdom. An yis'll sït doon on thrones an judge tha twal clans o Israel.” An wi that, he went on tae say, “Simon, Simon, lïsten tae me! Satan haes axt tae hae yis aa, fer tae rïddle ye as wheat.  But A hae prayed fer ye, Simon, that yer faith wull houl oot. An whan ye hae turnt bak tae me, ye ir tae haud up yer brithers.”  An Petèr saed, “Loard, A'm readie tae gang tae jail wi ye, or e'en tae dee wi ye.”  “A'm tellin ye, Petèr,” saed Jesus, “tha roostèr wull no craa themorra moarnin, afore ye hae saed thrie times ower that ye dïnnae ken me.” An he went on tae say tae thaim aa, “Whan A sent yis oot wi nae pooch, nae baag, an nae shune, dïd yis want fer ocht?” An the' saed, “Naethin ava!”  “But noo,” saed Jesus, “If yis hae a pooch or a baag, tak thaim wi yis. An ïf ye hinnae a sword, sell tha cóat aff yer bak, an buy yin.  It's writ doon ïn tha Scrïptures: ‘He wus coontit amang tha laa brekkers.’ An A tell yis that whut wus writ doon thair aboot me maun cum aboot. Deed ay, ït wull aa cum aboot.”  An the' saed, “Loard, here's twa swords.” Saed he bak tae thaim, “That'll dae!” An Jesus cum oot o tha hoose an made hïs róad tae tha Moont o Olives, as he wus ïn tha habit o daein. An hïs follaers went alang wi hïm.  Whan he got tae tha place, he toul thaim, “Pray that whan ye ir tempit, ye dïnnae gie ïn tae ït.”  He went awa as faur as ye cud clod a stane, an he got doon on hïs knees an prayed,  sayin, “Faither, ïf ye ir wullin, wud ye tak thïs cup o sufferin awa frae me? Aa tha same, no ma wull, but yours be daen.”  [Then an angel frae heiven appeart til hïm, an gien hïm strenth.  An bein ïn a wile agonie, Jesus prayed mair an mair frae tha hairt, tae tha sweit wus faain aff hïm tae tha grun, laik bïg draps o bluid.]  Whan he wus daen prayin, he got ontae hïs feet an went bak tae hïs follaers. He fun thaim sleepin, aa wore oot wi sorra.  An he saed tae thaim, “Whut ir yis sleepin fer? Git up an pray, less ye gie ïn tae temptation!” Tha wurds wus harlie oot o hïs mooth, whan up cum a hale thrang o fowk. An Judas, yin o tha Twal, wus at tha heid o thaim. He waakit up tae Jesus, an he gien hïm a kïss o greetin.  But Jesus saed tae hïm, “Judas, wud ye bethray tha Sinn o Man wi a kïss?”  Whan Jesus' ither follaers saa whut wus aboot tae happen, the' saed, “Loard, shud we tak oor swords tae thaim?”  An yin o thaim hut tha sarvint o tha Heich Preesht, an he sneddit hïs richt lug aff.  But Jesus saed, “Houl on! Nae mair o that!” An he püt hïs han on tha ear an hailt tha man.  Then Jesus saed tae tha heid preeshts, tha offyshers o tha Temple gaird an tha eldèrs, that haed cum oot tae tak houl o hïm: “Am A some soart o a reiver, that yis hae cum oot wi swords an stavs agin me?  Whan A wus wi yis iverie day ïn tha Hoose o God, yis niver layed a fïng'r on me. But thïs ïs tha time fer yous tae ect; tha pooer o dairkness ïs ower yis noo.” Then the' tuk houl o Jesus, an led hïm oot, an brocht hïm tae tha Heich Preesht's hoose. Petèr wus follaein behin, keepin hïs distance.  An the' kïnnelt a fire ïn tha mïddle o tha coortyaird, an the' sut doon thegither, an Petèr amang thaim.  An thair wus thïs wee sarvin lass tuk a clase luk at hïm ïn tha lowe o tha fire. “Thïs man wus wi hïm tae,” saed she.  But Petèr saed, “Na, na, lass, A dïnnae know hïm.”  Eftèr a while anither yin saa hïm an saed, “Ye ir yin o thaim tae.” But Petèr saed, “Man, na, A'm naethin o tha soart!”  An aboot an oor eftèr that, anither yin insïstit, “Thïs fella wus shairlie wi hïm, fer wi'oot a doot he's frae Galilee tae!”  But wi that Petèr saed, “Man, A dïnnae know whut ye ir taakin aboot!” An tha wurds wusnae richt aff hïs tung, whan a roostèr craad.  An tha Loard turnt an lukt at Petèr. An Petèr haed mine o hoo tha Loard haed saed tae hïm: “Afore tha roostèr craas ïn tha moarnin, ye wull deny me thrie times.”  An Petèr went oot o tha coortyaird, greetin sair. Noo tha men houlin Jesus wur mockin hïm, an giein hïm a guid whalin.  An the' püt a blinfoul on hïm, [the' hut hïm on tha face], an axt, “Weel, proaphit, tell iz wha skelpt ye?”  An the' caad hïm iverie name unnèr tha sin. Then at tha scraich o day, aa tha eldèrs o tha fowk gethert thegither, baith tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa. The' led Jesus awa tae thair Cooncil , an the' saed tae hïm,  “If ye ir tha Christ, tell iz!” An he saed bak tae thaim, “If A dae tell yis, yis'll no believe me.  An ïf A ax yis oniethin, yis'll no gie me an answer oniehoo.  But frae thïs time forrit, tha Sinn o Man wull be saitit at tha richt han o tha Michtie Yin.”  An the' aa saed, “Sae ye ir tha Sinn o God, then?” An Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “Weel, ye saed ït yersels!”  “Whut mair pruif dae we need?” the' axt. “Noo we hae heerd ït fer oorsels frae hïs ain mooth!” Then tha Cooncil, tha hale lock o thaim, tuk Jesus an brocht hïm up tae Pilate.  An the' stairtit tae brïng chairges agin hïm, an saed, “We fun thïs man leadin tha fowk asthray, tellin thaim no tae pye onie tex tae Caesar, makkin hissel oot tae be Christ tha Messiah, an a kïng!”  Pilate axt Jesus, “Ir you tha Kïng o tha Jews?” An Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “You hae saed ït.”  Then Pilate saed tae tha heid preeshts an tha thrang o fowk, “A cannae fin oniethin agin thïs man!”  But the' kep on at Pilate, sayin, “Thïs man ïs stïrrin up naethin but bother, wi tha thïngs he's bin lairnin tha fowk tha lenth an breadth o tha lan, frae Galilee richt doon tae here.” Whan Pilate heerd thïs, he axt, “Ach, daes he cum frae Galilee then?”  An as shuin as he fun oot that Jesus cum unnèr Herod's thortie, he sent hïm up tae hïm, fer Herod happent tae be ïn Jerusalem hissel at tha time.  Noo whan Herod saa Jesus, he wus hairt gled, fer he haed heerd aa aboot hïm an haed bin langin tae see hïm. He haed hoped he micht see hïm daein some mïracle.  Sae he axt Jesus a hale lock o questions, but Jesus niver saed a wurd bak.  An tha heid preeshts an tha maistèrs o tha Laa wus stannin aboot, hoochin an yellin thair accusations agin Jesus.  Herod alang wi hïs sodgers jeert an made lïttle o hïm, riggin hïm oot ïn a braw fancie goon. An the' sent hïm agane tae Pilate.  That verie day Herod an Pilate becum guid freens; afore that thair wus nae love loast atween thaim. Sae Pilate caad thegither tha heid preeshts an ither releejus heidyins, alang wi aa tha ordinarie fowk.  An he saed tae thaim, “Yis hae brocht thïs man afore me sayin that he wus stïrrin up fowk an casin bother. A hae examined hïm afore yis aa, an A hae fun naethin wrang ava, as faur as whut yis say he haes daen.  Na, Herod dïdnae ither, fer he sent hïm bak tae iz. Lïsten tae me, thïs man haes daen naethin tae warrant bein püt tae deith.  Sae A'll gie hïm a whalin tae lairn hïm a lesson, an let hïm gang!”  [Fer he maun let yin wrangdaer gang at tha Faist.] Then tha hale crood o thaim yellt oot, “Awa wi thïs man! Let Barabbas oot!”  Noo Barabbas haed bin püt ïn jail fer murdèr an riotin ïn Jerusalem.  Pilate wantit tae let Jesus gang free, sae he spauk agane tae thaim aa.  But the' kep on cryin oot, “Crucyfie hïm! Crucyfie hïm!”  Pilate saed tae thaim a thurd time, “Why, whut wrang haes he daen? A dïnnae fin oniethin tae pit hïm tae deith ower. A'll gie hïm a whalin an let hïm gang.”  But tha hale thrang shoutit aa tha mair that Jesus shud be crucyfied. An tha crood an tha heid preeshts got thair ain wye.  Sae Pilate gien ïn tae whut the' wantit;  he daen as the' axt hïm, an he let gang tha man that haed bin püt ïn jail fer riot an murdèr. But Jesus he hannit ower tae thaim; the' cud dae whut the' wantit wi hïm. As the' led Jesus awa, the' clappt hans on Simon frae Cyrene, that wus makkin hïs wye ïn frae tha kintrie. The' püt tha cross on hïs shoodèr, an the' gart hïm tae cairrie ït behin Jesus.  A hale crood o fowk wus follaein ahint hïm, an amang thaim a lock o weemen that wur batin thair breeshts an lamentin ower whut wus gaun tae happen tae Jesus.  But Jesus turnt roon tae thaim an saed, “Dochtèrs o Jerusalem, dïnnae greet fer me, greet fer yersels an yer weans!  Fer luk, tha day's no faur aff, whan the' wull be sayin, ‘Blisst ir tha weemen that's barren, an tha wames that niver bair weans, an tha breeshts that niver gie mïlk.’  In that day the' wull stairt sayin tae tha muntins, ‘Faa doon on iz!’ An tae tha hïlls, ‘Cover iz ower!’  Noo ïf the' wud dae that whaniver tha tree ïs ïn fu leaf an growein weel, whut wull the' dae whan tha trees ir wuthert?” Twa ithers as weel, that wur crïmnals, wur led oot tae be püt tae deith alang wi Jesus.  An whan the' cum tae tha place caad “Calvarie” , the' crucyfied hïm thair, an tha twa crïmnals alang wi hïm, yin on tha richt han side, tha tither on tha left.  [An Jesus saed, “Faither, forgie thaim, fer the' dïnnae ken whut the'r daein.”] An tha sodgers gemmelt fer hïs claes, pairtin thaim amang thairsels.  Aa tha while, tha fowk stud bye, lukkin on. But tha heidyins o tha Jews giekt at hïm, sayin, “He saved ithers. Let hïm save hissel, ïf he's God's Messiah, tha chosen yin!”  Tha sodgers jeert hïm tae, cumin up an offerin hïm soor wine.  An the' saed tae hïm, “If you ir tha Kïng o tha Jews, save yersel!”  An the' püt up a signboord abain hïm [an ït saed ïn tha Greek, tha Latin an tha Hebrew]: “THIS IS THA KING O THA JEWS” Noo yin o tha crïmnals hingin alangside o hïm yellt abuse at hïm. “Ir ye no tha Messiah?” he axt. “Save yersel, an iz forbye!”  But tha ither yin gien aff tae hïm, an axt hïm, “Dae ye no fear God, seein as ye ir condemned tae dee as weel?  We ir jist gettin whut we desarve fer whut we hae daen. But thïs man haes daen naethin wrang ava!”  An wi that he saed, “[Loard] Jesus, keep mine o me whan ye cum ïntae yer Kïngdom.”  Saed Jesus bak tae hïm, “A tell ye tha truith, ye'll be wi me ïn paradise thïs verie day!” Bi thïs time ït wus nuin, an dairkness cum ower tha hale lan tae thrie ïn tha eftèrnuin.  Tha licht o tha sin wus blekt oot, an tha curtin hingin ïn tha Halie o Halies wus torn ïn twa.  Then Jesus cryed oot wi a lood voice, “Faither, A gie ma spïrit up ïntae your hans!” An wi that, he gien hïs last breath.  Noo whan tha centurion  saen whut wus daen, he gien glorie tae God, an saed, “Thon man wus a guid man, that's fer shair!”  An aa tha fowk that cum tae see whut wus gaun on, whan the' saa whut wus daen, the' bate thair breeshts ïn sorra an went awa.  An aa Jesus' freens, alang wi tha weemen that follaed hïm frae Galilee, stud awa bak takkin ït aa ïn. Noo thair wus a man caad Joseph, a coonciller, a guid an dacent man, that haednae gan alang wi thair deceesion tae kïll Jesus. He wus frae Arimathea, a toon o tha Jews, an he wus bidin hïs time, waitin on tha Kïngdom o God tae cum.  Joseph went tae Pilate an axt fer tha bodie o Jesus.  An he tuk ït doon frae tha cross, lapt ït ïn lïnen claith, an layed ït ïn a tomb cut oot o tha roak, whar naebodie haed bin layed afore.  An ït wus late ïn tha day on Friday, tha day fer gettin readie fer tha Sabbath.  Tha weemen that haed cum wi Jesus frae Galilee follaed eftèr, an the' tuk heed o tha tomb an hoo hïs bodie wus layed oot thair.  The' went awa an made up spices an ointments, an then the' stapt thair wark fer tha Sabbath day accoardin tae tha commaun o God. On tha furst day o tha week, at tha scraich o day, tha weemen cum tae tha tomb, an brocht tha spices the' haed makkit readie. [An thair wus ither yins alang wi thaim.]  An the' fun tha stane rowlt awa frae tha tomb.  The' went ïn, but tha bodie o tha Loard Jesus wus naewhar tae be saen.  An the' wur wile fasht aboot ït. Aa o a suddent, thair wur twa men stannin bye ïn bricht claes.  Tha weemen wus hairt feart, an bood doon wi thair faces tae tha grun. An tha men saed, “Fer why ir yis lukkin tha leevin amang tha deid?  [He's no here, he's ris!] Dae yis no mine hoo he taakt tae yis bak ïn Galilee,  sayin, ‘Tha Sinn o Man maun be gien ïntae tha hans o sïnfu men tae be crucyfied, an tha thurd day rise agane’?”  “Ay, richt eneuch,” the' saed, “that's jist whut Jesus toul iz wud happen.”  Sae the' cum awa frae tha tomb, an toul tha eleiven possels aa that haed cum aboot, an the' toul aa tha rest o thaim as weel.  It wus Mary Magdalene, an Johanna, an Mary tha mither o Jeames, an ither weemen that wur wi thaim that toul these thïngs tae tha possels.  An the' dïdnae believe thaim, an thocht the' wur taakin blethers.  Then Petèr got up an run tae tha tomb an stoopit doon an keekt ïn. He saa tha linen claiths lyin bye thair lane, an he went awa wunnèrin tae hissel whut haed cum aboot. That same day, twa o Jesus' follaers set oot fer tha vïllage o Emmaus, sïx or seiven mile frae Jerusalem.  An the' wur taakin tae yin anither aboot aa tha goins-on.  An whan the' wur taakin aboot ït an tryin tae unnèrstan ït, Jesus hissel cum up alangside o thaim an waakit wi thaim.  The' saa hïm aa richt, but the' dïdnae ken wha he wus.  An he saed tae thaim, “Whut wur ye taakin aboot thair, alang tha róad?” The' cum tae a stap, lukkin doon ïn tha mooth.  An yin o thaim, caad Cleopas, saed tae hïm, “Ye maun be a stranger ïn Jerusalem ïf ye hinnae heerd ocht o whut's bin happenin thair ïn tha last wheen o days!”  Saed he tae thaim, “Whut thïngs?” An the' saed, “Dïd ye no hear aboot Jesus o Nazareth, a proaphit, michtie ïn hïs wurds an daeins afore God an aa tha fowk?  An aboot hoo oor heid preeshts an heidyins hannit hïm ower? The' passt a sentence o deith on hïm, an nailt hïm tae a cross, sae the' dïd.  We haed thocht he wus tha yin that wud redeem Israel. Oniehoo, ït's thrie days since thïs happent.  Ay, an parteeclar weemen frae amang iz, that wur up earlie at hïs tomb, tuk iz bak whan the' saed the' cudnae fin hïs bodie, an the' cum bak an toul iz the'd saen a vïsion o angels sayin Jesus wus leevin!  An sartin o thaim that wus amang iz went tae tha tomb an richt eneuch, the' fun ït jist as tha weemen haed saed: Jesus wusnae thair.”  Then Jesus saed tae tha twa o thaim, “Ye coofs, yis ir slow tae tak ïn aa that tha proaphits spauk aboot!  The' saed that Christ wud hae tae dree aa these thïngs afore he gaed ïntae hïs glorie, dïd the' no?”  An stairtin wi Moses an aa tha proaphits, he made plain tae thaim whut aa tha Scrïptures saed aboot hissel. An whan the' cum nearhan tha vïllage whar the' wur gaun, he lukt as ïf he wus gaun on furdèr.  But the' coaxt hïm, sayin, “Wud ye no stap wi iz, fer ït's dailygan, an ït'll be dairk shuin?” Sae he went ïn wi thaim.  An ït cum aboot, as he sut doon tae ait wi thaim, that he tuk breid, blisst ït an brauk ït, an gien ït tae thaim.  An aa o a suddent thair een wus apent, an the' kent wha he wus, an wi that Jesus wus nae mair tae bi saen!  The' saed tae yin anither, “Dïd ït no set oor hairts a-low, whan he taakt tae iz on tha róad, an apent up tha Scrïptures tae iz?”  Sae the' ris up tha same oor, an the' went bak tae Jerusalem, an fun tha eleiven gethert thegither, an thaim that wur wi thaim.  “Tha Loard ïs ris, richt eneuch!” the' wur toul. “An Simon haes saen hïm!”  An tha twa frae Emmaus toul aa that haed happent on tha róad, an hoo the' knowed ït wus Jesus tha mïnit he brauk tha breid. An jist as the' wur taakin, thair stud Jesus ïn tha mïddle o thaim aa, [an he saed tae thaim, “Peace be wi yis!”]  But the' wur aa hairt-scarred an afeart, an thocht the' haed saen a wraith.  An he saed tae thaim, “Fer why ir yis püt aboot? An why aa tha doots wi'ïn yersels?  Tak a luk at ma hans an ma feet. It's masel! Hannle me an see! Fer a wraith haesnae flesh an banes as yis see A hae.”  [An eftèr sayin thïs, he showed thaim hïs hans an hïs feet.]  An the' wur that blythesum an dumfoonèrt, the' cud harlie tak ït ïn. An he axt thaim, “Hae yis ocht tae ait ïn tha hoose?”  The' gien hïm a bït o brannèrt fïsh, [an a wee bït o honeycomb],  an he tuk ït an et ït afore thaim. Then he saed tae thaim, “Thïs ïs whut A toul ye whaniver A wus still amang yis, that aa tha thïngs that wur writ doon consarnin me ïn tha Laa o Moses, tha Proaphits an tha Psaums maun cum aboot.”  Then he apent thair mines tae unnèrstan tha Scrïptures,  sayin tae thaim, “It's writ doon that tha Christ maun suffer, he maun dee an rise frae tha deid tha thurd day;  an that wi ma thortie yis ir tae praich thïs message tae aa nations: ‘Repent o yer sïns, an God wull forgie yis.’ Yis ir tae stairt frae Jerusalem.  Yous hae saen these thïngs, sae yis ir wutnesses o thaim aa.  Noo, lïsten tae me, A wull senn upon yis tha gift ma Faither promist. But yous ir tae stap here, ïn Jerusalem, tae yis ir claithed wi pooer frae abain.” An Jesus led thaim oot tha lenth o Bethanie, an thair he lïftit up hïs hans an blisst thaim.  An ït cum aboot, that while he wus blissin thaim, he pairtit frae thaim, an he wus taen up ïntae heiven.  [An the' wurshipt hïm] an the' went bak tae Jerusalem wi blythesum hairts.  An the' spent aa thair time laudin an blissin ïn tha Hoose o God. Richt at tha stairt, ye haed tha Wurd. Tha Wurd wus thair alang wi God, an tha Wurd wus God.  He wus thair alang wi God richt frae tha stairt.  Iverie last thïng wus made throu hïm; athoot hïm, naethin ava wus iver made.  In hïm wus life, an thïs life wus tha licht o mankine.  Tha licht beams ïn tha mirk, but tha mirk cannae pit ït oot. Thair wus thïs man sent oot frae God bi tha name o Jhone.  An he cum fer tae be a wutness tae tha licht, sae that acause o hïm aa fowk micht believe.  Noo he wusnae thon licht hissel, but he cum fer tae be a wutness tae tha licht. Tha true licht, hïm that gies licht tae iverie man, wus cumin ïntae tha warl.  He wus ïn tha warl, but tha mair ït wus o hïs makkin, tha warl dïdnae ken wha he wus.  He cum tae hïs ain lan, but hïs ain fowk wantit naethin tae dae wi hïm.  Yit tae aa thaim that dïd tak hïm ïn, an trustit on hïs name, he gien thaim tha richt tae be makkit childèr o God;  Childèr, that wus no boarn bi tha wye o nature, ner bi tha wull o flesh an bluid, ner bi tha notion a husban micht hae. Na, but childèr that wus boarn o God. Tha Wurd cum tae be flesh an bluid an leeved amang iz. We hae saa hïs glorie, tha glorie o tha Yin an Ainlie that cum frae tha Faither, fu o grace an truith.  Jhone gien wutness o hïm. He caad oot, cryin, “Thon's hïm A wus taakin aboot whaniver A saed, ‘Hïm that cums eftèr me ïs abain me, fer he wus thair afore iver A wus boarn.’ ”  Oot o tha fu guidness o hïs hairt we hae aa got yin blissin on tap o anither.  Tha mair tha Laa wus gien throu Moses, grace an truith cum throu Jesus Christ.  Naebodie haes iver saen God; ït ïs God's yae Sinn, wha bides ïn tha hairt o tha Faither, that haes showed hïm tae fowk. Noo, tha day tha Jews sent preeshts an Levites frae Jerusalem tae ax Jhone wha he wus, here ïs whut he saed tae thaim. He wus aye apen aboot ït, an toul thaim strecht, “A'm no tha Christ.”  Sae the' axt hïm, “Wha ir ye then? Wud ye be Elijah?” “Na, A'm no,” qo he. “Ir ye tha Proaphit we ir waitin on?” “Na,” saed he.  At tha enn o ït the' speered, “Wha ir ye? Gie iz yer answer tae tak bak tae thaim that sent iz. Whut hae ye tae say fer yersel?”  Jhone answert wi tha wurds o Isaiah tha proaphit, “A'm tha voice o yin caain oot ïn tha wiles, ‘Mak tha róad readie fer tha Loard cumin.’ ” Noo, some Pharisees that haed bin sent speered hïm mair,  “Gin ye'r no tha Christ, ner Elijah, ner tha Proaphit, hoo cum ye'r baptisin fowk then?”  “A baptise wi wattèr,” Jhone answert, “but thair's yin stud amang ye that yis dïnnae know.  Hïm that cums alang eftèr me, he's tha yin. An A'm no fït tae lowse hïs buits fer hïm.”  Noo thïs aa cum aboot at Bethanie on tha faur side o tha Joardan, whar Jhone wus baptisin. Tha nixt day Jhone saa Jesus cumin up tae hïm an saed, “Luk an behoul, tha Lamb o God that taks awa tha sïn o tha warl!  Thon's tha man A wus taakin aboot whaniver A saed, ‘Thair's a man cumin eftèr me that's o heicher stannin ner me, fer he wus thair afore iver A wus boarn.’  A dïdnae unnèrstan masel wha he wus, but ït wus tae mak him kent tae Israel that A cum baptisin wi wattèr.”  Then Jhone gien thïs accoont: “A saa tha Spïrit cum doon frae heiven laik a doo an bide on hïm.  A wudnae a knowed hïm, but tha yin that sent me fer tae baptise wi wattèr toul me, ‘Whan ye see tha Spïrit cum doon an bide on a man, ït's hïm that wull baptise wi tha Halie Spïrit.’  A hae saa ït fer masel an A'm wutness tae ït. Thon man daes be tha Sinn o God.” Tha nixt day Jhone wus bak thonner wi twa o hïs ain follaers.  Whaniver he saa Jesus slippin bye, he saed, “Luk, thon's tha Lamb o God!”  Whaniver tha twa follaers heerd hïm say thïs, the' turnt an went eftèr Jesus.  Lukkin roon, Jesus saa thaim cumin eftèr hïm an axt, “Whut dae yis want?” “Rabbi” the' saed ('Rabbi' stans fer ‘Dominie’), “whar ir ye stappin thenicht?”  “Cum on an see,” he answert. Sae the' went an saa whar he wus stappin, an the' passt tha rest o tha day wi hïm, fer ït wus aboot fower ïn tha eftèrnuin.  Andra, Simon Petèr's brither, wus yin o tha twa that went eftèr Jesus whaniver the' heerd whut Jhone haed saed.  Tha furst thïng Andra daen wus tae fin hïs brither Simon an tell hïm, “We hae fun tha Messiah!” (mainin, tha Christ).  An he brocht hïm tae Jesus. Jesus tuk a guid luk at hïm an he saed, “Sae ye ir Simon, Jhone's sinn. Ye'll noo be caad Cephas.” (Cephas stans fer Petèr, mainin ‘a roak’.) Tha nixt day Jesus made up hïs mine tae heid fer Galilee. He fun Phïlip an saed tae hïm, “Follae me.”  Noo Phïlip cum frae Bethsaida, tha same toon as Andra an Petèr.  Phïlip fun Thannie an toul hïm, “We hae fun tha yin Moses writ aboot ïn tha Laa, hïm that tha proaphits writ aboot forbye - Jesus o Nazareth, tha sinn o Joseph.”  “Nazareth! Cud ye iver see ocht guid cumin oot o thonner?” Thannie axt. “Cum an see fer yersel,” saed Phïlip.  Whan Jesus saa Thannie cumin, he saed thïs aboot hïm: “Noo thair's a guid Israelite; thair's naethin fauss aboot hïm!”  “Hoo ïs ït ye ken me?” Thannie axt. Jesus answert, “A saa ye whaniver ye wur still unnèr tha fïg tree, afore Phïlip caad ye.”  Wi that Thannie declared, “Rabbi, you ir tha Sinn o God, sae ye ir. Tha Kïng o Israel!”  Jesus saed, “You lippen jist wi me tellin ye A saa ye unnèr tha fïg tree? Weel, ye'll see ower mair ner that.”  An then he addit, “A'm tellin yis tha truith, thair's a day cumin whaniver ye'll see heiven apen up, an tha angels o God gaun up an cumin doon on tha Sinn o Man.” Cum tha thurd day thair wus thïs waddin on at Cana ïn Galilee, an tha mither o Jesus wus at ït.  An Jesus wus axt tae tha waddin tae, alang wi hïs follaers.  Noo whaniver tha wine wus aa daen, Jesus's mither saed til hïm, “The' hae nae mair wine.”  “Wumman dear,” Jesus answert, “whut ir ye brïngin me ïntae ït fer? Ma oor ïsnae cum yit.”  Hïs mither saed til tha sarvints, “whutiver he bïds yis dae, dae ït.”  Noo nearhan thair wus sïx stane wattèr crocks, tha soart tha Jews uised fer rïtual waashin, that cud houl aboot twuntie tae thurtie gallon apiece.  Jesus toul tha sarvints, “Fïll tha crocks fu o wattèr”. Sae the' fïllt thaim fu tae tha lïp.  Then he toul thaim, “Noo lave a drap oot an tak ït tae tha heid sarvint.” Sae the' daen as the' wur bïd.  An tha heid sarvint preed a wee taste o tha wattèr that haed bin turnt ïntae wine. He'd nae notion whar ït cum frae, tha mair tha sarvints that haed brocht tha wattèr knowed. Sae he tuk tha bridegruim tae tha yin side.  Qo he, “Onie ither bodie wud gie oot tha guid wine at tha furst, an whan fowks hae a lock o drïnk ïn thaim, the' brïng oot tha chaip stuff. But you hae kep tha guid wine tae noo.”  Thïs sign, at Cana ïn Galilee, wus tha furst that Jesus wrocht. In daein thïs, hïs glorie wus thair fer aa tae see, an hïs follaers believed ïn hïm. Eftèr thïs, Jesus tuk hissel doon wi hïs follaers tae Capernaum alang wi hïs mither an brithers, an the' aa stapt thonner fer twarthie days.  Whaniver tha time cum fer tha Jews tae houl tha Passower, Jesus gaed up tae Jerusalem.  An ïn tha coortyaird o tha Hoose o God he cum on men dailin ïn kye, sheep an doos, an ithers sïttin at thair tables changin siller.  Sae he püt thegither a whup o coards, an driv tha hale lock oot o tha Temple gruns, alang wi sheep an kye; he skailt tha siller o tha money changers an coupt thair tables.  Tae thaim that soul doos he saed, “Tak aa thïs awa oot o here! Hoo dar yis mak a margymore oot o ma Faither's hoose!”  Hïs follaers haed mine o tha Scrïpture whar ït's writ, “A'll be het up wi a hung'r fer your hoose!”  Sae tha Jews then axt hïm strecht, “Whut sign cud ye gie iz fer pruif o yer richt tae dae aa thïs?”  Jesus gien thaim tha answer, “Fletten thïs temple, an ïn thrie days A wull rise ït agane.”  But tha Jews cum bak wi, “It tuk fowertie-sïx year tae big thïs Temple, an ye'r fer risin ït agane ïn thrie days?”  Hooaniver, tha temple he wus taakin aboot wus hïs ain bodie.  Eftèr he wus ris frae tha deid, hïs follaers haed mine o whut he saed. Then the' püt thair faith ïn Scrïpture an tha wurd o Jesus.  Noo whaniver he wus ïn Jerusalem fer tha Faist o tha Passower, monie fowks püt thair faith ïn hïs name, whan the' saen tha signs he daen.  But Jesus wudnae pit hïs faith ïn thaim, fer he knowed whut fowk wus laik.  He dïdnae need oniebodie tae tell hïm ocht aboot fowk, fer he kent weel eneuch whut wus ïn thair hairts. Noo thair wus yin o tha Pharisees caad Nicodemus, a memmer o tha Heich Cooncil o tha Jews.  He cum tae Jesus at nicht an saed, “Rabbi, we ken ye'r a taicher that haes cum frae God, fer naebodie cud wark these signs ye ir daein ïf God wusnae wi hïm.”  Jesus saed bak tae hïm, “A'm tellin ye tha truith, naebodie wull see tha Kïngdom o God, ïf he ïsnae boarn agane.”  “Hoo cud ye get boarn agane whaniver ye'r aareadie oul?” Nicodemus axt. “Shair ye cudnae gang bak ïntae yer mither's wame, an be boarn agane, cud ye!”  Jesus answert, “A'm tellin ye tha truith, naebodie can get ïntae tha Kïngdom o God ïf he ïsnae boarn o wattèr an tha Spïrit.  Whut's boarn o tha flesh ïs flesh, but whut's boarn o tha Spïrit ïs Spïrit.  Dïnnae be tuk bak whaniver A tell ye, yis maun be boarn agane.  Tha wun blaas whutiver airt ït wants. Ye hear tha sugh o ït, but ye dïnnae ken whar ït's cum frae, ner whar ït's gaun tae. It's tha same wi iveriebodie that's boarn o tha Spïrit.”  Nicodemus saed bak tae hïm, “Weel, hoo cud that be?”  “Wi you bein a taicher o Israel,” saed Jesus, “ye'd thïnk ye wud unnèrstan these thïngs!  A'm tellin ye tha truith, whut we ir tellin ye aboot, ïs baith whut we ken an whut we hae wutnesst, but yous fowk dïnnae tak onie heed o iz.  Whan A hae toul ye aboot tha thïngs o tha irth, an yis dïnnae tak ma wurd fer ït, hoo ir ye gaun tae believe whan A taak aboot tha thïngs o heiven?  Naebodie haes iver gan up tae heiven apairt frae tha yin that ïs cum doon frae heiven - tha Sinn o Man [wha ïs ïn heiven].  But jist as Moses püt up tha sarpent on a poul ïn tha wuldèrness, tha Sinn o Man maun be lïftit up tae;  Sae that iveriebodie that believes on hïm [wull no perish], but wull hae ayelastin life.  Fer God loved tha warl that much, that he gien hïs yin an ainlie Sinn, sae that whaiver pits thair trust ïn hïm wull no be loast, but wull leeve fer ivermair.  Fer God niver sent hïs Sinn ïntae tha warl fer tae judge ït, but rether fer tae save ït.  Oniebodie that believes on hïm ïs no condemned, but oniebodie that daesnae believe ïs aareadie condemned, fer he haesnae believed on tha name o God's yin an ainlie Sinn.  An thïs ïs tha judgemen: that tha licht haes cum ïntae tha warl, but men wud rether hae tha dairk ner tha licht on accoont o thair wrangdaeins.  Iverie wrangdaer haits tha licht, an the'll no cum ïntae tha licht fer fear thair wrangdaeins wull be fun oot.  But oniebodie that leeves bi tha truith cums ïntae tha licht, sae ït's oot ïn tha apen fer aa tae see, that whut he haes daen wus God's daein.” Eftèr thïs, Jesus an hïs follaers cum ïntae tha kintrie o Judea whar he stapt a wheen o days alang wi thaim, an baptised fowks.  Weel, Jhone wus baptisin fowk forbye, at Aenon nearhan Salim, fer thair wus wattèr a-plentie thair an fowks wus cumin lukkin baptised.  (But thïs wus afore Jhone wus püt ïntae jail.) Twarthie o Jhone's follaers haed wurds wi a Jew ower rïtual waashin.  The' cum tae Jhone an saed, “Rabbi, ye mine thon man that wus wi ye on tha ither side o tha Joardan - ye ken tha yin ye toul iz aboot - weel, he ïs baptisin, an the' ir aa flockin tae hïm!”  Jhone saed bak tae thaim, “Naebodie can get ocht, less ït's gien tae hïm frae heiven.  Shair yis know yersels, A toul yis strecht; ‘A'm no tha Christ, A wus jist sent aheid o hïm.’  Tha bridegruim's tha yin that tha bride belangs tae. Still an aa, tha freen lukkin eftèr hïm stans alangside o hïm an bes gye gled tae lïsten tae tha soon o hïs voice. Noo A'm owercum wi joy masel.  He maun growe bïgger, an A maun get smaaer.” Tha Yin that cums frae abain ïs abain aa; tha yin that ïs frae tha irth belangs tae tha irth an taaks aboot tha thïngs o tha irth. Tha yin that cums frae heiven ïs abain aa.  He's toul thaim whut aa he haes saen an heerd, but naebodie taks onie heed.  Tha yin that daes tak heed o ït, tha same yin wud warrant that God spakes tha truith.  Tak tent, tha yin that God haes sent taaks tha wurds o God, fer thair's nae lïmit tae tha Spïrit God gies hïm.  Tha Faither loves tha Sinn an haes gien aa thïngs ïntae hïs han.  An oniebodie that pits thair belief ïn tha Sinn haes ayelastin life, but oniebodie that turns thair bak on tha Sinn winnae see life, but tha wrath o God hings ower hïm. Tha Pharisees heerd that Jesus wus getherin mair follaers roon hïm ner Jhone, an he wus baptisin thaim.  (Tha mair ïn fect ït wusnae Jesus, but hïs follaers, that wus daein tha baptisin.)  But whaniver tha Loard heerd thïs, he upt an left Judea an went awa hame yinst mair tae Galilee.  Noo he beed tae gang throu Samaria.  Sae he cum tae thïs toon ïn Samaria wi tha name o Sychar, nearhan tha wee bït o grun that Jacob haed gien tae Joseph.  Jacob's wal wus thonner, an Jesus, daen oot frae aa hïs trevelin, sut doon agin tha wal. An ït wus aboot tha mïddle o tha day.  Noo a Samaritan wumman cum fer a go o wattèr oot o tha wal, an Jesus saed til hir, “Gie iz a drïnk o yer wattèr.”  (Hïs follaers wur awa ïntae tha toon tae buy mait.)  Tha wumman saed bak tae hïm, “Hoo cum ye'r axin me fer a drïnk, an you a Jew, an me a Samaritan wumman?” (Fer tha Jews haed nae truck wi tha Samaritans.)  Jesus gien hir tha answer, “If ye haed onlie but knowed whut God haes tae gie, an wha's axin ye fer tha drïnk, ye wud hae axt hïm, an he wud hae gien ye tha leevin wattèr.”  “Sïr,” qo she, “Ye hae naethin tae lave tha wattèr oot wi, an tha wal ïs brave an deep. Whar dae ye get thïs leevin wattèr frae?  Dae ye thïnk ye'r a bïgger man ner oor forefaither Jacob, that gien iz tha wal an drunk frae ït hissel, laik hïs sinns daen forbye, an hïs beese anaa?”  Jesus saed til hir, “Oniebodie that taks a drïnk o thïs wattèr wull aye hae a druith on thaim agane.  But oniebodie that taks a drïnk o tha wattèr that A gie hïm wull niver hae a druith agane. Deed, ay, tha wattèr A gie hïm wull be a wattèr spoot, wallin up tae ayelastin life.”  Tha wumman saed tae hïm, “Weel sïr, gie's a drap o thïs wattèr then, sae A'll niver hae a druith on me agane, ner hae tae keep cumin bak here fer tae draa wattèr.”  He toul hir, “Awa an caa yer husban an cum bak here.”  “A hae nae husban,” she answert. Jesus saed til hir, “Ye'r richt thair, whaniver ye say ye hinnae a husban.  Tha truith o tha mettèr ïs, ye hae haed five husbans an tha man ye'r leevin wi jist noo ïs no yer husban ava. Sae ye wur richt ïn whut ye saed.”  “Sïr,” tha wumman saed, “Ye maun be a proaphit!  Oor forefaithers wurshipt on thïs muntin, but yous Jews houl that we hae tae woarship ïn Jerusalem.”  Jesus saed, “Believe you me, wumman, tha time's cumin whan ït'll no be on thïs here muntin, ner ïn Jerusalem ether, that yis'll be woarshippin tha Faither!  Yous Samaritans dïnnae ken whut yis ir woarshippin; we Jews dae ken whut we'r woarshippin, fer salvation ïs frae tha Jews.  Yit tha oor's cumin, an ït's here noo, whan tha true woarshippers wull woarship tha Faither ïn spïrit an truith, fer thaim's tha soart tha Faither's lukkin fer tae woarship hïm.  God ïs spïrit, an thaim that woarship hïm, maun woarship ïn spïrit an truith.”  Tha wumman saed, “A ken that tha Messiah - hïm the' caa Christ - ïs cumin. Whaniver he cums he'll mak aa thïngs clear tae iz.”  Saed Jesus til hir, “A'm hïm. Tha verie yin that's taakin tae ye!” Jist then hïs follaers cum bak, an the' wur stoondit that Jesus wus taakin wi a wumman. But naebodie axt hïm, “Whut dae ye want wi hir?” or “Whut ir ye daein taakin tae hir?”  Sae tha wumman set hir wattèr jar doon, an went aff bak ïntae tha toon. Thair she telt tha fowk,  “Cum an see thïs man that toul me aa A iver daen. Cud thïs no be tha Christ?”  Sae oot the' cum frae tha toon an made thair wye up tae hïm.  While thïs wus gaun on, hïs follaers kep at hïm, sayin, “Rabbi, wud ye no tak a bite tae ait?”  But he toul thaim, “A hae mait tae ait that yis ken naethin aboot.”  Then hïs follaers saed tae yin anither, “Cud oniebodie hae brocht hïm mait whaniver we wur awa?”  “Ma mait,” saed Jesus, “ïs daein tha wull o hïm that sent me, an tae get hïs wark aa daen.  Dae yis no say, ‘Fower mair month an then tha hairvest’? A'm tellin ye but, cast yer een oot ower tha fiels! The' ir ripe an readie fer tha hairst.  Tha shearer wull get hïs wages pyed, an wull gether tha craps fer ayelastin life, sae tha sower an tha shearer wull be gled thegither.  Sae ït's tha truith whut the' say, ‘Yin man saas an tha tither yin shears’.  A sent ye fer tae shear whut ye hinnae wrocht at. Ithers hae daen aa tha haird wark, an yous hae got tha guid o thair labourin.” A guid wheen o tha Samaritans frae thon toon believed ïn hïm becas o tha wumman's wutness whaniver she telt thaim, “He toul me iveriethin A iver daen.”  Sae whaniver tha Samaritans cum tae see hïm, the' plaidit wi hïm tae stap a bït lang'r wi thaim. Sae he stapt wi thaim twa days.  Monie mair believed ïn Jesus fer whut he saed.  An the' toul tha wumman eftèr, “We ir no believin ïn hïm onie mair jist becas o whut you telt iz. We hae heerd hïm fer oorsels, an noo we ken that thïs man ïs tha Saviour o tha warl.” Noo eftèr twa days, Jesus tuk hïs leave an gan aff tae Galilee.  (Fer as Jesus hissel haed brocht tae thair notysh, nae proaphit ïs iver weel thocht o ïn hïs ain hametoon.)  An whaniver he cum tae Galilee, tha fowk thonner gien hïm a guid walcum. Fer the' haed saen iveriethin he daen ïn Jerusalem at tha Faist o tha Passower, whaniver the' wur up at ït thairsels.  Jesus stapt aff agane at Cana ïn Galilee, whar he haed turnt tha wattèr ïntae wine. An thïs heidyin frae tha Palace wus thair, whase sinn wus lyin seeck at Capernaum.  Whaniver tha man heerd that Jesus wus bak ïn Galilee frae Judea, he cum plaidin wi Jesus tae cum doon an mak hïs sinn bettèr. Hïs sinn wus gye faur throu.  “Ye see yous fowk, less ye get signs an wunnèrs tae luk at,” Jesus telt hïm, “ye'll niver believe.”  Tha man frae tha Palace saed, “O sïr, cum doon noo, afore ma weefla slips awa.”  Saed Jesus, “Gan yer wa. Yer sinn wull leeve.” Tha man tuk Jesus at hïs wurd an went on hame.  Whan he wus on tha róad, hïs sarvints cum oot tae meet hïm an tell hïm hïs weefla wus aa richt.  Sae he axt at whut oor o tha day hïs sinn tuk a turn fer tha bettèr, an the' toul hïm, “Tha faivir quït at yin o'clock yestèrday.”  Then tha faither knowed richt awa that ït wus tha verie time o day that Jesus saed tae hïm, “Yer sinn wull leeve.” Sae he becum a believer tae, hïm an aa ïn hïs hoose.  Thïs wus tha saicont mïracle Jesus wrocht fer a sign, eftèr cumin bak frae Judea ïntae Galilee. Eftèr a bït, Jesus gaed up tae Jerusalem fer a Faist-day o tha Jews.  Noo, alangside tha Sheep Gate ïn Jerusalem thair's thïs puil that gets tha name o Bethzatha ïn tha Aramaic tung. An ït haes five ruifed-ïn waak-wyes wi apen pillars richt roon ït.  Bïg nummers o disabelt fowk uist tae lie roon ït - tha blin, tha crippelt an tha paralysed, waitin on tha rummlin o tha wattèr.  Fer an angel wud gae doon at a sartin time ïntae tha puil, fer tae rummle tha wattèr. Tha furst yin ïntae tha wattèr eftèr tha rummlin wus makkit weel o whutiver ailment he haed.  Noo yin o thaim that wus lyin thonner haed bin ailin fer thurtie-echt year.  Whan Jesus saa hïm an kent tha lang he wus seeck, he axt hïm, “Dae ye want tae be made weel?”  “Sïr,” tha lameter answert, “A hae naebodie tae gie me a han ïntae tha wattèr whaniver ït's rummelt. Jist whan A'm makkin tae get ïn, some ither bodie aye gets doon afore me.”  Then Jesus saed tae hïm. “Up ye get! Lïft yer mat up an waak.”  Strecht aff tha man wus made weel. He lïftit hïs mat an waakt. Noo aa thïs happent on tha Sabbath day.  An sae tha Jews saed tae tha man that wus makkit weel, “It's tha Sabbath day an tha Laa daesnae alloo ye tae cairrie a mat.”  But he cum bak wi thïs: “Tha man that made me weel saed tae me, ‘Lïft yer mat up an waak.’ ”  An the' axt hïm, “Wha's thïs that toul ye tae lïft ït up an waak?”  Tha man that wus makkit weel haed nae notion ava o wha ït wus, fer Jesus haed jookt aff thonner ïntae tha thrang o fowk.  A while eftèr, Jesus fun hïm at tha Hoose o God an saed til hïm, “Luk see, ye'r weel agane. Sae quït yer sïnnin or sumthin waur micht happen tae ye!”  Tha man went awa an toul tha Jews that ït wus Jesus that made hïm weel. Sae, on accoont o Jesus daein these thïngs on tha Sabbath day, tha Jews wur eftèr hïm, [an wur oot tae pit an enn tae hïm].  But Jesus saed tae thaim, “Ma Faither ïs aye warkin, richt up tae thïs verie day. An A'm warkin tae.”  That's fer why tha Jews ettled aa tha mair tae kïll hïm, no jist fer brekkin tha Sabbath, but forbye he wus caain God hïs ain Faither, an pittin hissel on a level wi God.  Then Jesus toul thaim, “A'm tellin ye tha truith, tha Sinn can dae naethin on hïs ain, but onlie whut he sees hïs Faither dae; fer whutiver tha Faither daes, tha Sinn daes tae.  Fer tha Faither loves tha Sinn an shows hïm aa he daes. Ay, he'll show hïm even bïgger thïngs ner these, thïngs ower an abain aa ye cud tak ïn.  Fer jist laik tha Faither rises tha deid an gies thaim life, sae tha Sinn gies life tae whaiver he plaises.  An mair ner that, tha Faither daesnae judge oniebodie, but haes gien aa judgemen tae tha Sinn,  That aa micht gie honour tae tha Sinn, jist as the' gie honour tae tha Faither. Hïm that daesnae honour tha Sinn, daesnae honour tha Faither that sent hïm.  A'm tellin ye tha truith, whaiver hears ma wurd an believes hïm that sent me haes ayelastin life; he wull no be condemned; he haes flïttit frae deith tae life.  Here's tha truith o ït: tha oor ïs cumin - ay, ït's cum noo! - whan tha deid wull hear tha voice o tha Sinn o God, an thaim that hears wull leeve.  Fer jist laik tha Faither haes tha pooer o life ïn hissel, sae he haes gien tha Sinn tha pooer o life tae.  An he haes gien hïm tha richt tae judge, becas he ïs tha Sinn o Man.  Dïnnae be püt aboot bi thïs, fer tha oor ïs cumin whan aa thaim that's deid an buriet wull hear hïs voice  an cum oot o thair graves - thaim that haes daen guid wull be ris tae life, an thaim that haes daen ïll wull be ris tae damnation.  On ma ain A can dae naethin; A judge jist whut A hear, an ma judgin ïs richt, fer A'm no lukkin tae plaise masel, but tae plaise hïm that sent me.” “If A wutness aboot masel, ma testimonie daesnae stan up.  But thair's anither yin that gies me a guid testimonie, an A ken that hïs testimonie aboot me stans up.  Yis hae sent fowk tae Jhone, an he haes wutnesst tae tha truith aboot me.  No that A need tae tak man's testimonie, but A mak mention o ït sae as ye micht be saved.  Jhone wus a bricht, shinin lamp, an yis wur hairt gled tae leeve ïn tha licht o ït fer a wee while.  But A hae testimonie that houls mair wecht ner Jhone's. Fer tha verie wark that tha Faither haes gien me tae feenish, that's whut A am aboot noo, an ït's wutness tae yin an aa that tha Faither haes sent me.  An tha Faither that sent me haes testified aboot me hissel. Yis hae niver heerd hïs voice ner set yer een on hïm,  Nether daes hïs wurd bide ïn ye, fer ye dïnnae lippen tha yin he sent.  Yis ir aye lukkin at tha ïns an oots o tha Scrïptures, fer ye thïnk that's tha wye ye'll hae ayelastin life. But A'm tha yin tha Scrïptures ïs taakin aboot!  An yit ye wull no cum tae me tae hae life.  Tha praise o man mains naethin tae me.  But A know richtlie whut yous ir laik. A ken that yis dïnnae hae tha love o God ïn yer hairts.  A hae cum ïn ma Faither's name an ye wudnae pye onie heed tae me; but ïf anither bodie cums ïn hïs ain name, ye wud tak heed o hïm, sae ye wud.  Yis ir content eneuch tae tak praise frae yin anither, yit yis mak nae effort tae get tha praise that cums frae tha yin an ainlie God? Sae nae wunnèr yis cannae believe me!  But dïnnae be thïnkin A'm fer accusin ye afore tha Faither. It's Moses that'll accuse ye, tha verie yin yis ir pittin aa yer hope on!  If ye haed hae believed Moses, ye wud hae believed me, fer ït's me he writ aboot.  But seein as ye dïnnae believe whut he writ, ye ir no gaun tae believe whut A say, ir ye?” Eftèr thïs, Jesus went ower tae tha ither side o Loch Galilee (whiles caad Loch Tiberias),  An a hale thrang o fowk wus cumin behin hïm, fer the' saa tha wunnèrs he'd daen wi tha seeck.  Sae Jesus gaed up tha braeside an sut doon wi hïs follaers.  Noo tha Passower Faist, hel bi tha Jews, wus cumin up. Whaniver Jesus lïftit hïs een an saa a bïg nummer o fowk cumin til hïm, he saed tae Phïlip, “Whar cud we buy breid tae feed aa thae fowk?”  But he jist axt thïs tae try hïm oot, fer he knowed fine weel whut he wus fer daein.  Phïlip toul hïm, “Twa hunnèr denarii wudnae be eneuch tae buy breid fer thaim aa!”  Anither o hïs follaers, Andra, Simon Petèr's brither, cum forrit an saed,  “Thair's a weefla here wi five barley bannocks an twa wee fïsh, but hoo faur wud the' gang amang that crood?”  Jesus saed, “Gar tha fowk tae sut doon.” Thair wus onie amoont o gress thonner, an tha men sut doon, aboot five thoosan o thaim.  An then Jesus tuk tha bannocks, gien thenks, an the' wur hannit roon bi hïs follaers tae thaim that wus sut on tha grun, as much as the' wantit. He daen tha same wi tha fïsh.  Whaniver the' aa haed et thair fïll, he toul hïs follaers, “Gether up aa tha left-owers. An mine ye dïnnae waste ocht!”  Sae eftèr iveriebodie haed et, the' gethert tha leains o tha five barley bannocks, an fïllt twal creels wi thaim.  An whaniver tha fowk saa tha wunnèr Jesus wrocht, the' saed, “Thair's nae doot thïs maun be thon Proaphit the' saed wud cum ïntae tha warl.”  Jesus knowed that the' wur ettlin tae mak hïm kïng agin hïs wull, sae he went aff on hïs lane tae tha muntin agane. Bi noo ït wus dailygan, an hïs follaers went doon tae tha loch,  whar the' got ïntae a bóat an set aff ower tha loch heidin fer Capernaum. It wus dairk got an Jesus haednae turnt up yit.  A fierce wun wus blaain, an tha wattèrs wus reuch gettin.  Eftèr the' haed bin rowin thrie or fower mile, the' saa Jesus cumin up tae tha bóat, waakin on tha wattèr; an the' wur wile feart.  But he saed til thaim, “It's masel; dïnnae be feart.”  An sae the' wur gled tae tak hïm aboord tha bóat, an richt awa tha bóat landit on tha shore whar the' wur heidin tae.  Tha nixt day, tha fowk that haed stapt on tha ither shore o tha loch, mindit that thair haed jist bin tha yin bóat thonner, an Jesus haednae got ïn ït alang wi hïs follaers, but that the' haed set aff on thair lane.  But then some bóats frae Tiberias landit near tae whar tha fowk et tha breid eftèr tha Loard haed gien thenks.  Sae tha mïnit tha fowk twigged that Jesus an hïs follaers wurnae aboot, the' got ïntae tha bóats an went tae Capernaum tae luk fer Jesus. Whaniver the' fun hïm on tha ither side o tha loch, the' axt hïm, “Rabbi, whan dïd ye get here?”  Jesus answert, “A'm tellin yis tha truith, yis ir no lukkin fer me acause ye saa wunnèrs. It's becas yis et yer fïll o tha loafs.  Dïnnae wark fer mait that gaes aff. Na, wark fer mait that keeps tae ayelastin life that tha Sinn o Man wull gie tae ye. Fer God tha Faither haes püt tha keel-mairk o hïs bakkin on tha Sinn.”  Sae the' axt hïm, “But whut maun we dae ïf we'r tae dae tha wark that God wud hae iz dae?”  Jesus answert, “Here's whut tha wark o God ïs: that yis pit yer belief ïn tha yin he haes sent.”  An sae the' axt hïm, “Whut sign cud ye gie iz sae that we micht see fer oorsels an believe ye? Whut ir ye fer daein?  Oor forefaithers et tha manna ïn tha wuldèrness; jist laik ït's writ doon ïn tha Scrïptures: ‘He gien thaim breid frae heiven fer tae ait.’ ”  Then Jesus saed tae thaim, “A'm tellin yis tha truith, ït's no Moses that gien ye tha breid frae heiven; ït cum frae ma Faither. An noo ma Faither ïs giein ye tha true breid frae heiven.  Fer tha breid o God ïs hïm that cums doon frae heiven an gies life tae tha warl.”  “Loard,” the' saed, “Frae noo on, thon's tha breid we want.” An Jesus saed tae thaim, “A am tha breid o life. Hïm that cums tae me wull niver get hung'rie, an hïm that believes ïn me wull niver hae a druith agane.  But laik A telt ye, tha mair ye hae saen me, yis dïnnae believe.  Aa that tha Faither gies me wull cum tae me, an oniebodie that cums tae me A'll niver turn thaim awa.  Fer A'm no cum frae heiven tae dae ma ain wull, but tae dae tha wull o hïm that sent me.  An thïs ïs tha wull o hïm that sent me, that oot o aa he haes gien me thair'll be nane ava loast, but A'll rise thaim aa up on tha Last Day.  Fer ït's ma Faither's wull that oniebodie that luks tae tha Sinn an pits hïs trust ïn hïm wull hae ayelastin life, an A wull rise hïm up on tha Last Day.” Wi that, tha Jews stairtit grummlin aboot hïm, acause he saed, “A be tha breid that cum doon frae heiven.”  The' saed, “Is thon no Jesus, hïm that's tha sinn o Joseph? Shair we ken hïs faither an mither! Hoo cum he's noo sayin, ‘A cum doon frae heiven’?”  “Wud ye quït grummlin amang yersels,” Jesus toul thaim.  “Naebodie can cum tae me less tha Faither that sent me draas hïm, an A wull rise hïm up on tha Last Day.  It ïs writ ïn tha proaphits: ‘The'll aa be lairnt bi God.’ Iveriebodie that taks heed o tha Faither, an lairns frae hïm, wull cum tae me.  Naebodie haes iver saen tha Faither apairt frae tha yin that's alang wi God; ït's jist hïm haes saen tha Faither.  Am tellin ye tha truith, thaim at believes haes ayelastin life.  A be tha breid o life.  Yer forefaithers et tha manna ïn tha wuldèrness, yit fer aa that, the' deed.  But thïs here breid that cums doon frae heiven, a man can ait ït, an no dee.  A be tha leevin breid that cums doon frae heiven. If oniebodie aits thïs breid, he wull leeve fer aye. Thïs breid ïs ma flesh, that A wull gie fer tha life o tha warl.” Wi that tha Jews stairtit an argyin match amang thairsels, sayin, “Hoo cud yer man gie iz hïs flesh tae ait?”  But Jesus toul thaim, “A'm tellin ye tha truith, less ye ait tha flesh o tha Sinn o Man, an drïnk hïs bluid, ye'll hae nae life ïn ye.  Whaiver aits ma flesh an drïnks ma bluid haes ayelastin life, an A wull rise hïm up on tha Last Day.  Fer ma flesh ïs tha rael mait, an ma bluid ïs tha rael drïnk.  Whaiver aits ma flesh an drïnks ma bluid, bides ïn me, an me ïn hïm.  Jist as tha leevin Faither sent me an A leeve acause o tha Faither, sae tha yin that feeds on me wull leeve acause o me.  Thïs ïs tha breid that cum doon frae heiven. Yer forefaithers et manna an the' deed, but thïs breid's no laik that. Hïm that feeds on thïs here breid wull leeve fer aye.”  Jesus toul thaim aa thïs whaniver he wus lairnin fowks ïn tha Meetin Hoose ïn Capernaum. Monie o hïs follaers, whan the' heerd aa thïs, the' saed, “Thon's haird tae stomach. Wha cud tak ït ïn?”  Jesus knowed ïn hissel that hïs follaers wus grummlin aboot ït, an he axt thaim, “Is yer faith shuk bi thïs?  Whut ïf ye saa tha Sinn o Man gang up tae whar he wus afore?  It's tha Spïrit gies life; tha flesh coonts fer naethin ava. Tha wurds A hae spauk til yis ir spïrit, an the'r life as weel.  Yit thair's yins amang ye that dïnnae believe.” Fer Jesus knowed richt frae tha stairt whut yins o thaim wudnae believe an wha ït wus that wud bethray hïm.  He went on tae say, “That's why A toul ye that naebodie can cum tae me less ma Faither alloos ït.”  Noo ower tha heid o aa thïs, monie o hïs follaers turnt thair baks on hïm an haed naethin mair tae dae wi hïm.  “Yous wudnae be fer leain me tae, wud ye?” Jesus axt tha twal.  Simon Petèr cum bak wi, “Loard, wha else wud we gang til? It's yersel haes tha wurds o ayelastin life.  We houl an we ken fine weel that you ir tha Halie Yin o God!”  An Jesus reponed, “Dïd A no pïck tha twal o ye? But fer aa that, yin o yis ïs a deil!”  (He wus taakin aboot Judas, tha sinn o Simon Iscariot, that wus aboot tae bethray hïm, tha mair he wus yin o tha twal.) Eftèr aa thïs, Jesus trevelt roon aboot Galilee, an he kep hissel weel oot o Judea, fer tha Jews thonner wur lukkin tae dae awa wi hïm.  But whaniver tha Jews' Faist o Shiltèrs  cum near,  Jesus's brithers toul hïm, “Ye shud lea here an gang tae Judea, sae as yer follaers can aa see tha guid warks ye'r daein.  Naebodie that's lukkin tae get tae tha tap iver daes thïngs ïn hidlins. Seein as ye'r aye daein these thïngs, dae thaim oot ïn tha apen, afore tha fowk!”  Fer no e'en hïs ain brithers believed ïn hïm.  Jesus saed bak tae thaim, “Na, fer masel tha richt time ïs no here yit; but onie time fer yous wud dae.  Tha warl haes nae cal tae hait yous. It haits me but, fer A stan wutness that tha warl daes nocht but ïll.  Awa on up yersels tae tha Faist. A'm no fer gaun up jist noo, fer ït's no tha richt time yit fer masel.”  Whan he toul thaim that, he stapt ïn Galilee. Hooaniver, eftèr hïs brithers haed gan up tae tha Faist, he went up on hïs lane, on tha quait an no ïn tha apen.  Noo at tha Faist tha Jews wur lukkin oot fer hïm an axin, “Whar's thon man?”  Thair wus a wile lock o whusperin amang tha thrang aboot hïm. Some saed, “Thon's yin guid man.” “Na!” saed ithers. “He's pittin fowk tha wrang róad.”  But fer fear o tha Jews naebodie wud say ocht aboot hïm oot ïn tha apen. Whan tha Faist wus half ower, Jesus gaed up tae tha coortyaird o tha Hoose o God, an he stairtit lairnin tha fowks.  Tha Jews wur stoondit an axt, “Whar dïd yer man git sitch lairnin, an hïm wi nae schuilin ava?”  Jesus toul thaim, “Ma taichin ïs no ma ain. It cums frae hïm that sent me.  If oniebodie haes a mine tae dae tha wull o God, he'll fin oot ïf ma taichin cums frae God, or whuther ït's jist ma ain.  Hïm that gies oot hïs ain thochts daes ït fer hïs ain glorie. But hïm that daes ït fer tha glorie o tha yin that sent hïm, he's a man o truith; thair's nae lees aboot hïm ava.  Dïd Moses no gie ye tha laa? Yit thair's no yin o yis keeps tha laa. Whut ir ye wantin tae kïll me fer?”  “Ye hae a divil ïn ye,” tha thrang answert. “Wha's oot tae kïll ye?”  Jesus toul thaim, “A daen tha yin mïracle an yis ir aa dumfoonèrt  .  Yit, Moses gien ye tha laa o circumcision - tha mair, ïn fect, ït dïdnae cum frae Moses ava, but frae tha patriarchs afore hïm - an acause o that, yous'll circumcise weans on tha Sabbath day.  Noo ïf ye'll circumcise a wean on tha Sabbath day sae as tha laa o Moses wull no git brauk, hoo cum yis'r ang'rie wi me fer makkin a hale man weel on tha Sabbath day?  Quït yer judgin bi tha luk o thïngs, but judge tha richt wye.” Richt then some o tha fowk frae Jerusalem begun axin yin anither, “Is thïs no tha man the'r lukkin tae kïll?  Luk, here he ïs, taakin oot ïn tha apen, an the'r no sayin yin wurd tae hïm! It cudnae be that oor heidyins haes cum roon tae thïnkin he's tha Christ, cud ït?  But shair we ken whar thïs man cums frae; yit whan tha Christ cums, naebodie wull ken whar he cums frae.”  An sae whaniver Jesus wus taichin ïn tha Temple coorts, he caad oot, “Ay, ye thïnk ye ken me, an ye thïnk ye ken whar A cum frae! But A'm no here on ma ain accoont. Hïm that sent me ïs true. Hïm yis dïnnae ken.  But A ken hïm, fer A cum frae hïm, an ït's hïm that sent me.”  Eftèr that, the' haed a mine tae grup Jesus, but niver tha yin layed a han on hïm, fer hïs oor haednae cum yit.  Wi aa that, monie o tha fowk püt thair faith ïn hïm. An the' saed, “Whaniver Messiah cums, dae ye thïnk he wud dae onie mair mïraclis signs ner thïs man?” Tha Pharisees heerd tha whuspers gaun roon tha crood aboot hïm. An sae tha heid preeshts an tha Pharisees sent sodgers o tha Temple Gaird tae tak hïm ïn.  Jesus toul thaim, “A'm wi ye fer a wee while langer jist, an then A'm gaun tae tha yin that sent me.  Ye'll luk fer me, but ye'll no fin me; an whar A be, ye cannae cum.”  Tha Jews saed tae yin anither, “Whar's thïs man fer gaun that we'll niver fin hïm? Wull he gang whar oor fowks ïs leevin skailt amang tha Greeks, an taich tha Greeks?  Whut wus he taakin aboot whan he saed, ‘Ye'll luk fer me, but ye'll no fin me; an whar A be, ye cannae cum.’?” On tha last day - tha bïg day - o tha Faist, Jesus stud up an caad oot lood, “If oniebodie haes a druith on thaim, cum tae me an tak a drïnk.  Oniebodie that lippens on me - jist as Scrïpture haes saed - ‘Leevin wattèrs wull rin oot frae hïs hairt.’ ”  He wus taakin here aboot tha Spïrit, that hïs follaers wud be gien latèr on. Up tae noo tha Spïrit wusnae gien, fer Jesus haednae cum ïntae hïs glorie yit. Whaniver the' heerd hïs wurds, some o tha fowk saed, “Thïs man fer shair maun be tha Proaphit!”  Ithers saed, “Thïs man ïs tha Christ.” But ither yins axt, “Hoo cud tha Christ cum frae Galilee?  Dae tha Scrïptures no say that Christ wull cum frae tha femlie o Davit, an fae tha toon o Bethlehem, whar Davit leeved?”  An sae tha fowk wus divïd aboot hïm.  Some wur lukkin tae lay houl o hïm. But naebodie layed a fïng'r on hïm. Sae eftèr aa that, tha sodgers o tha Temple Gaird went bak tae tha heid preeshts an Pharisees, an the' wur axt, “Hoo cum yis niver brocht hïm ïn?”  “Naebodie iver taakt tha wye thon man daes,” tha sodgers toul thaim.  “Ye'r no tellin iz he haes tuk yous ïn anaa?” tha Pharisees speered.  “Daes onie o iz heidyins or Pharisees houl wi hïm?  Na, nane but thon gether-up that kens naethin o tha Laa - an the' ir damned oniehoo!”  Noo Nicodemus, yin o tha Pharisees - hïm that cum tae Jesus afore - axt thaim,  “Daes oor Laa fin a bodie guiltie wioot giein hïm a hearin furst, fer tae fin oot whut he's daen?”  The' cum bak an saed, “Ir you frae Galilee anaa? Luk ïntae ït an ye'll fin that nae proaphit cums oot o Galilee.” Sae the' aa went bak hame tae thair ain hoose. Hooaniver, Jesus gaed up tae tha Moont o Olives.  At furst licht, he turnt up yinst mair ïn tha Temple coorts, whar aa tha fowk gethert roon hïm, an he sut doon an begun lairnin thaim.  Tha maistèrs o tha laa an tha Pharisees brocht ïn a wumman catched ïn adultèrie. The' gart hir tae stan ïn tha mïddle o tha getherin,  an the' saed tae Jesus, “Taicher, the' catched thïs wumman here ïn tha verie ect o adultèrie!  Noo ïn oor laa, Moses bïd iz tae stane sitch weemen tae deith. Whut dae you say but?”  The' wur quïzzin hïm fer tae ketch hïm oot, tae get tha gruns fer a chairge agin hïm. But Jesus stoopit doon an he stairtit tae scrieve ïn tha stour wi hïs fïng'r.  Whan the' kep on at hïm, he stud up strecht an toul thaim, “Whaiver yin o yis haes niver sïnned, weel, let hïm clod tha furst stane at hir!”  Yinst mair he stoopt doon an scrievit ïn tha stour o tha grun.  Whaniver the' heerd thïs, [convictit ïn thair hairts], the' stairtit tae slip awa yin bi yin, tha oul yins furst, an tha ithers eftèr thaim. Jesus wus left on hïs lane, wi tha wumman stannin afore hïm.  He stud up [an seein naebodie bar tha wumman] he saed tae hir, “Sae whar ir the' aa? Haes nane o thaim condemned ye?”  “Naebodie, Loard,” qo she. “Weel, nether dae A condemn ye,” saed Jesus. “Awa ye gang an sïn nae mair!” Whaniver Jesus taakt agane wi tha fowk, he toul thaim, “A be tha licht o tha warl. Whaiver follaes me wull no waak ïn tha dairk onie mair, but the' wull hae tha licht o life.”  Tha Pharisees saed til hïm, “Thair ye ir agane, pittin yersel forrit as yer ain wutness; that kine o testimonie daesnae coont fer ocht.”  But Jesus cum bak wi thïs: “Tha mair A gie ma ain testimonie, ma testimonie stans, fer A ken whar A cum frae an whar A'm gaun. But yous hae nae notion o whar A hae cum frae, or whar A'm gaun.  You mak yer ain judgemens accoardin tae tha wye man daes; but A mak nae judgemens on naebodie.  But ïf A dïd judge, ye wud fin ma judgemens wud be richt. It's no me ectin on ma lane, fer tha Faither that sent me stans alang wi me.  Shair ït says ïn yer ain laa that twa men's wurd ïs tuk as tha truith.  A be tha yin that wutnesses fer masel; ma ither wutness ïs tha Faither that sent me.”  An sae the' axt hïm, “Whar's yer Faither at?” “Ye nether know me ner ma Faither,” qo Jesus. “If ye knowed me, ye wud know ma Faither forbye.”  He telt thaim aa thïs whaniver he wus lairnin fowks ïn tha Temple yaird, nearhan tha kïst fer tha offerins. Aa tha same, naebodie layed a fïng'r on hïm, fer hïs time wusnae cum yit. An Jesus went on tae tell thaim, “Luk see, A'm gaun aff. Ye'll luk fer me, an ye'll dee ïn yer sïn. Whar A'm gaun, yis cannae cum.”  Tha Jews saed amang thairsels, “Is he gaun tae dae hissel ïn? Cud that be fer why he's sayin, ‘Whar A'm gaun, yis cannae cum’?”  But he toul thaim mair, “Yous ir frae doon unnèr; A be frae abain. Yous ir o thïs warl; A dïnnae belang tae thïs warl.  A toul ye that yis wud dee ïn yer sïns; fer less ye lippen that A be tha yin that A say that A am, yis'll dee ïn yer sïns fer shair.”  “Wha ir ye then?” the' axt. “Jist whut A hae bin tellin yis al alang,” Jesus reponed.  “A hae monies a thïng A cud say aboot yis, an tae condemn yis wi. A'll no say ït but. Hïm that sent me ïs siccar, an ït's whut A hae heerd frae hïm that A tell tha warl.”  Still an aa, the' dïdnae unnèrstan that he wus taakin aboot hïs Faither.  Sae Jesus saed, “Whan ye hae lïftit up tha Sinn o Man, then ye wull ken that A am tha yin A saed A wus, an that A dae naethin ava on ma ain, but gie wurd o whut tha Faither haes tocht me.  An tha yin that sent me ïs wi me; he haesnae left me on ma lane, fer A aye dae whut plaises hïm.”  An aa tha while Jesus wus taakin, monie fowk lippened on hïm. Tae tha Jews at haed lippened on hïm, Jesus saed, “If yis houl tae whut A hae tocht ye, ye'r ma follaers aa richt.  Yis wull ken tha truith, an tha truith wull mak ye free.”  An the' cum bak wi thïs, “Luk, we ir tha childèr o Abraham, an we wur niver slaves tae naebodie. Sae hoo can ye say that we wull be let lowse?” Jesus gie thaim thïs answer: “Noo here's tha truith o ït. Iveriebodie that daes wrang ïs a slave tae wrang. Sïn ïs hïs maistèr.  Noo a slave haes nae richt tae be a pairt o tha femlie fer iver, but a sinn belangs tae tha femlie fer iver an aye.  Sae ïf tha Sinn maks ye free, then ye'll be free fer shair!  A ken yis ir tha childèr o Abraham. But yis ir lukkin tae kïll me, fer yis hae nae ruim ïn yer hairts fer whut A hae tae say.  A'm tellin ye whut A saa whan A wus alang wi ma Faither; but yous follae tha bïddin o your faither.” “Abraham ïs oor faither,” the' answert. “Gin you wur tha childèr o Abraham,” qo Jesus, “then ye wud dae whut Abraham daen.  An yit naethin'll dae yis but seein me kïllt, me that haes toul ye tha truith A heerd frae God. Abraham niver wud a daen that.  Yous jist dae whut yer ain faither daes!” “Nane o iz wus boarn ootbye a laafu femlie,” the' answert bak. “We hae tha yin faither, an that's God hissel!” Jesus telt thaim, “If God wus yer Faither, ye wud love me, fer A cum frae God, an noo here A be. A'm no cum on ma ain accoont; ït wus hïm that sent me.  Hoo cum yis cannae tak ïn whut A'm tellin ye? A'll tell ye fer why, ït's acause ye'r no wullin tae lïsten!  Ye belang tae your faither, tha deil, an ye'r wantin tae dae whut's ïn yer faither's hairt. He wus a murdèrer richt frae tha stairt, nae freen o tha truith, fer thair's nae truith ïn hïm. Whan he tells lees, he taaks hïs ain leid, fer he's a doonricht liar, ay, tha faither o lees.  Yit, whaniver ït's me tellin ye tha truith, ye dïnnae believe me!  Is thair yin amang ye can gie onie pruif A'm guiltie o sïn? An ïf A'm tellin ye tha truith, hoo cum ye dïnnae lippen whut A say?  Hïm that belangs tae God, taks tent tae whut God says. Tha raison yous dïnnae lïsten ïs that yis dïnnae belang tae God.” Tha Jews axt hïm, “Ir we no richt ïn sayin ye'r a Samaritan wi a divil ïn ye?”  “Thair's nae divil ïn me,” qo Jesus, “but A hae regaird fer ma Faither an yous hae nae regaird fer me.  A'm no eftèr glorie fer masel; but thair ïs yin that ïs lukkin ït for me, an he ïs tha yin tae judge.  Here's tha truith o ït, ïf oniebodie houls tae ma wurd, he wull niver dee.”  Wi that tha Jews caad oot, “Noo we ken fer shair that thair's a divil ïn ye! Abraham deed an tha proaphits deed as weel. Yit you'r tellin iz that ïf oniebodie houls tae yer wurd, he'll niver dee!  Wud you be a bïgger man ner oor faither Abraham? He deed an sae dïd tha proaphits. Wha dae you thïnk you ir?”  Jesus reponed, “If A gie masel tha glorie, thon glorie mains naethin. Ma Faither, that yous mak oot ïs your God, he's tha yin at gies me tha glorie.  Tha mair yous dïnnae ken hïm, A ken hïm weel. If A saed A dïdnae, that wud mak me a liar laik yous! But A dae ken hïm an A houl tae hïs wurd.  Yer faither Abraham wus fu o joy at tha thocht o seein ma day cum; he saa ït an wus hairt gled.”  “Ketch yersel on. Ye'r no fïftie yit,” tha Jews saed tae hïm, “an ye'r tellin iz ye hae saa Abraham?!”  “A'm tellin ye tha truith,” answert Jesus, “afore iver Abraham wus boarn, A be!”  Whaniver the' heerd that, the' tuk up stanes fer tae pelt hïm, but Jesus jookt oot o sicht, an left tha Temple gruns. Yin day Jesus wus waakin alang an he cum on thïs man blin frae tha day he wus boarn.  Hïs follaers axt hïm, “Rabbi, wha wus ït daen wrang that thïs here man wus boarn blin? Wus ït hissel, or wus ït hïs mither an faither?”  “Nether thïs man, ner hïs mither ner hïs faither haes sïnned,” he answert, “but ït cum aboot sae that tha warks o God micht be showed ïn hïs life.  Whan ït's daylicht, we maun dae tha wark o hïm that sent me. Nicht ïs cumin whan naebodie can wark.  Aa tha while A'm ïn tha warl, A be tha licht o tha warl.”  Wi that, he sput on tha grun an made some glar wi hïs spïttle, an püt ït on tha man's een.  “Awa,” he telt hïm, “an waash ïn tha Puil o Siloam” (Siloam haes tha mainin o ‘Sent’). Sae tha man went aff, an waasht, an cum bak able tae see!  Hïs nighbers an thaim that knowed hïm as a blin beggar-man axt, “Wud thïs no be tha same man that uist tae sït an beg?”  Some ledged that he wus. Ithers saed, “Na, he jist favours hïm.” But tha man kep on tellin thaim aa, “It's me richt eneuch.”  “Sae whut wye dïd ye git yer een apent?” the' axt hïm.  He reponed, “Tha man the' caa Jesus made some glar an püt ït on ma een. He toul me tae gang til tha Puil o Siloam an waash. Sae aff A went an waasht, an eftèr that A cud see!”  “Whar's thon man at noo?” the' axt hïm. “A dïnnae ken,” qo he. The' brocht tha man that uist tae be blin up afore tha Pharisees.  Noo ït wus a Sabbath day that Jesus made tha mud an apent tha man's een.  Sae tha Pharisees, they quïzzed hïm as weel aboot hoo he haed got hïs sicht. “He püt glar on ma een,” tha man answert, “an A waasht, an noo A can see.”  A nummer o tha Pharisees saed, “Thïs man ïsnae frae God, fer he daesnae keep tha Sabbath.” But ithers axt, “Hoo cud a sïnner dae aa thaim mïracles?” An the' wur divïd ower tha heid o ït.  Sae the' turnt agane an axt tha blin man, “An whut dae you say aboot hïm? Fer ït wus your een he apent.” Tha man reponed, “He ïs a proaphit.” Tha Jews still dïdnae believe that he wus iver blin, no tae the' sent fer tha man's mither an faither.  “Is thïs yer sinn?” the' axt thaim. “Wud ït be hïm ye'r tellin iz wus boarn blin? Hoo cum he can see noo?”  “We know fine weel thïs ïs oor sinn,” tha mither an faither reponed, “an we ken he wus boarn blin.  But hoo ït's cum aboot that he can see noo, or wha apent hïs een, we cannae tell ye. Ax hïm yersels. He's oul eneuch tae taak fer hissel.”  Hïs mither an faither wus taakin that wye fer fear o tha Jews, fer tha Jews haed thair mines made up tae pit iveriebodie oot o tha Meetin Hoose that allooed Jesus wus tha Christ.
